------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Xhosa Bible: Genesis

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> Ekuqalekeni uThixo wadala amazulu
nehlabathi.

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> Ke ehlabathini kwakusenyanyeni, kuselubala;
kwakumnyama phezu kwamanzi enzonzobila. UMoya kaThixo wafukama phezu
kwamanzi lawo.

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> Wathi uThixo, Makubekho ukukhanya. Kwabakho
ke ukukhanya.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> Wakubona ke uThixo ukukhanya ukuba
kulungile, wahlula uThixo phakathi kokukhanya nobumnyama.

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Wathi uThixo ukukhanya yimini, wathi
ubumnyama bubusuku. Kwahlwa, kwasa: yangumhla wokuqala.

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> Wathi uThixo, Makubekho isibhakabhaka
phakathi kwawo amanzi, sibe ngumahlulo wokwahlula amanzi kumanzi.

<span id="an_1:7">1:7</span> Wasenza uThixo isibhakabhaka, wawahlula
amanzi angaphantsi kwesibhakabhaka kuwo amanzi angaphezu
kwesibhakabhaka. Kwaba njalo.

<span id="an_1:8">1:8</span> Wathi uThixo isibhakabhaka ngamazulu.
Kwahlwa, kwasa: yangumhla wesibini.

<span id="an_1:9">1:9</span> Wathi uThixo, Amanzi angaphantsi kwamazulu
makahlanganiselwe ndaweni-nye, kubonakale okomileyo. Kwaba njalo.

<span id="an_1:10">1:10</span> Wathi uThixo okomileyo ngumhlaba, wathi
intlanganisela yamanzi ziilwandle. Wabona uThixo ukuba kulungile.

<span id="an_1:11">1:11</span> Wathi uThixo, Umhlaba mawuphume uhlaza,
imifuno evelisa imbewu, imithi yeziqhamo, eyenza iziqhamo ngohlobo
lwayo, embewu ikuyo, emhlabeni. Kwaba njalo.

<span id="an_1:12">1:12</span> Umhlaba waphuma uhlaza, nemifuno evelisa
imbewu ngohlobo lwayo, nemithi eyenza iziqhamo, embewu ikuyo, ngohlobo
lwayo. Wabona uThixo ukuba kulungile.

<span id="an_1:13">1:13</span> Kwahlwa kwasa: yangumhla wesithathu.

<span id="an_1:14">1:14</span> Wathi uThixo, Makubekho izikhanyiso
esibhakabhakeni samazulu, zibe ngumahlulo wokwahlula imini kubusuku;
zibe zezemiqondiso, zibe zezamaxesha amisiweyo, zibe zezemihla
neminyaka;

<span id="an_1:15">1:15</span> mazibe zizikhanyiso esibhakabhakeni
samazulu, zikhanyise ehlabathini. Kwaba njalo.

<span id="an_1:16">1:16</span> Wenza uThixo izikhanyiso ezikhulu
zazibini, esona sikhulu isikhanyiso ukuba silawule imini, esona
sincinane isikhanyiso ukuba silawule ubusuku; wenza neenkwenkwezi.

<span id="an_1:17">1:17</span> Wazibeka uThixo esibhakabhakeni samazulu,
ukuba zikhanyise ehlabathini, zilawule imini nobusuku,

<span id="an_1:18">1:18</span> zahlule ukukhanya kubumnyama. Wabona
uThixo ukuba kulungile.

<span id="an_1:19">1:19</span> Kwahlwa, kwasa: yangumhla wesine.

<span id="an_1:20">1:20</span> Wathi uThixo, Amanzi la makanyakazele
inyakanyaka, imiphefumlo ephilileyo; zithi neentaka ziphaphazele
ehlabathini, esibhakabhakeni sezulu.

<span id="an_1:21">1:21</span> Wadala uThixo oominenga mikhulu, nayo
yonke imiphefumlo ephilileyo enambuzelayo, awanyakazela ngayo amanzi
ngohlobo lwayo, neentaka zonke ezinamaphiko ngohlobo lwazo. Wabona
uThixo ukuba kulungile.

<span id="an_1:22">1:22</span> Wazisikelela uThixo, esithi, Qhamani,
nande, niwazalise amanzi aselwandle; zithi iintaka zande ehlabathini.

<span id="an_1:23">1:23</span> Kwahlwa, kwasa: yangumhla wesihlanu.

<span id="an_1:24">1:24</span> Wathi uThixo, Umhlaba mawuphume
imiphefumlo ephilileyo ngohlobo lwayo: izinto ezizitho zine,
nezinambuzane, nezinto eziphilileyo zomhlaba ngohlobo lwazo. Kwaba
njalo.

<span id="an_1:25">1:25</span> Wenza uThixo izinto eziphilileyo zomhlaba
ngohlobo lwazo, nezinto ezizitho zine ngohlobo lwazo, nazo zonke
izinambuzane zomhlaba ngohlobo lwazo. Wabona uThixo ukuba kulungile.

<span id="an_1:26">1:26</span> Wathi uThixo, Masenze umntu
ngokomfanekiselo wethu ngokufana nathi. Mababe nobukhosi ezintlanzini
zolwandle, nasezintakeni zezulu, nasezintweni ezizitho zine,
nasemhlabeni wonke, nasezinambuzaneni zonke ezinambuzela emhlabeni.

<span id="an_1:27">1:27</span> Wamdala ke uThixo umntu ngokomfanekiselo
wakhe; wamdala ngokomfanekiselo kaThixo; wadala indoda nenkazana.

<span id="an_1:28">1:28</span> Wabasikelela uThixo, wathi kubo uThixo,
Qhamani, nande, niwuzalise umhlaba niweyise; nibe nobukhosi ezintlanzini
zolwandle, nasezintakeni zezulu, nasezintweni zonke eziphilileyo
ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni.

<span id="an_1:29">1:29</span> Wathi uThixo, Yabonani, ndininikile yonke
imifuno evelisa imbewu, esemhlabeni wonke, nayo yonke imithi eneziqhamo
zemithi evelisa imbewu: yoba kukudla kuni.

<span id="an_1:30">1:30</span> Nezinto zonke eziphilileyo zomhlaba,
neentaka zonke zezulu, nezinambuzane zonke ezisemhlabeni, ezinomphefumlo
ophilileyo, ndizinike yonke imifuno eluhlaza ukuba ibe kukudla. Kwaba
njalo.

<span id="an_1:31">1:31</span> Wakubona uThixo konke akwenzileyo, nanko,
kulungile kunene. Kwahlwa, kwasa: yangumhla wesithandathu.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> Agqitywa ke amazulu nehlabathi, nawo wonke
umkhosi wezo zinto.

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> Wawugqiba ke uThixo ngomhla wesixhenxe
umsebenzi wakhe awawenzayo; waphumla ngomhla wesixhenxe kuwo wonke
umsebenzi wakhe awawenzayo.

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Wawusikelela uThixo umhla wesixhenxe,
wawungcwalisa; ngokuba waphumla ngawo kuwo wonke umsebenzi wakhe
awawudalayo uThixo, wawenza.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> Yiyo le ke inzala yamazulu nehlabathi
ekudalweni kwezo zinto, mini wenza uYehova uThixo ihlabathi namazulu,

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> onke amatyholo asendle engekaveli
emhlabeni, nayo yonke imifuno yasendle ingekantshuli; kuba uYehova
uThixo ebengekanisi mvula emhlabeni; kwaye kungekho mntu wokuwusebenza
umhlaba.

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> Kwaye kunyuka inkungu iphuma ehlabathini,
yawunyakamisa wonke umhlaba.

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> UYehova uThixo wambumba umntu ngothuli
lwasemhlabeni, waphefumlela emathatheni akhe impefumlo yobomi; umntu ke
waba ngumphefumlo ophilileyo.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> UYehova uThixo watyala umyezo e-Eden
ngasempumalanga; wambeka khona umntu abembumbile.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> UYehova uThixo wantshulisa emhlabeni yonke
imithi enqwenelekayo ngokukhangeleka, nelungele ukudliwa; nomthi wobomi
emyezweni phakathi, nomthi wokwazi okulungileyo nokubi.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> Kwaphuma umlambo e-Eden wokuwunyakamisa
umyezo; wahluka apho, waba ziimbaxa ezine.

<span id="an_2:11">2:11</span> Igama lowokuqala yiPishon; nguwo lowo
ujikeleze lonke ilizwe laseHavila, apho ikhona igolide.

<span id="an_2:12">2:12</span> Igolide yelo lizwe intle, ikhona
ibhedolaki nelitye lebherilo.

<span id="an_2:13">2:13</span> Igama lowesibini umlambo yiGihon; nguwo
lowo ujikeleze lonke ilizwe lakwaKushi.

<span id="an_2:14">2:14</span> Igama lowesithathu umlambo yiHidekele;
nguwo lowo uya phambi kwelakwa-Asiriya. Owesine umlambo ngumEfrati.

<span id="an_2:15">2:15</span> UYehova uThixo wamthabatha umntu, wambeka
emyezweni we-Eden, ukuba awusebenze, awugcine.

<span id="an_2:16">2:16</span> UYehova uThixo wamwisela umthetho umntu,
esithi, Yonke imithi yomyezo ungayidla uyidle;

<span id="an_2:17">2:17</span> ke wona umthi wokwazi okulungileyo nokubi
uze ungawudli; kuba mhlana uthe wawudla, uya kufa.

<span id="an_2:18">2:18</span> Wathi uYehova uThixo, Akulungile ukuba
umntu abe yedwa, ndiya kumenzela umncedi onguwabo.

<span id="an_2:19">2:19</span> UYehova uThixo wabumba ngomhlaba zonke
izinto eziphilileyo zasendle, nazo zonke iintaka zezulu, wazisa kuye
uAdam ukubona ukuba wothini na ukuzibiza, ukuze oko azibize ngako uAdam
zonke izinto eziphilileyo, ibe ligama lazo elo.

<span id="an_2:20">2:20</span> Wazithiya amagama uAdam zonke izinto
ezizitho zine, neentaka zasezulwini, nazo zonke izinto eziphilileyo
zasendle; ke uAdam akafunyanelwanga mncedi unguwabo.

<span id="an_2:21">2:21</span> UYehova uThixo wawisa ubuthongo obukhulu
phezu koAdam, walala. Wathabatha lwalunye ezimbanjeni zakhe, wavingca
ngenyama esikhundleni salo.

<span id="an_2:22">2:22</span> UYehova uThixo walwakha ubambo
abeluthabathe kuAdam, lwaba ngumfazi; wamzisa kuAdam.

<span id="an_2:23">2:23</span> Wathi uAdam, Eli ke ngoku lithambo
lasemathanjeni am, yinyama yasenyameni yam; lo yena ukubizwa kothiwa
ngumfazi, ngokuba ethatyathwe endodeni.

<span id="an_2:24">2:24</span> Ngenxa yoko indoda yomshiya uyise nonina,
inamathele kumkayo, babe nyama-nye ke.

<span id="an_2:25">2:25</span> Baye bobabini behamba ze, umntu lowo
nomkakhe, bengenazintloni.

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> Ke kaloku inyoka yaye inobuqhophololo
ngaphezu kwazo zonke izinto eziphilileyo zasendle, abezenzile uYehova
uThixo. Yathi kumfazi Utshilo na okunene uThixo ukuthi, Ze ningadli kuyo
yonke imithi yomyezo?

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> Wathi umfazi kwinyoka, Eziqhameni zemithi
yomyezo singadla;

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> ke eziqhameni zomthi osemyezweni phakathi,
uthe uThixo, Ze ningadli kuzo; ze ningazichukumisi, hleze nife.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> Yathi inyoka kumfazi, Anisayi kufa:

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> kuba esazi uThixo ukuba, mhlana nithe nadla
kuzo, oqabuka amehlo enu, nibe njengoThixo, nazi okulungileyo nokubi.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> Wabona umfazi ukuba umthi ulungele
ukudliwa, nokuba uyakhanukeka emehlweni, ingumthi onqwenelekela
ukuqiqisa, wathabatha eziqhameni zawo, wadla; wanika nendoda yakhe
inaye, yadla.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> Aqabuka amehlo abo bobabini, bazi ukuba
bahamba ze; bathunga amagqabi omkhiwane, bazenzela imibhinqo.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> Basiva isandi sikaYehova uThixo, ehamba
emyezweni empepheni yasemini; basuka bazimela uAdam nomkakhe ebusweni
bukaYehova uThixo, phakathi kwemithi yomyezo.

<span id="an_3:9">3:9</span> UYehova uThixo wambiza uAdam, wathi kuye,
Uphi na?

<span id="an_3:10">3:10</span> Wathi yena, Ndive isandi sakho emyezweni,
ndasuka ndoyika, ngokuba ndihamba ze; ndazimela.

<span id="an_3:11">3:11</span> Wathi, Uxelelwe ngubani na, ukuba uhamba
ze? Udlile na kuwo umthi, endakuwisela umthetho ngawo, ndathi, Uze
ungadli kuwo?

<span id="an_3:12">3:12</span> Wathi uAdam, Umfazi owandinikayo ukuba
abe nam, nguye ondinikileyo kuwo umthi, ndadla ke.

<span id="an_3:13">3:13</span> Wathi uYehova uThixo kumfazi, Yintoni na
le nto uyenzileyo? Wathi umfazi, Inyoka indilukuhlile, ndadla ke.

<span id="an_3:14">3:14</span> Wathi uYehova uThixo kwinyoka, Ngokuba
uyenzile le nto, uqalekisiwe wena ngaphezu kwezinto zonke ezizitho zine,
neento zonke eziphilileyo zasendle; uya kuhamba ngesisu, udle uthuli,
yonke imihla yobomi bakho.

<span id="an_3:15">3:15</span> Ndiya kumisa ubutshaba phakathi kwakho
nomfazi, naphakathi kwembewu yakho nembewu yakhe; yona iya kukutyumza
intloko, wena uya kuyityumza isithende.

<span id="an_3:16">3:16</span> Wathi kumfazi, Ndiya kukwandisa kakhulu
ukubulaleka kwakho ekumitheni, uzale abantwana unembulaleko; inkanuko
yakho ibe sendodeni yakho, ikulawule yona.

<span id="an_3:17">3:17</span> KuAdam wathi, Ngokuba uphulaphule izwi
lomkakho, wadla kuwo umthi endakuwisela umthetho ngawo, ndathi, Uze
ungadli kuwo, uqalekisiwe umhlaba ngenxa yakho; uya kudla kuwo
ubulaleka, yonke imihla yobomi bakho.

<span id="an_3:18">3:18</span> Uya kukuntshulela imithana enameva
neenkunzane, udle umfuno wasendle.

<span id="an_3:19">3:19</span> Uya kudla ukudla kokubila kobuso bakho,
ude ubuyele emhlabeni kobuso bakho, ude ubuyele emhlabeni, kuba
uthatyathwe kuwo; ngokuba uluthuli, uya kubuyela kwaseluthulini.

<span id="an_3:20">3:20</span> UAdam walibiza igama lomkakhe ngokuthi
nguEva, ngokuba yena engunina wabaphilileyo bonke.

<span id="an_3:21">3:21</span> UYehova uThixo wabenzela iingubo zezintsu
uAdam nomkakhe, wabambathisa.

<span id="an_3:22">3:22</span> Wathi uYehova uThixo, Yabonani, umntu
usuke waba njengomnye wethu, ukwazi okulungileyo nokubi; hleze ke olule
isandla sakhe, athabathe nakuwo umthi wobomi, adle, aphile ngonaphakade:

<span id="an_3:23">3:23</span> uYehova uThixo wamndulula emyezweni
we-Eden, ukuba asebenze umhlaba abethatyathwe kuwo.

<span id="an_3:24">3:24</span> Wamgxotha ke umntu; wamisa
ngasempumalanga kuwo umyezo we-Eden iikerubhi, nelangatye lekrele
elijikajikayo lokugcina indlela eya emthini wobomi.

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> Ke kaloku uAdam wamazi uEva umkakhe;
wamitha wazala uKayin, wathi, Ndizuze indoda ngoYehova.

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> Waphinda wazala umninawa wakhe, uAbheli;
uAbheli waba ngumalusi wezimvu, uKayin waba ngumsebenzi womhlaba.

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> Kwathi ekupheleni kwamihla ithile, uKayin
wathabatha eziqhameni zomhlaba, wazisa umnikelo kuYehova.

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> UAbheli wazisa naye, ethabathe kumazibulo
ezimvu zakhe, kwezinamanqatha. Waza uYehova wambheka uAbheli nomnikelo
wakhe.

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Akambheka uKayin nomnikelo wakhe. Waqumba
kunene uKayin, basangana ubuso bakhe.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> Wathi uYehova kuKayin, Yini na ukuba
uqumbe, yini na ukuba busangane ubuso bakhe?

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> Ukuba uthe walungisa, abuyi kuswabuluka
ubuso yini na? Ukuba uthe akwalungisa, isono sibuthumile ngasesangweni,
singxamele wena; ke wena, silawule.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> Wathetha uKayin noAbheli umninawa wakhe,
kwathi besendle, wesuka uKayin wamvunukela uAbheli umninawa wakhe,
wambulala.

<span id="an_4:9">4:9</span> Wathi uYehova kuKayin, Uphi na uAbheli,
umninawa wakho? Wathi yena, Andazi; ndingumgcini womninawa wam, yini na?

<span id="an_4:10">4:10</span> Wathi, Wenze ntoni na? Izwi legazi
lomninawa wakho liyakhala emhlabeni kum.

<span id="an_4:11">4:11</span> Ngoko uqalekisiwe emhlabeni, owakhamise
umlomo wawo ukuba ulithabathe igazi lomninawa wakho esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_4:12">4:12</span> Xenikweni uwusebenzayo umhlaba, awusayi
kuphinda ukunike amandla awo; uya kubhadula uphalaphale ehlabathini.

<span id="an_4:13">4:13</span> Wathi uKayin kuYehova, ityala lam likhulu
ngokungenakuthwalwa.

<span id="an_4:14">4:14</span> Yabona, undigxdothile namhla phezu
komhlaba; ndiya kusithela nasebusweni bakho, ndibhadule ndiphalaphale
ehlabathini bathi bonke abantu abandifumanayo bandibulale.

<span id="an_4:15">4:15</span> Wathi uYehova kuye, xa kunjalo, bonke
ababulala uKayin kophindezelwa kubo kasixhenxe. UYehova wammisela uKayin
umqondiso, ukuze bonke abamfumanayo bangamsiki.

<span id="an_4:16">4:16</span> Waphuma uKayin, wemka ebusweni
bukaYehova; wahlala ezweni lakwaKuphalaphala phambi kwe-Eden.

<span id="an_4:17">4:17</span> UKayin wamazi umkakhe, wamitha, wazala
uEnoki. Wakha umzi, wawuthiya loo mzi ngegama lonyana wakhe uEnoki.

<span id="an_4:18">4:18</span> UEnoki wazalelwa uIradi; uIradi wazala
uMehuyaheli; uMehuyaheli wazala uMetusaheli; uMetusaheli wazala uLameki.

<span id="an_4:19">4:19</span> ULameki wazeka abafazi ababini; igama
lomnye belinguAda, igama lowesibini belinguZila.

<span id="an_4:20">4:20</span> UAda wazala uYabhali yena waba nguyise
wabahlala ezintenteni, nabafuyileyo.

<span id="an_4:21">4:21</span> Igama lomninawa wakhe belinguYubhali;
yena waba nguyise wabo bonke abaphatha uhadi nogwali.

<span id="an_4:22">4:22</span> UZila uthe naye wazala uTubhalekayin,
obekhanda yonke impahla enobukhali yobhedu nesinyithi; udade
woTubhalekayin ebenguNahama.

<span id="an_4:23">4:23</span> Wathi uLameki kubafazi bakhe, ada noZila,
liveni ilizwi lam. Bafazi bakaLameki, phulaphulani intetho yam.
Sendibulele indoda ngenxa yenxeba lam, nendodana ngenxa yomvumbo wam.

<span id="an_4:24">4:24</span> Xa uKayin aya kuphindezelwa kasixhenxe,
Yena uLameki uya kuphindezelwa kamashumi osixhenxe anesixhenxe.

<span id="an_4:25">4:25</span> UAdam wabuya wamazi umkakhe, wazala
unyana, wathi igama lakhe nguSete, kuba wathi, UThixo undimisele enye
imbewu esikhundleni sika-Abheli owabulawa nguKayin.

<span id="an_4:26">4:26</span> USete naye wazalelwa unyana, wathi igama
lakhe nguEnoshe. Kwaqalwa oko ukunqulwa igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> Yiyo le incwadi yenzala ka-Adam. Mhlana
uThixo wamdala umntu, wamenza ngokufana noThixo.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Wadala indoda nenkazana, wabasikelela,
wabathiya igama elinguAdam, mhlana wabadala.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> UAdam wahlala iminyaka elikhulu elinamanci
mathathu, wazala unyana ngokufana naye, ngokomfanekiso wakhe, wamthiya
igama elinguSete.

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> Imihla ka-Adam emveni kokuzala kwakhe uSete
yaba yiminyaka emakhulu asibhozo; wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> Iyonke imihla ka-Adam, awahlala ngayo, yaba
yiminyaka emakhulu asithoba anamanci mathathu; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> USete wahlala iminyaka elikhulu
elinaminyaka mihlanu, wazala uEnoshe.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> USete wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uEnoshe iminyaka emakhulu asibhozo aneminyaka esixhenxe; wazala oonyana
neentombi.

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> Iyonke imihla kaSete yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba anashumi-nye linamibini; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> UEnoshe wahlala iminyaka emashumi asithoba,
wazala uKenan.

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> UEnoshe wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uKenan iminyaka emakhulu asibhozo anashumi-nye linamihlanu; wazala
oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Iyonke imihla kaEnoshe yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba anamihlanu; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> UKenan wahlala iminyaka emashumi
asixhenxe, wazala uMahalaleli.

<span id="an_5:13">5:13</span> UKenan wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uMahalaleli iminyaka emakhulu asibhozo anamanci mane: wazala oonyana
neentombi.

<span id="an_5:14">5:14</span> Iyonke imihla kaKenan yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba, aneminyaka elishumi; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:15">5:15</span> UMahalaleli wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathandathu anamihlanu, wazala uYerede.

<span id="an_5:16">5:16</span> UMahalaleli wahlala emveni kokuzala
kwakhe uYerede iminyaka emakhulu asibhozo anamanci mathathu; wazala
oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:17">5:17</span> Iyonke imihla kaMahalaleli yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asibhozo anamanci asithoba anamihlanu; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:18">5:18</span> UYerede wahlala iminyaka elikhulu
elinamanci mathandathu anamibini, wazala uEnoki.

<span id="an_5:19">5:19</span> UYerede wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uEnoki iminyaka emakhulu asibhozo; wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:20">5:20</span> Iyonke imihla kaYerede yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba anamanci mathandathu anamihlanu, anamibini; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:21">5:21</span> UEnoki wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathandathu anamihlanu, wazala uMethusela.

<span id="an_5:22">5:22</span> UEnoki wahamba noThixo, emveni kokuzala
kwakhe uMethusela, iminyaka emakhulu mathathu; wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:23">5:23</span> Iyonke imihla kaEnoki yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu mathathu, anamanci mathandathu anamihlanu.

<span id="an_5:24">5:24</span> UEnoki wahamba noThixo; akabakho, ngokuba
uThixo wamthabatha.

<span id="an_5:25">5:25</span> UMethusela wahlala iminyaka elikhulu
elinamanci asibhozo anesixhenxe, wazala uLameki.

<span id="an_5:26">5:26</span> UMethusela wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uLameki iminyaka emakhulu asixhenxe anamanci asibhozo anamibini; wazala
oonyana eneentombi.

<span id="an_5:27">5:27</span> Iyonke imihla kaMethusela yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba, anamanci mathandathu anesithoba; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:28">5:28</span> ULameki wahlala iminyaka elikhulu
elinamanci asibhozo anamibini; wazala unyana.

<span id="an_5:29">5:29</span> Wamthiya igama elinguNowa, esithi, Lo uya
kusithuthuzela emsebenzini wethu, nasekubulalekeni kwezandla zethu,
ngenxa yomhlaba awawuqalekisayo uYehova.

<span id="an_5:30">5:30</span> ULameki wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uNowa iminyaka emakulu mahlanu anamanci asithoba anamihlanu; wazala
oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_5:31">5:31</span> Iyonke imihla kaLameki yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asixhenxe anesixhenxe; wafa ke.

<span id="an_5:32">5:32</span> Ke uNowa ebeminyaka imakhulu mahlanu
ezelwe; uNowa wazala ooShem noHam noYafete.

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> Kuthe bakuqala ukwanda abantu ehlabathini,
bakuzalelwa iintombi,

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> bazibona oonyana bakaThixo iintombi zabantu
ukuba zintle, bazeka abafazi kuzo zonke abazinyulayo.

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> Wathi uYehova, UMoya wam akayi kulawula
ebantwini ngonaphakade; ekulahlekeni kwabo bayinyama; imihla yabo iya
kuba yiminyaka elikhulu elinamanci mabini.

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> Kwakukho iingxilimbela ehlabathini ngaloo
mihla; kananjalo emveni koko, xeshikweni oonyana bakaThixo bangenayo
kuzo iintombi zabantu, zabazalela abantwana. Aba baba ngamagorha
ababekho kwasephakadeni, amadoda adumileyo.

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Wabona uThixo ukuba ububi babantu bandile
ehlabathini, konke ukuyila kweengcinga zentliziyo yabo kubububi bodwa
imihla yonke.

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> Wazohlwaya uYehova, ngokuba emenzile umntu
ehlabathini, kwaba buhlungu kuye entliziyweni.

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> Wathi uYehova, Ndiya kumcima umntu
endimdalileyo, angabikho ehlabathini, kuthabathele emntwini kuse
ezinkomeni, kuse ezinambuzaneni, kuse ezintakeni zezulu, ngokuba
ndizohlwaya ngokuba ndizenzile ezo zinto.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> UNowa yena wababalwa nguYehova.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaNowa. UNowa waye
eyindoda elilungisa, egqibeleleyo, ezizukulwaneni zakhe. UNowa wahamba
noThixo.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> UNowa wazala oonyana abathathu: uShem
noHam noYafete.

<span id="an_6:11">6:11</span> Ihlabathi lalonakele ebusweni bukaThixo;
ihlabathi lalizele lugonyamelo.

<span id="an_6:12">6:12</span> UThixo walikhangela ihlabathi, nalo,
lonakele! Ngokuba yonke inyama ibiyonakalisile indlela yayo ehlabathini.

<span id="an_6:13">6:13</span> Wathi uThixo kuNowa, Isiphelo senyama
yonke sifikile phambi kwam; ngokuba ihlabathi lizele lugonyamelo
oluphuma kubo; yabona ke, ndiya kubonakalisa, bona ndawonye nehlabathi.

<span id="an_6:14">6:14</span> Zenzele ke umkhombe ngemithi yegofere,
uwenze izindlu umkhombe, uwuqabe ngaphakathi nangaphandle ngebhitumene.

<span id="an_6:15">6:15</span> Wenjenje ukuwenza: bube ngamakhulu
omathathu eekubhite ubude bomkhombe, namashumi omathathu eekubhite
ububanzi bawo, namashumi omathathu eekubhite ukuphakama kwawo.

<span id="an_6:16">6:16</span> Wenze ikroba emkhombeni, ukuligqiba
kwakho kube yikubhite enye, ithabathela phezulu; umnyango womkhombe
uwumise ecaleni lawo; wenze izindlu zodidi lwaphantsi, nolwesibini,
nolwesithathu.

<span id="an_6:17">6:17</span> Mna ke, uyabona, ndihlisa unogumbe
wamanzi ehlabathini, wokonakalisa yonke inyama enomoya wokuphila kuyo,
ephantsi kwamazulu; konke okusehlabathini kuya kuphuma umphefumlo;

<span id="an_6:18">6:18</span> ndiwumise umnqophiso wam nawe, ungene
emkhombeni wena, noonyana bakho, nomkakho, nabafazi boonyana bakho,
ndawonye nawe.

<span id="an_6:19">6:19</span> Kwizinto zonke eziphilileyo, kwinyama
yonke, uze ungenise emkhombeni ngambini kuzo zonke, ukuze zisindiswe
nawe, ibe yinkunzi nemazi;

<span id="an_6:20">6:20</span> kwiintaka ngohlobo lwazo, kwiinkomo
ngohlobo lwazo, kuzo zonke izinambuzane zomhlaba ngohlobo lwazo, zibe
ngambini kuzo zonke, eziya kungena kuwe, ukuba zisindiswe.

<span id="an_6:21">6:21</span> Wena ke, uthabathele kuwe ekudleni konke
okudliwayo, uhlanganisele kuwe kube kukudla kuwe nakuzo.

<span id="an_6:22">6:22</span> Wenza uNowa konke uThixo abemwisele
umthetho ngako, wenza njengoko.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> Wathi uYehova kuNowa, Ngena, wena nendlu
yakho yonke, emkhombeni, ngokuba ndibona wena ilungisa phambi kwam kwesi
sizukulwana.

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> Kwizinto zonke ezizitho zine
ezihlambulukileyo, thabathela kuwe ngasixhenxe, ngasixhenxe, inkunzi
nemazi yayo; kwizinto ezizitho zine eziziinqambi thabatha ngambini,
inkunzi nemazi yayo;

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> nakwiintaka zezulu ngasixhenxe,
ngasixhenxe, inkunzi nemazi, ukuze imbewu igcinakale ehlabathini lonke.

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> Kuba zisesixhenxe iintsuku, ndize ndinise
imvula ehlabathini iimini zibe mashumi mane nobusuku obumashumi mane,
ndiyicime into yonke emiyo endayenzayo, ingabikho phezu kwehlabathi.

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> Wenza uNowa konke uYehova awamwisela
umthetho ngako.

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> UNowa waye eminyaka imakhulu mathandathu
ezelwe, wabakho unogumbe wamanzi ehlabathini.

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> Wangena uNowa emkhombeni, enoonyana bakhe,
nomkakhe, nabafazi boonyana bakhe, ndawonye naye, ngenxa yamanzi
onogumbe.

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> Kuzo izinto ezizitho zine
ezihlambulukileyo, nakuzo izinto ezizitho zine eziziinqambi, nakuzo
iintaka, nakuzo zonke izinto ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni,

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> kwangena ngambini, ngambini, kuNowa
emkhombeni, inkunzi nemazi, njengoko uThixo abemwisele umthetho uNowa.

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> Kwathi emva kweentsuku ezisixhenxe,
amanzi onogumbe abakho ehlabathini.

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> Ngomnyaka wamakhulu omathandathu wokudla
ubomi kukaNowa, ngenyanga yesibini, ngosuku lweshumi elinesixhenxe
enyangeni leyo, kanye ngayo loo mini, yagqabhuka yonke imithombo yamanzi
enzonzobila enkulu, iingcango zezulu zavuleka.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> Wabakho umvumbi wemvula ehlabathini
iimini ezimashumi mane nobusuku obumashumi mani.

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Wangena emkhombeni kwangaloo mini uNowa,
noShem noHam noYafete, oonyana bakaNowa, nomkaNowa, nabafazi bobathathu
boonyana bakhe, ndawonye naye.

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> Bona, neento zonke eziphilileyo ngohlobo
lwazo, nezinto zonke ezizitho zine ngohlobo lwazo, nezinambuzane zonke
ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni ngohlobo lwazo, neentaka zonke ngohlobo lwazo,
iinto zonke eziphaphazelayo, ezinamaphiko,

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> zangena kuNowa emkhombeni, ngambini,
ngambini, kwinyama yonke enomoya wokuphila kuyo.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> Zangena iinkunzi neemazi kwinyama yonke;
zangena njengoko uThixo abemwisele umthetho. UYehova wamvalela
ngaphakathi.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> Yaba ngunogumbe imihla emashumi mane
ehlabathini, enyuka amanzi, awufukula umkhombe, wafunquleka emhlabeni.

<span id="an_7:18">7:18</span> Aba namandla amanzi, enyuka kunene
ehlabathini, wahamba umkhombe phezu kwamanzi.

<span id="an_7:19">7:19</span> Aba namandla amanzi kunene kakhulu
ehlabathini, zagutyungelwa zonke iintaba eziphakamileyo kakhulu,
eziphantsi kwamazulu onke.

<span id="an_7:20">7:20</span> Aba namandla amanzi, ada aba ziikubhite
ezilishumi elinantlanu, ethabathela phezulu; zagutyungelwa ke iintaba.

<span id="an_7:21">7:21</span> Yaphuma umphefumlo yonke inyama
enambuzelayo emhlabeni, kwiintaka, nakwizinto ezizitho zine, nakwizinto
eziphilileyo, nakwinyakanyaka yonke enyakazelayo emhlabeni, nabantu
bonke.

<span id="an_7:22">7:22</span> Iinto zonke ezikuphefumla komoya
wokuphila kusemathatheni azo, kwiinto zonke ezisemhlabeni owomileyo,
zafa.

<span id="an_7:23">7:23</span> Zabhujiswa ke izinto zonke ezimiyo,
eziphezu komhlaba, kwathabathela emntwini kwesa ezintweni ezizitho zine,
nasezinambuzaneni, nasezintakeni zezulu; zabhujiswa azabakho
ehlabathini; kwasala uNowa yedwa, nababenaye emkhombeni.

<span id="an_7:24">7:24</span> Aba namandla amanzi ehlabathini imihla
elikhulu elinamanci mahlanu.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> UThixo wamkhumbula uNowa, neento zonke
eziphilileyo, nezinto zonke ezizitho zine ezazinaye emkhombeni; uThixo
wahambisa umoya ehlabathini, awutha amanzi.

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> Yavingcwa imithombo yamanzi enzonzobila
neengcango zezulu, wathintelwa umvumbi wezulu.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> Abuya amanzi emhlabeni, amana ebuya, awutha
amanzi ekupheleni kwemihla elikhulu elinamanci mahlanu.

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> Umkhombe wazimisa ngenyanga yesixhenxe,
ngosuku lweshumi elinesixhenxe enyangeni leyo, phezu kweentaba
zaseArarati.

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> Amanzi amana ewutha, kwada kwayinyanga
yeshumi; ngeyeshumi ke, ngosuku lokuqala enyangeni leyo, zabonakala
iincopho zeentaba.

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Kwathi, ekupheleni kwemihla emashumi mane,
wayivula uNowa ifestile yomkhombe abeyenzile;

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> wathuma ihlungulu, laphuma lamana
lizulazula, ada atsha amanzi ehlabathini.

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Wasusa ihobe, ukuze abone ukuba amanzi
awuthile na phezu kwehlabathi.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> Ihobe alifumananga ndawo yakuphumza
nentende yethupha lalo, labuyela kuye emkhombeni, ngokuba amanzi
abephezu kwehlabathi lonke; wolula isandla sakhe, walithabatha,
walingenisa kuye emkhombeni.

<span id="an_8:10">8:10</span> Walinda eminye imihla esixhenxe, waphinda
walisusa ihobe emkhombeni.

<span id="an_8:11">8:11</span> Leza kuye ihobe ngexesha langokuhlwa;
nanko, kukho igqabi lomnquma elisandula ukukhiwa emlonyeni walo; wazi
uNowa, ukuba ehlile amanzi ehlabathini.

<span id="an_8:12">8:12</span> Walinda eminye imihla ekwasixhenxe,
walisusa ihobe; aliphindanga libuyele kuye kanjalo.

<span id="an_8:13">8:13</span> Kwathi, ngomnyaka wamakhulu omathandathu
anamnye, ngolokuqala enyangeni yokuqala, amanzi atsha ehlabathini; uNowa
walususa uphahla lomkhombe; wakhangela, nango umhlaba womile.

<span id="an_8:14">8:14</span> Ngenyanga yesibini, ngosuku lwamashumi
omabini anesixhenxe enyangeni leyo, woma kwaphela umhlaba.

<span id="an_8:15">8:15</span> Wathetha uThixo kuNowa, esithi,

<span id="an_8:16">8:16</span> Phuma emkhombeni, wena nomkakho, noonyana
bakho, nabafazi boonyana bakho, ndawonye nawe.

<span id="an_8:17">8:17</span> Zonke izinto eziphilileyo ezikuwe,
kwinyama yonke, ezintakeni, nasezintweni ezizitho zine,
nasezinambuzaneni zonke ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni, phuma nazo, zizalise
ihlabathi, ziqhame, zande ehlabathini.

<span id="an_8:18">8:18</span> Waphuma ke uNowa, noonyana bakhe,
nomkakhe, nabafazi boonyana bakhe, ndawonye naye.

<span id="an_8:19">8:19</span> Zonke izinto eziphilileyo, zonke
izinambuzane, neentaka zonke, iinto zonke ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni,
ngeentlobo zazo, zaphuma emkhombeni.

<span id="an_8:20">8:20</span> UNowa wamakhela uYehova isibingelelo,
wathabatha kwizinto zonke ezizitho zine ezihlambulukileyo, nakwiintaka
zonke ezihlambulukileyo, wanyusa amadini anyukayo esibingelelweni eso.

<span id="an_8:21">8:21</span> UThixo weva ivumba elithozamisayo, wathi
uYehova entliziyweni yakhe, Andisayi kuphinda ndilitshabhise ihlabathi
ngenxa yomntu, ngokuba ukuyila kwentliziyo yomntu kubi kwasebutsheni
bakhe; andisayi kuphinda ndizibhubhise zonke izinto eziphilileyo,
njengoko ndenze ngako.

<span id="an_8:22">8:22</span> Kuthabathela apha, ngayo yonke imihla
yehlabathi, akuyi kuphela ukuhlwayela nokuvuna, ukubanda nobushushu,
ihlobo nobusika, imini nobusuku.

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> UThixo wamsikelela uNowa noonyana bakhe,
wathi kubo, Qhamani, nande, nizalise ihlabathi.

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> Ukoyikeka kwenu, nokuqhiphula kwenu
umbilini, makube phezu kwezinto zonke eziphilileyo zomhlaba, naphezu
kweentaka zonke zezulu, nakwiinto zonke ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni,
nakwiintlanzi zonke zolwandle; zona zinikelwe esandleni senu.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> Zonke izinambuzane eziphilileyo mazibe
kukudla kuni; njengomfuno oluhlaza, ndininikile oko konke.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> Yinyama yodwa enomphefumlo wayo, enegazi
layo, eningasayi kuyidla.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> Ligazi lenu lodwa, imiphefumlo yenu ke,
endiya kulibiza; esandleni sezinto zonke eziphilileyo ndiya kulibiza,
nasesandleni somntu; esandleni salowo ungumzalwana wakhe, ndiya kuwubiza
umphefumlo womntu.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Ophalaza igazi lomntu, igazi lakhe
lophalazwa ngumntu, ngokuba umntu wenziwa ngokomfanekiselo kaThixo.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> Nina ke, qhamani nande, nilizalise
ihlabathi, nande kulo.

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> Watsho uThixo kuNowa, nakoonyana bakhe
ndawonye naye, ukuthi,

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> Yabonani, mna ndiyawumisa umnqophiso wam
nani, nembewu yenu emva kwenu,

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> nayo yonke imiphefumlo ephilileyo ekuni,
kwiintaka, nakwizinto ezizitho zine, nakwizinto zonke eziphilileyo
zehlabathi ezikuni; kwiinto zonke eziphume emkhombeni, ezizizinto zonke
eziphilileyo zehlabathi.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> Ndiwumise umnqophiso wam nani, ukuba
ingabi sanqunyulwa yonke inyama ngamanzi onogumbe, kungabi sabakho
nogumbe wokulonakalisa ihlabathi.

<span id="an_9:12">9:12</span> Wathi uThixo, Nguwo lo umqondiso
womnqophiso endiwubekayo phakathi kwam nani, nayo yonke imiphefumlo
ephilileyo ekuni, kuse kwizizukulwana zasephakadeni:

<span id="an_9:13">9:13</span> umnyama wam ndiwubeke efini, ukuba ube
ngumqondiso womnqophiso ophakathi kwam nehlabathi.

<span id="an_9:14">9:14</span> Kothi, ndakuwusibekelisa ngelifu umhlaba,
ubonakale umnyama lowo efini;

<span id="an_9:15">9:15</span> ndiwukhumbule umnqophiso wam ophakathi
kwam nani, nayo yonke imiphefumlo ephilileyo enyameni yonke, angabi
sabakho amanzi onogumbe okonakalisa inyama yonke.

<span id="an_9:16">9:16</span> Umnyama woba semafini ke, ndiwukhangele,
ndikhumbule umnqophiso ongunaphakade phakathi koThixo nayo yonke
imiphefumlo ephilileyo, enyameni yonke esehlabathini.

<span id="an_9:17">9:17</span> Wathi uThixo kuNowa, Nguwo lowo umqondiso
womnqophiso endiwumisileyo phakathi kwam nayo yonke inyama
esehlabathini.

<span id="an_9:18">9:18</span> Ke kaloku oonyana bakaNowa, abaphuma
emkhombeni, babengooShem, noHam, noYafete; uHam ke nguyise kaKanan.

<span id="an_9:19">9:19</span> Aba bathathu ngoonyana bakaNowa; balizaza
ihlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_9:20">9:20</span> UNowa wathi, engumlimi womhlaba, waqala
watyala isidiliya.

<span id="an_9:21">9:21</span> Wasela iwayini, wanxila, wazihluba
phakathi kwentente yakhe.

<span id="an_9:22">9:22</span> UHam, uyise kaKanan, wabubona ubuze
bukayise, waxelela abakhuluwa bakhe bobabini ngaphandle.

<span id="an_9:23">9:23</span> UShem noYafete bathabatha ingubo,
bayibeka emagxeni abo bobabini, baya ngomva, babugubungela ubuze
bukayise.

<span id="an_9:24">9:24</span> Wavuka uNowa ewayinini yakhe, wakwazi
akwenzileyo unyana wakhe omnci kuye.

<span id="an_9:25">9:25</span> Wathi, Makaqalekiswe uKanan, Abe sisicaka
sezicaka kubazalwana bakhe.

<span id="an_9:26">9:26</span> Wathi, Makabongwe uYehova uThixo kaShem,
UKanan abe sisicaka kubo.

<span id="an_9:27">9:27</span> UThixo makamvulele uYafete, Ahlale
ezintenteni zikaShem, UKanan abe sisicaka kubo.

<span id="an_9:28">9:28</span> Wahlala uNowa emveni konogumbe iminyaka
emakhulu mthathu anamanci mahlanu.

<span id="an_9:29">9:29</span> Yonke imihla kaNowa yaba yiminyaka
emakhulu asithoba anamanci mahlanu; wafa ke.

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> Yiyo le ke inzala yoonyana bakaNowa:
uShem, noHam, noYafete. Bazalelwa oonyana emveni konogumbe.

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> Oonyana bakaYafete nguGomere, noMagogi,
noMadayi, noYavan, noTubhali, noMesheki, noTirasi.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> Oonyana bakaGomere nguAshekenazi,
noRifati, noTogarma.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> Oonyana bakaYavan nguElisha, noTarshishe,
ngamaKiti namaDodan.

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> Zadabuka kubo abo iziqithi zeentlanga
emazweni, lwaolo ngokolwimi lwalo, ngokwesizwe salo ezintlangeni zazo.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> Oonyana bakaHam nguKushi, noMitserayim,
noPuti, noKanan.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> Oonyana bakaKushi nguSebha, noHavila,
noSebheta, noRama, noSabheteka; oonyana bakaRama nguShebha noDedan.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> UKushi wazala uNimrodi; yena waqala waba
ligorha ehlabathini.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> Yena waba ligorha lezingela phambi
koYehova; ngenxa yoko kwathiwa, NjengoNimrodi, igorha lezingela phambi
koYehova.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> Ukuqala kobukumkani bakhe yiBhabheli,
ne-Ereki, neAkadi, neKalene, ezweni leShinare.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> Kulo elo zwe waphuma waya
kwelaseAsiriya, wikha iNineve neRehobhotire nomzi weKala,

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> neRezen, phakathi kweNineve neKala;
nguloo mzi mkhulu ke lowo.

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> UMitzerayim wazala amaLudi, nama-Anam,
namaLehabhi, namaNafetuyi,

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> namaPatrusi, namaKaseluyi, apho
kwaphuma khona amaFilisti namaKafetori.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> UKanan wazala uTsidon, owamazi bulo
wakhe, noHeti,

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> namaYebhusi, nama-Amori, namaGirgashi,

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> namaHivi, nama-Areki, namaSin,

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> nama-Arvadi, namaTsemari, namaHamati;
emveni koko zaphangalala izizwe zamaKanan.

<span id="an_10:19">10:19</span> Umda wamaKanan wathabathela eTsidon,
wasinga eGerare, wasa eGaza; wasinga eSodom, neGomora, neAdama,
neTsebhoyim, wasa eLasha.

<span id="an_10:20">10:20</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaHam, ngokwezizwe
zabo, ngokweelwimi zabo, emazweni abo, ezintlangeni zabo.

<span id="an_10:21">10:21</span> UShem wazalelwa naye; unguyise wabo
bonke oonyana bakaEbhere, ungumzalwana omkhulu kaYafete.

<span id="an_10:22">10:22</span> Oonyana bakaShem nguElam, noAsuri,
noArpakishadi, noLudi, noAram.

<span id="an_10:23">10:23</span> Oonyana baka-Aram ngu-Utse, noHuli,
noGetere, noMashi.

<span id="an_10:24">10:24</span> UArpakishadi wazala uShela, uShela
wazala uEbhere.

<span id="an_10:25">10:25</span> UEbhere wazalelwa oonyana bababini;
igama lomnye belinguPelege, ngokuba ngemihla yakhe bahlukahluka abemi
behlabathi; igama lomninawa wakhe belinguYoketan.

<span id="an_10:26">10:26</span> UYoketan wazala uAlemodadi, noShelefe,
noHatsaremavete, noYera,

<span id="an_10:27">10:27</span> noHadoram, noUzali, noDikela,

<span id="an_10:28">10:28</span> no-Obhali, noAbhimayeli, noShebha,

<span id="an_10:29">10:29</span> no-Ofire, noHavila, noYobhabhi; bonke
abo bangoonyana bakaYoketan.

<span id="an_10:30">10:30</span> Ukuma kwabo kwathabathela eMesha,
kwasinga eZefara, intaba yasempumalanga.

<span id="an_10:31">10:31</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaShem ngokwezizwe
zabo, ngokweelwimi zabo, emazweni abo, ngokweentlanga zabo.

<span id="an_10:32">10:32</span> Zizo ezo izizwe zoonyana bakaNowa,
ngokweenzalo zabo, ezintlangeni zabo; zadabuka kubo abo iintlanga
ehlabathini emveni konogumbe.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> Ke kaloku lonke ihlabathi libe
lintetho-nye, limazwi manye.

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Kwathi, ekundulukeni kwabo besinga
empumalanga, bafumana ithafa ezweni laseShinare; bahlala khona. Bathi
abanye kwabanye, Yizani, senze izitena, sizitshise kunene.

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> Baba nezitena endaweni yamatye,
nebhitumene endaweni yodaka.

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> Bathi, Yizani, sizakhele umzi, nepoma
lenqaba elincopho isemazulwini; sizenzele igama, hleze sichithakalele
ehlabathini lonke.

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> UYehova wehla, eza kukhangela umzi lowo,
nenqaba leyo inde, bayakhayo oonyana boluntu.

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> Wathi uYehova, Yabona, abantu banye,
bantetho-nye bonke bephela; yingqalo ke le yokwenza kwabo; kaloku abayi
kunqatyelwa nto bayinkqangiyeleyo ukuyenza.

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> Yizani, sihle, sidube khona apho intetho
yabo, ngokokuze bangevani ngentetho.

<span id="an_11:8">11:8</span> UYehova wabachithachitha kwalapho
ehlabathini lonke; bayeka ukuwakha loo mzi.

<span id="an_11:9">11:9</span> Ngenxa yoko kwathiwa igama lawo
yiBhabheli; ngokuba uYehova wayiduba khona apho intetho yehlabathi
lonke, wabachithachitha kwalapho uYehova ehlabathini lonke.

<span id="an_11:10">11:10</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaShem: uShem
ubeminyaka ilikhulu ezelwe, wazala uArpakishadi, iminyaka emibini emveni
konogumbe.

<span id="an_11:11">11:11</span> UShem wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uArpakishadi iminyaka emakhulu mahlanu, wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_11:12">11:12</span> UArpakishadi wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu anamihlanu, wazala uShela.

<span id="an_11:13">11:13</span> UArpakishadi wahlala emveni kokuzala
kwakhe uShela iminyaka emakhulu mane anamathathu, wazala oonyana
neentombi.

<span id="an_11:14">11:14</span> UShela wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu, wazala uEbhere.

<span id="an_11:15">11:15</span> UShela wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uEbhere iminyaka emakhulu mane anamithathu, wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_11:16">11:16</span> UEbhere wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu anamine, wazala uPelege.

<span id="an_11:17">11:17</span> UEbhere wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uPelege iminyaka emakhulu mane anamanci mathathu, wazala oonyana
neentombi.

<span id="an_11:18">11:18</span> UPelege wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu, wazala uRehu.

<span id="an_11:19">11:19</span> UPelege wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uRehu iminyaka emakhulu mabini anesithoba, wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_11:20">11:20</span> URehu wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu anamibini, wazala uSerugi.

<span id="an_11:21">11:21</span> URehu wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uSerugi iminyaka emakhulu mabini anesixhenxe, wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_11:22">11:22</span> USerugi wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mathathu, wazala uNahore.

<span id="an_11:23">11:23</span> USerugi wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uNahore iminyaka emakhulu mabini, wazala oonyana neentombi.

<span id="an_11:24">11:24</span> UNahore wahlala iminyaka emashumi
mabini anesithoba, wazala uTera.

<span id="an_11:25">11:25</span> UNahore wahlala emveni kokuzala kwakhe
uTera iminyaka elikhulu elinashumi-nye linesithoba, wazala oonyana
neentombi.

<span id="an_11:26">11:26</span> UTera wahlala iminyaka emashumi
asixhenxe, wazala uAbram, noNahore, noHaran.

<span id="an_11:27">11:27</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaTera: uTera wazala
uAbram, noNahore, noHaran; uHaran wazala uLote.

<span id="an_11:28">11:28</span> Wafa uHaran esekho uTera uyise, ezweni
lokuzalwa kwakhe, eUre yamaKaledi.

<span id="an_11:29">11:29</span> UAbram noNahore bazeka abafazi; igama
lomka-Abram lalinguSarayi; igama lomkaNahore lalinguMilka, intombi
kaHaran, usoMilka, usoYiska.

<span id="an_11:30">11:30</span> USarayi ebengazali, engenamntwana.

<span id="an_11:31">11:31</span> UTera wamthabatha uAbram, unyana wakhe,
noLote unyana kaHaran, unyana wonyana wakhe, noSarayi umolokazana wakhe,
umka-Abram unyana wakhe, baphuma nabo eUre yamaKaledi, besiya ezweni
lakwaKanan; bafika kwelakwaHaran, bahlala khona.

<span id="an_11:32">11:32</span> Imihla kaTera yaba yiminyaka emakhulu
mabini anamihlanu; wafa uTera kwelakwaHaran.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> Ke kaloku uYehova wathi kuAbram, Hamba,
umke ezweni lakowenu, kwelokuzalwa kwakho, nasendlwini kayihlo, uye
ezweni endokubonisa lona;

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> ndikwenze uhlanga olukhulu,
ndikusikelele, ndilikhulise igama lakho, ube yintsikelelo;

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> ndibasikelele abakusikelelayo,
ndimtshabhise okuqalekisayo; zisikeleleke ngawe zonke izizwe zehlabathi.

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> Wahamba uAbram njengoko wathethayo
uYehova kuye; wahamba naye uLote. UAbram ubeminyaka imashumi asixhenxe
anamihlanti ezelwe, ukuphuma kwakhe kwelakwaHaran.

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> UAbram wathabatha uSarayi umkakhe, noLote
unyana womninawa wakhe, nengqwebo yabo yonke ababeyiqwebile, nabantu
ababebafumene kwelakwaHaran; baphuma ke besiya ezweni lakwaKanan, bafika
ke ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> UAbram wacanda ilizwe, wada waya kwindawo
enoShekem, wada waya eMokini kaMore. AmaKanan abekho ngelo xesha kulo
ilizwe.

<span id="an_12:7">12:7</span> UYehova wabonakala kuAbram, wathi, Imbewu
yakho ndiya kuyinika eli lizwe. Wamakhela khona isibingelelo uYehova,
owabonakalayo kuye.

<span id="an_12:8">12:8</span> Wesuka khona waya entabeni
ngasempumalanga, eBheteli, wayitwabulula intente yakhe, iBheteli
ingasentshonalanga, iAyi ingasempumalanga; wamakhela khona isibingelelo
uYehova, wanqula igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_12:9">12:9</span> Wanduluka uAbram, ehamba encothula,
esinga kwelasezantsi.

<span id="an_12:10">12:10</span> Kwabakho indlala ezweni. Wehla uAbraham
waya eYiputa, ukuze aphambukele khona; ngokuba indlala ibinzima
elizweni.

<span id="an_12:11">12:11</span> Kwathi, akusondela ukuba angene
eYiputa, wathi kuSarayi umkakhe, Uyabona ke, ndiyazi ukuba ungumfazi
omhle imbonakalo.

<span id="an_12:12">12:12</span> Kothi ke, akukubona amaYiputa, athi,
Ngumkakhe lo; andibulale, akuyeke wena udle ubomi.

<span id="an_12:13">12:13</span> Uze uthi, ungudade wethu wena; ukuze
kulunge kum ngenxa yakho, umphefumlo wam udle ubomi ngenxa enawe.

<span id="an_12:14">12:14</span> Kwathi, akufika uAbram eYiputa, ambona
amaYiputa umfazi ukuba uyinzwakazi.

<span id="an_12:15">12:15</span> Bambona abathetheli bakaFaro, bamdumisa
kuFaro; umfazi wasiwa endlwini kaFaro.

<span id="an_12:16">12:16</span> Wamphatha ngokulungileyo uAbram ngenxa
yakhe; wanempahla emfutshane, neenkomo, namaesile, nabakhonzi,
nabakhonzazana, neemazi zamaesile, neenkamela.

<span id="an_12:17">12:17</span> UYehova wambetha uFaro nendlu yakhe
ngezibetho ezikhulu ngenxa kaSarayi, umka-Abram.

<span id="an_12:18">12:18</span> UFaro wambiza uAbram wathi, Yintoni na
le uyenzileyo kum? Yini na ukuba ungandixeleli ukuba ngumkakho?

<span id="an_12:19">12:19</span> Yini na ukuba uthi, ngudade wenu?
Ndamthabatha ukuba abe ngumfazi wam. Ngoku ke nanko unikakho, mthabathe
uhambe.

<span id="an_12:20">12:20</span> UFaro wawawisela umthetho amadoda
ngaye; amkhapha yena nomkakhe, nezinto zakhe zonke.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> Wenyuka uAbram, ephuma eYiputa, yena
nomkakhe, neento zakhe zonke, enoLote, esinga kwelasezantsi.

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> UAbram waye esisityebi kunene ngemfuyo,
nangesilivere, nangegolide.

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> Wahamba encothula, esuka kwelasezantsi,
wafika eBheteli, kuloo ndawo yayikhona intente yakhe matanci, phakathi
kweBheteli neAyi,

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> endaweni yesibingelelo awasenzayo khona
ekuqaleni. UAbram walinqula khona igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> Naye uLote, obehamba noAbram, waye
enempahla emfutshane, neenkomo, neentente.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> Ilizwe elo alaba nakubathwala, ukuba
bahlale ndawonye; ngokuba impahla yabo yayininzi, ababa nakuhlala
ndawonye.

<span id="an_13:7">13:7</span> Kwabakho ukubambana phakathi kwabalusi
bemfuyo ka-Abram nabalusi bemfuyo kaLote. Ngelo xesha ilizwe lalimiwe
ngamaKanan namaPerizi.

<span id="an_13:8">13:8</span> UAbram wathi kuLote, Makungabikho
mbambano kaloku phakathi kwam nawe, naphakathi kwabalusi bam nabalusi
bakho; ngokuba singamadoda azalanayo.

<span id="an_13:9">13:9</span> Aliphambi kwakho na ilizwe lonke?
Khawahluke kum; ukuba uya ekhohlo, ndoya ekunene, ukuba uya ekunene,
ndoya ekhohlo.

<span id="an_13:10">13:10</span> ULote waphakamisa amehlo akhe,
wawukhangela wonke ummandla waseYordan, ngokuba ubunamanzi wonke,
engekayonakalisi uYehova iSodom neGomora, unjengomyezo kaYehova,
unjengelizwe laseYiputa, usingise eTsohare.

<span id="an_13:11">13:11</span> ULote wawunyula wonke ummandla
waseYordan; wanduluka uLote waya ngasempumalanga; bahlukana ke.

<span id="an_13:12">13:12</span> UAbram wahlala ezweni lakwaKanan; uLote
wahlala emizini yaloo mmandla, wayisondezela eSodom intente yakhe.

<span id="an_13:13">13:13</span> Ke kaloku amadoda aseSodom ayengabenzi
bobubi, engaboni abakhulu kuYehova.

<span id="an_13:14">13:14</span> Wathi uYehova kuAbram, emveni kokuba
uLote ahlukane naye, Khawuwaphakamise amehlo akho ukuloo ndawo ukuyo,
ubhekise entla, nasezantsi, nasempumalanga, nasentshonalanga;

<span id="an_13:15">13:15</span> ngokuba lonke ilizwe olibonayo ndiya
kulinika wena, nembewu yakho, kude kuse ephakadeni;

<span id="an_13:16">13:16</span> ndiyenze imbewu yakho ibe njengothuli
lomhlaba, angathi ubani enako ukulubala uthuli lomhlaba, ayibale nembewu
yakho.

<span id="an_13:17">13:17</span> Suka, ulihambe ilizwe ngobude balo
nangobubanzi balo; ngokuba ndiya kulinika wena.

<span id="an_13:18">13:18</span> Wancothula uAbram intente yakhe, waya
wahlala ngaseMiokini kaMamre eseHebron, wakhela khona uYehova
isibingelelo.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> Kwathi ngemihla ka-Amrafele ukumkani
waseShinare, noAriyoki ukumkani wase-Elazare, noKedorlahomere ukumkani
wakwaElam, noTidali ukumkani wamaGoyi,

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> benza imfazwe noBhera ukumkani waseSodom,
noBhirsha ukumkani waseGomora, noShinabhi ukumkani waseAdama,
noShemebhere ukumkani waseTsebhoyim, nokumkani waseBhela, eyiTsohare.

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> Bonke abo baqukana entilini yaseSidim,
eluLwandle lweTyuwa.

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> Iminyaka elishumi elinamibini bakhonza
uKedorlahomere, bathi ngomnyaka weshumi elinantathu bagwilika.

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> Ngomnyaka weshumi elinamine weza
uKedorlahomere nookumkani ababanaye, bawatshabalalisa amaRafa
eAshtaroti-karnayim, namaZuzi eHam, namaEma ethafeni laseKiriyatayim,

<span id="an_14:6">14:6</span> namaHori entabeni yawo yakwaSehire, kwasa
kwiElparan, engasentlango.

<span id="an_14:7">14:7</span> Bajika, beza e-En-mishpati eyiKadeshe,
balitshabalalisa lonke ilizwe lakwa-Amaleki, nama-Amori abehleli
eHatsetson-tamare.

<span id="an_14:8">14:8</span> Waphuma ukumkani waseSodom, nokumkani
waseGomora, nokumkani waseAdama, nokumkani waseTsebhoyim, nokumkani
waseBhela, eyiTsohare, bakha uluhlu lokulwa nabo entilini yaseSidim;

<span id="an_14:9">14:9</span> noKedorlahomere ukumkani wakwaElam,
noTidali ukumkani wamaGoyi, noAmrafele ukumkani waseShinare, noAriyoki
ukumkani wase-Elazare: ookumkani abahlanu balwa nabane.

<span id="an_14:10">14:10</span> Ke intili yaseSidim yaye iyimingxuma
yodwa yebhitumene; basaba ookumkani, owaseSodom, nowaseGomora, beyela
khona, amasalela asabela entabeni.

<span id="an_14:11">14:11</span> Bayithabatha yonke impahla yaseSodom,
neGomora, nako konke ukudla kwabo, bemka.

<span id="an_14:12">14:12</span> Bamthabatha noLote, nempahla yakhe,
unyana womninawa ka-Abram, bemka; kuba wayehleli eSodom.

<span id="an_14:13">14:13</span> Wafika osindileyo, waxelela uAbram,
umHebhere; yena ebehleli eMiokini kaMamre umAmori, umzalwana kaEshkoli,
nomzalwana ka-Anere; bona ke bebengamanqophisana noAbram.

<span id="an_14:14">14:14</span> Weva ke uAbram, ukuba uthinjiwe
umzalwana wakhe, wawaphalaza amadoda akhe aqeqeshiweyo, azalelwe
endlwini yakhe, angamakhulu mathathu aneshumi elinesibhozo, wasukela,
waya kufika kwaDan.

<span id="an_14:15">14:15</span> Wawahlulahlula, wabawela ebusuku, yena
nabakhonzi bakho, wabagxotha, wabasukela wasa eHobha, engasekhohlo
kweDamasko.

<span id="an_14:16">14:16</span> Wazibuyisa zonke iimpahla, kwanoLote
unizalwana wakhe, wazibuyisa neempahla zakhe, kwanabafazi nabantu.

<span id="an_14:17">14:17</span> Waphuma ukumkani waseSodom, esiya
kumkhawulela ekubuyeni kwakhe ekutshabalaliseni uKedorlahomere,
nookumkani ebabenaye, entilini yeShave, eyintili yookumkani.

<span id="an_14:18">14:18</span> UMelkitsedeke, ukumkani waseSalem,
waphuma enesonka newayini, ubengumbingeleli kaThixo Osenyangweni.

<span id="an_14:19">14:19</span> Wamsikelela wathi, Makasikelelwe uAbram
nguThixo Osenyangweni, uMninimazulu nehlabathi!

<span id="an_14:20">14:20</span> Makabongwe uThixo Osenyangweni
obanikeleyo ababandezeli bakho esandleni sakho. UAbram wamnika isishumi
seento zonke.

<span id="an_14:21">14:21</span> Wathi ukumkani waseSodom, kuAbram,
Ndinike abantu, uthabathe impahla.

<span id="an_14:22">14:22</span> Wathi uAbram kukumkani waseSodom,
Isandla sam ndisiphakamisele kuYehova uThixo Osenyangweni, uMninimazulu
nehlabathi,

<span id="an_14:23">14:23</span> ukuba andiyi kuthabatha nosinga, nokuba
ngumtya wembadada, ukuba andiyi kuthabatha kuko konke okwakho; ukuze
ungatsho ukuthi, Mna nidimtyebisile uAbram.

<span id="an_14:24">14:24</span> Makungabikho nto iyeyam, kuphela ibe
yile nto idliweyo ngabafana, nesabelo samadoda abehamba nam, uAnere,
noEshkoli, noMamre; wona makasithabathe isabelo sawo.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> Emveni kwezo zinto, lafika ilizwe
likaYehova kuAbram ngombono, lisithi, Musa ukoyika, Abram;
ndiyingweletshetshe yakho, umvuzo wakho omkhulu kunene.

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> Wathi uAbram, Nkosi yam, Yehova,
wondinika ntoni na? Ndihamba ndingenamntwana; indlamafa yendlu yam ngulo
Eliyezere waseDamasko.

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> Wathi uAbram, Yabona, akundinikanga
mbewu; yabona, umntu ongowendlu yam uya kuba yindlamafa yam.

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> Nalo ilizwi likaYehova lifika kuye,
lisithi, Akayi kuba yindlamafa yakho lo; ngoya kuphuma ezibilini zakhe,
yena oya kuba yindlamafa yakho.

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> Wamsa phandle, wathi, Khawubheke phezulu
ezulwini, uzibale iinkwenkwezi, ukuba unokuzibala; wathi kuye, Iya kuba
njalo ke imbewu yakho.

<span id="an_15:6">15:6</span> Wakholwa kuYehova; oko wakubalela
ebulungiseni kuye.

<span id="an_15:7">15:7</span> Wathi kuye, NdinguYehova owakukhuphayo
eUre yamaKaledi, ukuba ndikunike eli lizwe, ulidle ilifa.

<span id="an_15:8">15:8</span> Wathi yena, Nkosi Yehova, ndiya kwazi
ngantoni na, ukuba ndiya kulidla ilifa?

<span id="an_15:9">15:9</span> Wathi kuye, Ndithabathele ithokazi
eliminyaka mithathu, nemazi yebhokhwe eminyaka mithathu, nenkunzi yemvu
eminyaka mithathu, nehobe, negobo levukuthu.

<span id="an_15:10">15:10</span> Wamthabathela ke zonke ezo zinto,
wazicanda kubini, wazibeka izahlulo, esinye sakhangelana nesinye; ke
zona iintaka akazicanda.

<span id="an_15:11">15:11</span> Ehla amaxhalanga phezu kwezidumbu,
wawaphekuza uAbram.

<span id="an_15:12">15:12</span> Kwathi, xa litshonayo ilanga, efikelwe
uAbram bubuthongo obukhulu, wabo na efikelwa kukothuka nabubumnyama
obukhulu.

<span id="an_15:13">15:13</span> Wathi kuAbram, Yazi ke, ukuba imbewu
yakho iya kuba ngumphambukeli ezweni elingelayo, ibakhonze abo,
bayicinezele, iminyaka emakhulu mane.

<span id="an_15:14">15:14</span> Kananjalo uhlanga eya kulukhonza ndiya
kulugweba; emveni koko iya kuphuma ineempahla ezininzi.

<span id="an_15:15">15:15</span> Ke wena uya kuya kooyihlo unoxolo;
ungcwatywe uyingwevu enkulu.

<span id="an_15:16">15:16</span> Kwesesine isizukulwana iya kubuyela
apha, kuba ubugwenxa bama-Amori abukazaliseki.

<span id="an_15:17">15:17</span> Kwathi, lakuba litshonile ilanga,
kwakuba sithokothoko, wabona kukho; iziko eliqhumayo, elinelangatye
elidangazelayo, elacanda phakathi kwezo zahlulo.

<span id="an_15:18">15:18</span> Ngaloo mini ke uYehova wenza umnqophiso
noAbram, wathi, Imbewu yakho ndiyinike eli lizwe, lithabathele emlanjeni
waseYiputa, lise emlanjeni omkhulu, emlanjeni ongumEfrati:

<span id="an_15:19">15:19</span> amaKeni, namaKinazi, namaKadimon,

<span id="an_15:20">15:20</span> namaHeti, namaPerizi, namaRafa,

<span id="an_15:21">15:21</span> nama-Amori, namaKanan, namaGirigashi,
namaYebhusi.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> Ke kaloku uSarayi umka-Abram
ubengamzaleli mntwana. Waye enomkhonzazana ongumYiputazana, ogama
belinguHagare.

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Wathi uSarayi kuAbram, Yabona, uYehova
undivingcile ukuba ndingazali; khawungene kumkhonzazana wam lo,
mhlawumbi ndingakheka ngaye. Waliphulaphula uAbram izwi likaSarayi.

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Wathi uSarayi, umka-Abram, wamthabatha
uHagare umYiputazana, umkhonzazana wakhe, emveni kokuba uAbram wayehleli
iminyaka elishumi ezweni lakwaKanan, wamnika uAbram indoda yakhe ukuba
abe ngumkakhe.

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> Wamngena ke uHagare, wamitha; akubona
ukuba umithi, inkosikazi yakhe yacukucezeka emehlweni akhe.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> Wathi uSarayi kuAbram, Ukoniwa kwam
makube phezu kwakho; umkhonzazana wam ndimnike mna esifubeni sakho; uthe
akubona ukuba umithi, ndacukucezeka emehlweni akhe; uYehova makagwebe
phakathi kwam nawe.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> Wathi uAbram kuSarayi, Yabona,
umkhonzazana wakho asesandleni sakho; yenza kuye okulungileyo emehlweni
akho. USarayi wamcinezela, wabaleka wemka ebusweni bakhe.

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> Ke kaloku isithunywa sikaYehova samfumana
ngasemthonjeni wamanzi entlango, ngasemthonjeni osendleleni eya eShure.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> Sathi, Hagare, mkhonzazana kaSarayi,
uvela phi na, usiya phi na? Wathi, Ndibaleke ndemka ebusweni bukaSarayi,
inkosikazi yam.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> Sathi isithunywa sikaYehova kuye, Buyela
kwinkosikazi yakho, uzithobe phantsi kwesandla sayo.

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> Sathi isithunywa sikaYehova kuye, Ndiya
kuyandisa kakhulu imbewu yakho, ingabalwa ngenxa yobuninzi.

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> Sathi isithunywa sikaYehova kuye,
Yabona umithi; uya kuzala unyana, umthiye igama elinguIshmayeli, ngokuba
uYehova uzivile iintsizi zakho.

<span id="an_16:12">16:12</span> Yena uya kuba ngumntu onjenge-esile
lasendle ukundweba; isandla sakhe siya kuchasana nabantu bonke, isandla
sabantu bonke sichasane naye; ahlale ebusweni babazalwana bakhe bonke.

<span id="an_16:13">16:13</span> Walibiza igama likaYehova, obethetha
naye, wathi, UnguThixo ozibonakalisayo. Ngokuba wathi, Ndisabona na
nalapha, emveni kokuba ndimbonile?

<span id="an_16:14">16:14</span> Ngenxa yoko walithiya elo qula igama
lokuthi liQula likaPhila-ebonile; nalo phakathi kweKadeshe neBherede.

<span id="an_16:15">16:15</span> UHagare wamzalela uAbram unyana; uAbram
ukumthiya igama unyana wakhe, lowo abemzalele yena uHagare, wathi
nguIshmayeli.

<span id="an_16:16">16:16</span> UAbram ubeminyaka imashumi asibhozo
anamithandathu ezelwe, oko uHagare wamzalelayo uAbram uIshmayeli.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> Kwathi, uAbram akuba minyaka imashumi
asithoba anesithoba ezelwe, uYehova wabonakala kuAbram, wathi kuye,
NdinguThixo uSomandla; hamba phambi kwam ube ngogqibeleleyo.

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> Ndiya kuwubeka umnqophiso wam phakathi
kwam nawe, ndikwandise kakhulu kunene.

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> Wawa uAbram ngobuso bakhe.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> UThixo wathetha naye, esithi, Mna,
yabona, umnqophiso wam unawe; uya kuba nguyise wengxokolo yeentlanga.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> Kananjalo akusayi kuthiwa igama lakho
nguAbram; igama lakho liya kuba nguAbraham, ngokuba ndikwenze uyise
wengxokolo yeentlanga;

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> ndiya kukuqha misa kakhulu kunene,
ndikwenze iintlanga, kuphume ookumkani kuwe;

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> ndiwumise umnqophiso wam phakathi kwam
nawe, naphakathi kwembewu yakho emva kwakho kwizizukulwana zayo, ube
ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade, wokuba ndibe nguThixo kuwe, nakwimbewu yakho
emva kwakho;

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> ndilinike wena nembewu yakho emva kwakho
ilizwe lokuphambukela kwakho, lonke ilizwe eli lakwaKanan, ukuba libe
yinto yenu ngonaphakade, ndibe nguThixo wabo.

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> Wathi uThixo kuAbraham, Wena ke,
umnqophiso wam wowugcina, nembewu yakho emva kwakho kwizizukulwana zabo.

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> Nguwo lo umnqophiso wam eniya kuwugcina
phakathi kwam nani, nembewu yakho emva kwakho: wokuba yonke into
eyindoda kuni yaluswe; naluswe inyama yokwaluswa;

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> oko kube ngumqondiso womnqophiso
ophakathi kwam nani.

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> Unyana omihla isibhozo makaluswe kuni,
yonke into eyindoda kwizizukulwana zenu, ezelwe endlwini, nezuzwe
ngemali kubani wolunye uhlanga, ongengowembewu yakho yena.

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> Makaluswe ozelwe endlwini yakho,
nozuzwe ngemali yakho; umnqophiso wam enyameni yenu uya kuba
ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade.

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> Into eyindoda engalukileyo, enyama
yokwaluswa ingaluswanga, loo mphefumlo mawunqanyulwe, ungabikho
ebantwini bakowawo; uwaphule umnqophiso wam.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> Wathi uThixo kuAbraham, USarayi umkakho
akuyi kumbiza ngegama lokuba nguSarayi; igama lakhe loba nguSara.

<span id="an_17:16">17:16</span> Ndiya kumsikelela; kananjalo ndikunike
unyana ngaye, ndimsikelele, abe ziintlanga, kuphume ookumkani bezizwe
kuye.

<span id="an_17:17">17:17</span> UAbraham wawa ngobuso bakhe, wahleka,
wathi entliziyweni yakhe, Azi umntu ominyaka ilikhulu wozalelwa na? Azi
uSara, intokazi eminyaka imashumi asithoba, angazala na?

<span id="an_17:18">17:18</span> Wathi uAbraham kuThixo, Wanga
uIshmayeli angadla ubomi phambi kwakho!

<span id="an_17:19">17:19</span> Wathi uThixo, Ewe, uSara umkakho uya
kukuzalela unyana, umbize ngegama lokuba nguIsake; ndiwumise umnqophiso
wam naye, ube ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade kwimbewu yakhe emva kwakhe.

<span id="an_17:20">17:20</span> Ngokusingisele kuIshmayeli ndikuvile;
uyabona, ndimsikelele, ndimqhamisile, ndimandisile kakhulu kunene. Uya
kuzala izikhulu ezilishumi elinazibini, ndimenze uhlanga olukhulu.

<span id="an_17:21">17:21</span> Umnqophiso wam wona ndowumisa noIsake,
oya kumzalelwa nguSara ngeli xesha nyakenye.

<span id="an_17:22">17:22</span> Wagqiba ukuthetha naye. Wenyuka uThixo
esuka kuAbraham.

<span id="an_17:23">17:23</span> UAbraham wamthabatha uIshmayeli unyana
wakhe, nabo bonke abazalelwe endlwini yakhe, nabo bonke abazuzwe ngemali
yakhe, yonke into eyindoda phakathi kwabantu bendlu ka-Abraham, wayalusa
inyama yokwaluswa kwangaloo mini, njengoko abethethile uThixo kuye.

<span id="an_17:24">17:24</span> UAbraham ebeminyaka imashumi asithoba
anesithoba ezelwe, ukwaluswa kwenyama yokwaluswa.

<span id="an_17:25">17:25</span> UIshmayeli, unyana wakhe, ebeminyaka
ilishumi elinamithathu ezelwe, ukwaluswa kwenyama yokwaluswa.

<span id="an_17:26">17:26</span> Kwangaloo mini waluswa uAbraham,
noIshmayeli unyana wakhe.

<span id="an_17:27">17:27</span> Nawo onke amadoda endlu yakhe, azalelwe
endlwini yakhe, nazuzwe ngemali kubani wolunye uhlanga, aluswa kunye
naye.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> UYehova wabonakala kuye eMiokini kaMamre,
ehleli emnyango wentente, ekufudumaleni kwemini.

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> Wawaphakamisa amehlo akhe, wabona, nango
amadoda amathathu emi ngakuye. Wabona, wagidima, eya kuwa khawulela,
esuka emnyango wentente.

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Waqubuda emhlabeni, wathi, Nkosi yam,
ukuba kaloku ndibabalwe nguwe, musa ukudlula umke kumkhonzi wakho.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> Makhe kuthatyathwe intwana yamanzi,
nihlambe iinyawo zenu, ningqengqe phantsi komthi lo;

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> ndithabathe iqhekeza lesonka, nixhase
iintliziyo zenu; kamva nodlula; kuba nize kudlula ngenxa yoko kumkhonzi
wenu. Athi, Yenza ngoko uthethe ngako.

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> Wakhawuleza uAbraham, waya ententeni
kuSara, wathi, Khawuleza, uxovule iiseha ezintathu zomgubo ocoliweyo,
wenze amaqebengwana ezonka.

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> Wagidima waya ezinkomeni uAbraham,
wathabatha ithole lenkomo, lithambile, lilungile, wanika umfana,
wakhawuleza ukulilungisa.

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> Wathabatha amasi, nobisi, nethole lenkomo
abelilungisile, wabeka phambi kwawo, wema ngakuwo phantsi komthi lowo,
adla.

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> Athi kuye, Uphi na uSara umkakho?

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> Wathi, Nanko ententeni. Yathi, Ndiya
kubuyela kuwe, lakubuya eli xesha; yabona, uSara umkakho uya kuba
nonyana. Weva uSara esemnyango wentente, wona esemva kwayo.

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> Ke kaloku uAbraham noSara
babesebaluphele, sebekhulile; kusekunqamkile kuSara okwendlela yabafazi.

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> USara wahleka ngaphakathi kwakhe,
esithi, Emveni kokuba ndihagele, ndisaya kuyolelwa na, nenkosi yam
yaluphele nje?

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> Wathi uYehova kuAbraham, Yini na ukuba
uSara ahleke, esithi, Kuhleliwe nje ndiya kuzala na ndaluphele nje mna?

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> Kukho nto ingamnqabelayo na uYehova?
Ngexesha elimisiweyo ndiya kubuyela kuwe, lakubuya eli xesha, uSara abe
nonyana.

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> Wakhanyela uSara, esithi, Andihlekanga;
kuba ebesoyika. Wathi yena, Hayi, uhlekile.

<span id="an_18:16">18:16</span> Asuka ke amadoda lawo ondela eSodom;
uAbraham ehamba nawo, ewaphelekelela.

<span id="an_18:17">18:17</span> Wathi uYehova, Ndomfihlela na uAbraham
into endiza kuyenza?

<span id="an_18:18">18:18</span> Kanti uAbraham uya kuthi abe luhlanga
olukhulu, olunamandla, zisikeleleke ngaye iintlanga zonke zehlabathi.

<span id="an_18:19">18:19</span> Kuba ndaze yena, ukuze abawisele
umthetho abantwana bakhe, nendlu yakhe emva kwakhe, bagcine indlela
kaYehova, benze ubulungisa nokusesikweni, ukuze uYehova amenzele
uAbraham into ayithethileyo kuye.

<span id="an_18:20">18:20</span> Wathi uYehova, Isikhalo saseSodom
neGomora sisikhulu nje, nesono sayo sinzima kunene nje,

<span id="an_18:21">18:21</span> ndiya kukha ndihle, ndikhangele ukuba
baphelelisile na ngokwesikhalo sayo esifikileyo kum; ukuba akunjalo,
ndazi.

<span id="an_18:22">18:22</span> Ajika apho amadoda lawo, asinga eSodom;
ke yena uAbraham wayesemi phambi koYehova.

<span id="an_18:23">18:23</span> Wasondela uAbraham, wathi, Ungade
ubhebhethe olilungisa kunye nongendawo yini na?

<span id="an_18:24">18:24</span> Hi, kwakho amashumi amahlanu amalungisa
phakathi komzi; ungade uyibhebhethe, ungayixoleli, loo ndawo yini na,
ngenxa yamalungisa amashumi mahlanu akuyo?

<span id="an_18:25">18:25</span> Makube lee kuwe ukwenza ngokwendawo
enjalo ukubulala olilungisa kunye nongendawo, ilungisa libe
njengongendawo; makube lee kuwe. Umgwebi wehlabathi lonke akayi kwenza
okusesikweni yini na?

<span id="an_18:26">18:26</span> Wathi uYehova, Ukuba ndithe ndafumana
eSodom amalungisa amashumi mahlanu phakathi komzi, ndoyixolela yonke loo
ndawo ngenxa yawo.

<span id="an_18:27">18:27</span> Waphendula uAbraham, wathi, Khawubone,
sendide ndathetha eNkosini, ndiluthuli nothuthu.

<span id="an_18:28">18:28</span> Hi ke, kwasweleka isihlanu kumalungisa
amashumi mahlanu, wowonakalisa ngenxa yesihlanu yini na wonke umzi?
Yathi, Andiyi kuwonakalisa, ukuba ndithe ndafumana khona amashumi omane
anesihlanu.

<span id="an_18:29">18:29</span> Waphinda kanjalo wathetha kuye, wathi,
Hi ke, kwafunyanwa khona amashumi omane? Yathi, Andiyi kukwenza ngenxa
yamashumi omane.

<span id="an_18:30">18:30</span> Wathi, Mayingabi namsindo iNkosi, khe
ndithethe. Hi ke, kwafunyanwa khona amashumi omathathu? Yathi, Andiyi
kukwenza, ukuba ndithe ndafumana khona amashumi omathathu.

<span id="an_18:31">18:31</span> Wathi, Khawubone, sendide ndathetha
eNkosini. Hi ke, kwafunyanwa khona amashumi omabini? Yathi, Andiyi
kuwonakalisa ngenxa yamashumi omabini.

<span id="an_18:32">18:32</span> Wathi, Mayingabi namsindo iNkosi,
khendithethe esi sihlandlo sodwa. Hi ke, kwafunyanwa khona ishumi
elinye? Yathi, Andiyi kuwonakalisa ngenxa yeshumi elinye.

<span id="an_18:33">18:33</span> Wemka uYehova, akugqiba ukuthetha
kuAbraham; uAbraham wabuyela endaweni yakhe.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> Zafika izithunywa ezo zozibini eSodom
ngokuhlwa, uLote ehleli esangweni leSodom. ULote wazibona, wesuka waya
kuzikhawulela, waqubuda ngobuso emhlabeni.

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> Wathi, Khanibone, zinkosi zam!
Khaniphambukele endlwini yomkhonzi wenu, nilale, nihlambe iinyawo zenu,
nivuke kusasa, nihambe indlela yenu. Zathi, Hayi, solala esitratweni.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> Wazijoka kunene, zaphambukela kuye,
zangena endlwini yakhe; wazenzela isidlo, woja nezonka ezingenagwele,
zadla.

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> Ke kaloku, zingekalali, amadoda aloo mzi,
amadoda aseSodom, ayirhawula indlu, ethabathela kumfana esa kwixhego,
bonke abantu bevela nasekupheleni kwawo.

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> Bambiza uLote, bathi kuye, Aphi na
amadoda angene kuwe ngobu busuku? Wakhuphele kuthi, siwazi.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> Waphuma uLote waya kubo emnyango,
waluvala ucango emva kwakhe,

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> wathi, Musani ukwenza into embi,
bazalwana.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> Khanibone, ndineentombi ezimbini
ezingazani nandoda; mandikhuphele zona kuni, nenze kuzo ngoko
kulungileyo emehlweni enu. Ke kula madoda musani ukwenza nto, kuba
angene ngenxa yoko emthunzini wophahla lwam.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> Bathi, Khwelela; batsho bathi, Lo wezayo
ngokuphambukela uhlala egweba; ngoku sokuphatha kakubi wena kunawo.
Besuka indulumbane phezu kwendoda uLote, basondela, beza kuluqhekeza
ucango.

<span id="an_19:10">19:10</span> Amadoda lawo asolula isandla sawo,
amngenisa uLote kuwo endlwini, aluvala ucango.

<span id="an_19:11">19:11</span> Awabetha ngobumfama amadoda
abesemnyango wendlu, ethabathela kwencinane esa kwenkulu, azidinisa ke
ukufuna umnyango.

<span id="an_19:12">19:12</span> Athi amadoda lawo kuLote, Usenabani na
apha? Umyeni, noonyana bakho, neentombi zakho, nabo bonke onabo kulo
mzi, bakhuphe kule ndawo;

<span id="an_19:13">19:13</span> ngokuba siya kuyonakalisa le ndawo,
ngokuba sikhulu isikhalo sabo ebusweni bukaYehova. UYehova usithume
ukuba siyonakalise.

<span id="an_19:14">19:14</span> Waphuma, uLote, wathetha kubayeni
beentombi zakhe, abaya kuzeka iintombi zakhe, wathi, Sukani, niphume
kule ndawo; ngokuba uYehova uya kuwonakalisa lo mzi. Usuke waba
njengohlekisayo emehlweni abayeni beentombi zakhe.

<span id="an_19:15">19:15</span> Izithunywa zamngxamisa uLote
ngesifingo, zathi, Vuka, thabatha umkakho, neentombi zakho zombini, aba
banokufumaneka, hleze ubhebhethwe ngobugwenxa balo mzi.

<span id="an_19:16">19:16</span> Wazilazila; amadoda abamba isandla
sakhe, nesandla somkakhe, nesandla seentombi zakhe zombini; uYehova
emvela, amkhupha, amyeka ngaphandle komzi.

<span id="an_19:17">19:17</span> Akuba emkhuphele phandle, athi,
Zisindise ngenxa yomphefumlo wakho. Musa ukubheka emva kwakho, musa
ukuma kuwo wonke lo mmandla; zisindise ngokuya entabeni, hleze
ubhebhethwe.

<span id="an_19:18">19:18</span> Wathi kuwo uLote, Hayi, Nkosi yam.

<span id="an_19:19">19:19</span> Khawubone, umkhonzi wakho umbabale.
Uyikhulisile inceba yakho ondenzeleyo, ukuba uwusindise umphefumlo wam;
mna ke andinako ukuzisindisa ngokuya entabeni, hleze ndinanyathelwe
bububi, ndife.

<span id="an_19:20">19:20</span> Khawubone, lo mzi ukufuphi, ukuba
kubalekelwe kuwo, mncinane; ndanga ndingazisindisa ngokuya kuwo
(awumncinane na?), usinde umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_19:21">19:21</span> Wathi kuye, Yabona, ndikunonelele
nangale nto, ukuba ndingawubhukuqi lo mzi uthethe ngawo.

<span id="an_19:22">19:22</span> Khawuleza, zisindise ngokuya khona,
kuba andinakwenza nto ude ufike khona. Ngenxa yoko igama laloo mzi
kwathiwa yiTsohare.

<span id="an_19:23">19:23</span> Ilanga lalise liphumile phezu
kwehlabathi, ukufika kukaLote eTsohare.

<span id="an_19:24">19:24</span> Wanisa ke uYehova phezu kweSodom
neGomora isulfure nomlilo ophuma kuYehova emazulwini;

<span id="an_19:25">19:25</span> wayibhukuqa loo mizi, nawo wonke loo
mmandla, nabo, bonke abemi baloo mizi, nesihlumo somhlaba.

<span id="an_19:26">19:26</span> Kodwa umkakhe, esemva kwakhe,
wakhangela ngasemva, waba yintsika yetyuwa.

<span id="an_19:27">19:27</span> UAbraham wavuka kusasa, waya kuloo
ndawo wayemi kuyo ebusweni bukaYehova.

<span id="an_19:28">19:28</span> Wondela eSodom neGomora, nakulo lonke
ilizwe laloo mmandla. Wakhangela; nango unyuka umsi welo zwe, njengomsi
weziko lemfutho.

<span id="an_19:29">19:29</span> Kwathi, xenikweni uThixo wayonakalisayo
imizi yaloo mmandla, uThixo wamkhumbula uAbraham, wamkhupha uLote
phakathi kobhukuqo olo, ekuyibhukuqeni imizi leyo abehleli kuyo uLote.

<span id="an_19:30">19:30</span> Wenyuka uLote ephuma eTsohare, wahlala
entabeni, eneentombi zakhe zombini, kuba ebesoyika ukuhlala eTsohare;
wahlala emqolombeni, yena neentombi zakhe zombini.

<span id="an_19:31">19:31</span> Yathi eyamazibulo kwencinane, Ubawo
waluphele; akukho ndoda ezweni apha yokusingena ngokwendlela yehlabathi
lonke;

<span id="an_19:32">19:32</span> yiza, simseze ubawo iwayini, silale
naye, sigcine imbewu ngobawo.

<span id="an_19:33">19:33</span> Zamseza ke uyise iwayini ngobo busuku;
yangena eyamazibulo, yalala noyise; akayazanga yena ukulala kwayo
nokuvuka kwayo.

<span id="an_19:34">19:34</span> Kwathi ngengomso, yathi eyamazibulo
kwencinane, Yabona, ndilele nobawo phezolo; masimseze iwayini nangobu
busuku, ungene, ulale naye, ukuba sigcine imbewu ngobawo.

<span id="an_19:35">19:35</span> Zamseza ke uyise iwayini nangobo
busuku, yasuka, encinane yalala naye; akayazanga yena ukulala kwayo
nokuvuka kwayo.

<span id="an_19:36">19:36</span> Zamitha zombini iintombi zikaLote
ngoyise.

<span id="an_19:37">19:37</span> Eyamazibulo yazala unyana, yambiza
ngegama elinguMowabhi; yena nguyise wamaMowabhi unanamhla.

<span id="an_19:38">19:38</span> Nencinane yazala unyana, yambiza
ngegama elinguBhenami; yena nguyise wonyana baka-Amon unanamhla.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> Ke kaloku uAbraham wanduluka apho, waya
ezweni lasezantsi, wahlala phakathi kweKadeshe neShure, waphambukela
eGerare.

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> Wathi uAbraham ngoSara umkakhe, Ngudade
wethu. UAbhimeleki ukumkani waseGerare wathuma, wamthabatha uSara.

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Weza uThixo kuAbhimeleki ngephupha
ebusuku, wathi kuye, Uyabona, ufile ngenxa yomfazi omthabathileyo;
ngumkamntu.

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> Ke uAbhimeleki ubengasondelanga kuye;
wathi, Nkosi, nolunobulungisa uhlanga wolubulala, yini na?

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> Akatshongo na yena kum ukuthi, Ngudade
wethu, naye ngokwakhe wathi, Ngumnakwethu? Le nto ndiyenze ngentliziyo
yam igqibelele, nangezandla zam zimsulwa.

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> Wathi uThixo kuye ngephupha, Nam ndiyazi
ukuba uyenze le nto ngentliziyo yakho igqibelele. Ndakunqanda nam, ukuba
ungoni kum; ngenxa yoko andikuvumelanga ukuba umchukumise.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> Ngoko mbuyise umfazi wale ndoda, ngokuba
ingumprofeti; yokuthandazela ukuba uphile; ukuba uthe akwambuyisa, yazi
ukuba uya kufa, wena nabo bonke onabo.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> Wavuka kwakusasa uAbhimeleki, wababiza
bonke abakhonzi bakhe, wawathetha onke la mazwi ezindlebeni zabo. Oyika
kakhulu loo madoda.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> UAbhimeleki wambiza uAbraham, wathi kuye,
Yintoni na le nto uyenzileyo kuthi? Ndikone ngantoni na, ukuba mna
nobukumkani bam isono esingaka? Wenze kum izenzo ezingezakwenziwa.

<span id="an_20:10">20:10</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki kuAbraham, Ubone
ntoni na, ukuba uyenze le nto?

<span id="an_20:11">20:11</span> Wathi uAbraham, Ndithe, akukho kanye
ukoyika uThixo kule ndawo; baya kundibulala ngenxa yomkam.

<span id="an_20:12">20:12</span> Okwenene ngudade wethu; yintombi
kabawo, kodwa akantombi kama, waba ngumkam ke.

<span id="an_20:13">20:13</span> Kwathi, uThixo akundiphambukisa,
andikhuphe endlwini kabawo, ndathi kuye, Nantsi inceba owondenzela yona:
ezindaweni zonke esofika kuzo, uze uthi ngam, Ngumnakwethu.

<span id="an_20:14">20:14</span> UAbhimeleki wathabatha impahla
emfutshane, neenkomo, nabakhonzi, nabakhonzazana, wanika uAbraham;
wambuyisela uSara umkakhe kuye.

<span id="an_20:15">20:15</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki, Nali ilizwe lam,
liphambi kwakho; hlala apho kulungileyo emehlweni akho.

<span id="an_20:16">20:16</span> Wathi kuSara, Yabona, umnakwenu
ndimnike iwaka lesilivere; yabona, sisigqubuthelo samehlo kuwe,
ngokusingisele kubo bonke aba nawe; naphakathi kwabo bonke ugwetyelwe.

<span id="an_20:17">20:17</span> Wathandaza uAbraham kuThixo; uThixo
wamphilisa uAbhimeleki, nomkakhe, nabakhonzazana bakhe, bazala.

<span id="an_20:18">20:18</span> Ngokuba uYehova ubezivingcile kanye,
zonke izizalo endlwini ka-Abhimeleki, ngenxa kaSara, umka-Abraham.

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> Ke kaloku uYehova wamvelela uSara
njengoko ebetshilo; uYehova wamenzela uSara njengoko abekuthethile.

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> Wamitha ke uSara, wamzalela uAbraham
unyana ekwaluphaleni kwakhe, ngexesha elimisiweyo abelithethile uThixo
kuye.

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> UAbraham wamthiya loo nyana wakho
abemzalelwe, awamzalayo uSara, igama elinguIsake.

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> UAbraham wamalusa uIsake unyana wakhe,
akuba ntsuku zisibhozo ezelwe, njengoko uThixo abemwisele umthetho.

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> UAbraham ube eminyaka ilikhulu,
ukuzalelwa kwakhe uIsake unyana wakhe.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> Wathi uSara, Undihlekisile uThixo; bonke
abakuvayo oku baya kuhleka nam.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> Wathi, Ngubani na obengatsholo kuAbraham
ukuthi, uSara wanyisa abantwana? Ngokuba ndimzalele unyana ekwaluphaleni
kwakhe.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> Wakhula umntwana, walunyulwa; uAbraham
wenza isidlo esikhulu mhlana walunyulwayo uIsake.

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> USara wambona unyana kaHagare
umYiputazana, awamzalela uAbraham, ehlekisa.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> Wathi kuAbraham, Mgxothe umkhonzazana
nonyana wakhe; kuba unyana walo mkhonzazana akayi kulidla ilifa ndawonye
nonyana wam uIsake.

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> Lalibi kunene elo zwi emehlweni
ka-Abraham ngenxa yonyana wakhe.

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> Wathi uThixo kuAbraham, Malingabi libi
emehlweni akho ngenxa yenkwenkwe, nangenxa yomkhonzazana wakho. Entweni
yonke ayithethileyo uSara kuwe, phulaphula izwi lakhe, ngokuba iya kuba
ngoIsake lo imbewu kuwe.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Kananjalo unyana womkhonzazana ndiya
kumenza uhlanga, ngokuba eyimbewu yakho.

<span id="an_21:14">21:14</span> Wavuka kusasa uAbraham, wathabatha
isonka nentsuba yamanzi, wanika uHagare, ebeka emagxeni akhe,
nenkwenkwe, wamndulula. Wemka ke, wandwendwela entlango yaseBher-shebha.

<span id="an_21:15">21:15</span> Aphela amanzi entsubeni, wayiphosa
inkwenkwe phantsi kwetyholo.

<span id="an_21:16">21:16</span> Waya wahlala phantsi malunga nayo,
umgama ongangowokutola ngotolo; kuba wathi, Mandingakuboni ukufa
kwenkwenkwe. Wahlala phantsi malunga nayo ke, waphakamisa izwi lakhe,
walila.

<span id="an_21:17">21:17</span> Waliva uThixo ilizwi lenkwenkwe.
Samemeza isithunywa sikaThixo kuHagare sisemazulwini, sathi kuye,
Unantoni na, Hagare? Musa ukoyika, ngokuba uThixo ulivile ilizwi
lenkwenkwe apho ikhona.

<span id="an_21:18">21:18</span> Suka ume, uyithabathe inkwenkwe,
uyibambe ngesandla; kuba ndiya kuyenza uhlanga olukhulu.

<span id="an_21:19">21:19</span> UThixo wawavula amehlo akhe, wabona
iqula lamanzi; waya wayizalisa intsuba ngamanzi, wayiseza inkwenkwe.

<span id="an_21:20">21:20</span> UThixo waba nenkwenkwe leyo; yakhula,
yahlala entlango, yaba yintoli yakukhula, yahlala entlango yaseParan;

<span id="an_21:21">21:21</span> unina wayithabathela umfazi ezweni
laseYiputa.

<span id="an_21:22">21:22</span> Kwathi ngelo xesha, wathetha
uAbhimeleki, noFikolo umthetheli womkhosi wakhe, kuAbraham, esithi,
UThixo unawe entweni yonke osukuba uyenza.

<span id="an_21:23">21:23</span> Ngoko ndifungele uThixo apha, ukuba
akuyi kundixokisa mna, noonyana bam, nenzalo yam; wothi ngokwenceba
endiyenzileyo kuwe, wenze kum, nakwilizwe ophambukele kulo.

<span id="an_21:24">21:24</span> Wathi uAbraham, Mna ndofunga.

<span id="an_21:25">21:25</span> UAbraham wamohlwaya uAbhimeleki ngenxa
yequla lamanzi elalihluthwe ngabakhonzi baka-Abhimeleki.

<span id="an_21:26">21:26</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki, Bendingazi ukuba
yenziwe ngubani na le nto; nawe ube ungandixelelanga; nam
bendingayivanga, ndiyiva namhla.

<span id="an_21:27">21:27</span> UAbraham wathabatha impahla emfutshane,
neenkomo, wanika uAbhimeleki, benza umnqophiso bobabini.

<span id="an_21:28">21:28</span> UAbraham wamisa amathokazi ezimvu
asixhenxe omhlambi, aba wodwa.

<span id="an_21:29">21:29</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki kuAbraham, Ayintoni
na la mathokazi ezimvu asixhenxe uwamisileyo odwa?

<span id="an_21:30">21:30</span> Wathi, La mathokazi ezimvu asixhenxe
wowathabatha esandleni sam, abe bubungqina bam bokuba ndilimbile eli
qula.

<span id="an_21:31">21:31</span> Ngenxa yoko kwathiwa loo ndawo
yiBher-shebha; ngokuba kulapho bafungayo bobabini.

<span id="an_21:32">21:32</span> Benza ke umnqophiso eBher-shebha.
Wesuka uAbhimeleki, noFikolo umthetheli womkhosi wakhe, babuyela ezweni
lamaFilisti.

<span id="an_21:33">21:33</span> UAbraham watyala umtamariske
eBher-shebha, walinqula khona igama likaYehova uThixo ongunaphakade.

<span id="an_21:34">21:34</span> UAbraham waye engumphambukeli ezweni
lamaFilisti imihla emininzi.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> Kwathi emveni kwezo nto, uThixo
wamvavanya uAbraham, wathi kuye, Abraham; wathi yena, Ndilapha.

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> Wathi, Khawuthabathe unyana wakho, emnye
kuwe, omthandayo, uIsake, uhambe uye ezweni laseMoriya, umnyuse khona
abe lidini elinyukayo phezu kwentaba endokuxelela yona.
