<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> Wavuka uAbraham kusasa, walibopha iesile
lakhe, wathabatha amabini kumadodana akhe, noIsake unyana wakhe, wacanda
iinkuni zedini elinyukayo, wesuka waya endaweni abemxelele yona uThixo.

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> Ngomhla wesithathu uAbraham wawaphakamisa
amehlo akhe, wayibona loo ndawo ikude.

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> Wathi uAbraham kumadodana akhe, Hlalani
nina apha ne-esile; mna nomfana lo soya phaya, sinqule, sibuye size
kuni.

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> Wazithabatha uAbraham iinkuni zedini
elinyukayo, wazibeka phezu koIsake unyana wakhe, waphatha umlilo
ngesandla, nesitshetshe, bahamba bobabini ndawonye.

<span id="an_22:7">22:7</span> Watsho uIsake kuAbraham uyise ukuthi,
Bawo. Wathi yena, Ndilapha, nyana wam. Wathi, Nangu umlilo neenkuni;
iphi na ke imvu yedini elinyukayo?

<span id="an_22:8">22:8</span> Wathi uAbraham, UThixo wozibonela imvu
yedini elinyukayo, nyana wam. Bahamba bobabini ndawonye.

<span id="an_22:9">22:9</span> Bafika endaweni abemxelele yona uThixo,
wakha khona uAbraham isibingelelo, wazicwangcisa iinkuni, wambopha
uIsake unyana wakhe, wambeka esibingelelweni phezu kweenkuni.

<span id="an_22:10">22:10</span> Wasolula uAbraham isandla sakhe,
wathabatha isitshetshe, ukuba amsike unyana wakhe.

<span id="an_22:11">22:11</span> Samemeza kuye isithunywa sikaYehova
sisemazulwini, sathi, Abraham, Abraham.

<span id="an_22:12">22:12</span> Wathi, Ndilapha. Sathi, Musa ukusisa
isandla sakho kumfana, musa ukumenza nto, kuba ndiyazi ngoku ukuba
uyamoyika uThixo; akunqabanga nonyana akho kum, emnye kuwe.

<span id="an_22:13">22:13</span> UAbraham waphakamisa amehlo akhe,
wakhangela, nantso inkunzi yegusha ngasemva, ibambeke ngeempondo
etyholweni; waya uAbraham, wayithabatha inkunzi yegusha, wayinyusa ukuba
ibe lidini elinyukayo esikhundleni sonyana wakhe.

<span id="an_22:14">22:14</span> UAbraham wathi igama laloo ndawo
linguYehova ozibonelayo ekuthiwa nanamhla, Entabeni abonakala kuyo
uYehova.

<span id="an_22:15">22:15</span> Samemeza isithunywa sikaYehova
kuAbraham okwesibini sisemazulwini sathi,

<span id="an_22:16">22:16</span> Ndizifungile, utsho uYehova, ngenxa
enokuba uyenzile le nto, akwanqaba nonyana wakho, emnye kuwe:

<span id="an_22:17">22:17</span> ukuba ndiya kukusikelela ndikusikelele;
ndiya kuyandisa ndiyandise imbewu yakho njengeenkwenkwezi zezulu,
nanjengentlabathi eselunxwemeni lolwandle; imbewu yakho ilidle ilifa
isango leentshaba zayo;

<span id="an_22:18">22:18</span> zisikelelwe ngembewu yakho zonke
untlanga zehlabathi, ngenxa enokuba uliphulaphule ilizwi lam.

<span id="an_22:19">22:19</span> Wabuyela uAbraham kumadodana akhe,
besuka baya bendawonye eBher-shebha, wahlala uAbraham eBher-shebha.

<span id="an_22:20">22:20</span> Kwathi emva kwezi zinto, kwaxelwa
kuAbraham kwathiwa, Yabona, uMilka ukwazele naye kuNahore, umninawa
wakho, abantwana:

<span id="an_22:21">22:21</span> u-Utse owamazibulo akhe, noBhuzi
umninawa wakhe, noKemuweli uyise ka-Aram,

<span id="an_22:22">22:22</span> noKesede, noHazo, noPildashe,
noYidelafu, noBhetuweli

<span id="an_22:23">22:23</span> (uBhetuweli ke wazala uRebheka); abo
bosibhozo uMilka wamzalela uNahore, umninawa ka-Abraham.

<span id="an_22:24">22:24</span> Ishweshwe lakhe, eligama linguRehuma,
lazala nalo uTebha, noGaham, noTahashe, noMahaka.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> Ke kaloku ukudla ubomi kukaSara kwaba
yiminyaka elikhulu elinamanci mabini aneminyaka esixhenxe; yiyo iminyaka
yokudla ubomi kukaSara.

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> Wafa ke uSara eKiriyati ka-Arbha,
eyiHebron, ezweni lakwaKanan. UAbraham waya kumbambazelela uSara
nokumlilela.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Wesuka uAbraham ebusweni bomfikazi lowo,

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> wathetha koonyana bakaHeti, esithi,
Ndingumphambukeli, ndilundwendwe kuni; ndinikeni ndibe nendawo yam
yokungcwaba phakathi kwenu, ukuze ndimngcwabe umfikazi, angabikho phambi
kwam.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> Bamphendula uAbraham oonyana bakaHeti,
bathi kuye, Sive, nkosi yam!

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> Usisikhulu sakwaThixo phakathi kwethu;
kwelona linyulekayo kumangcwaba ethu, mngcwabe umfikazi lowo; akukho
bani kuthi uya kwala nengcwaba lakhe, ukuba ungamngcwabi umfikazi lowo.

<span id="an_23:7">23:7</span> Wesuka uAbraham, waqubuda kubantu belizwe
elo, koonyana bakaHeti abo.

<span id="an_23:8">23:8</span> Wathetha nabo esithi, Ukuba
kusemphefumlweni wenu, ukuba ndimngcwabe umfikazi, angabikho phambi
kwam, ndiveni, nindibongozele kuEfron, unyana kaTsohare,

<span id="an_23:9">23:9</span> ukuba andinike umqolomba waseMakapela,
lowo anawo, osekupheleni kwentsimi yakhe, andinike wona ngemali
ezalisekileyo; ube yindawo yam yokungcwaba phakathi kwenu.

<span id="an_23:10">23:10</span> UEfron wayehleli phakathi koonyana
bakaHeti; uEfron umHeti wamphendula uAbraham ezindlebeni zoonyana
bakaHeti, zabo bonke abangenayo ngesango lomzi wakhe, esithi, Hayi,
nkosi yam, ndive!

<span id="an_23:11">23:11</span> Intsimi leyo ndiyakunika, nomqolomba
okuyo ndiyakunika; emehlweni oonyana babantu bakowethu ndiyakunika;
ngcwaba umfikizi loo.

<span id="an_23:12">23:12</span> Waqubuda uAbraham phambi kwabantu
belizwe elo.

<span id="an_23:13">23:13</span> Wathetha kuEfron ezindlebeni zabantu
belizwe elo, wathi, Wanga ungandiva; ndikunika imali ngentsimi;
yithabathe kum, ndingcwabe umfikazi khona.

<span id="an_23:14">23:14</span> UEfron wamphendula uAbraham, wathi
kuye,

<span id="an_23:15">23:15</span> Nkosi yam, ndive! Umhlaba ngoweeshekele
zesilivere ezimakhulu mane. Yintoni na loo nto phakathi kwam nawe?
Ngcwaba ke umfikazi lowo.

<span id="an_23:16">23:16</span> UAbraham wamphulaphula uEfron; uAbraham
wamlinganisela uEfron isilivere leyo, abethethe ngayo ezindlebeni
zoonyana bakaHeti, amakhulu omane eeshekele zesilivere evunywayo
ngumrhwebi.

<span id="an_23:17">23:17</span> Yaqiniseka ke intsimi kaEfron
eseMakapela ephambi kowakwaMamre, intsimi leyo nomqolomba okuyo, nemithi
yonke esentsimini, ekuyo yonke imilimandlela ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_23:18">23:18</span> Yaba yinzuzo kuAbraham emehlweni
oonyana bakaHeti, kubo bonke abangenayo ngesango lomzi wakhe.

<span id="an_23:19">23:19</span> Emveni koko uAbraham wamngcwaba uSara
umkakhe emqolombeni wentsimi yaseMakapela phambi kowakwaMamre,
kowaseHebron leyo, ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_23:20">23:20</span> Yaqiniseka ke intsimi leyo nomqolomba
okuyo kuAbraham, ukuze abe nendawo yakhe yokungcwaba, ngoonyana
bakaHeti.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> Ke kaloku uAbraham ebaluphele,
eselekhulile ebudaleni; uYehova waye emsikelele ke uAbraham ezintweni
zonke.

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> Wathi uAbraham kumkhonzi wakhe, oyena
mkhulu endlwini yakhe, obelawula zonke izinto abenazo, Khawubeke isandla
sakho phantsi kwethanga lam,

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> ndikufungise uYehova uThixo wamazulu,
uThixo wehlabathi, ukuba akuyi kumzekela unyana wam umfazi ezintombini
zamaKanan, endihleli phakathi kwawo;

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> ukuba woya ezweni lakowethu,
nakwelokuzalwa kwam, umzekele unyana wam uIsake umfazi.

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Wathi umkhonzi kuye, Hi ke, ayavuma
inkazana ukundilandela ukuza kweli lizwe, ndombuyisela na unyana wakho
kwelo zwe waphuma kulo wena?

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Wathi uAbraham kuye, Zilumkele
ungambuyiseli unyana wam khona.

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> UYehova, uThixo wamazulu,
owandithabathayo endlwini kabawo, ezweni lokuzalwa kwam, owathethayo
kum, owandifungelayo esithi, Imbewu yakho ndiya kuyinika eli lizwe, yena
wosithuma isithunywa sakhe phambi kwakho, umzekele umfazi unyana wam
khona.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> Ukuba ke inkazana leyo ithe ayavuma
ukukulandela, woba ukhululekile kwesi sifungo sam; kodwa uze
ungambuyiseli unyana wam khona.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> Wasibeka umkhonzi isandla sakhe
ngaphantsi kwethanga lika-Abraham inkosi yakhe, wamfungela loo nto.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> Umkhonzi wathabatha unkamela ezilishumi
kwunkamela zenkosi yakhe, wemka enezinto zonke ezilungileyo zenkosi
yakhe esandleni sakhe, wesuka waya kwa-Aram, phakathi kweMilambo, emzini
kaNahore.

<span id="an_24:11">24:11</span> Waziguqisa iinkamela ngaphandle komzi,
ngasequleni lamanzi, ngexa langokuhlwa, ngexa lokuphuma kwabakhi
bamanzi.

<span id="an_24:12">24:12</span> Wathi, Yehova, Thixo wenkosi yam
uAbraham, mawundithamsanqele namhla, uyenzele inkosi yam uAbraham
inceba.

<span id="an_24:13">24:13</span> Yabona, ndimi ngasemthonjeni wamanzi;
untombi zabantu balo mzi ziyaphuma, ziza kukha amanzi.

<span id="an_24:14">24:14</span> Ke intombi endothi kuyo, Khawuthobe
umphanda wakho ndisele; ize ithi, Sela, neenkamela zakho ndoziseza nazo:
mayibe yiyo oyimisele umkhonzi wakho uIsake; ndazi mna ngoko, ukuba
uyenzele inkosi yam inceba.

<span id="an_24:15">24:15</span> Kwathi, ingekagqibi ukuthetha, gqi
uRebheka esiza, lowo wazalwayo nguBhetuweli, unyana kaMilka, umkaNahore,
umninawa ka-Abraham, enomphanda wakhe egxalabeni lakhe.

<span id="an_24:16">24:16</span> Intombi leyo ibe intle kunene
imbonakalo, intombi eyintombi, engaziwanga ndoda; yehla, yeza
emthonjeni, yawuzalisa umphanda wayo, yenyuka.

<span id="an_24:17">24:17</span> Wagidima umkhonzi waya kuyikhawulela,
wathi, Ndiphe ndisele intwana yamanzi emphandeni wakho.

<span id="an_24:18">24:18</span> Yathi, Sela, nkosi yam. Yakhawuleza,
yawuhlisela esandleni umphanda wayo, yamseza.

<span id="an_24:19">24:19</span> Yakugqiba ukumseza, yathi, Neenkamela
zakho ndiya kuzikhelela, zide zigqibe ukusela.

<span id="an_24:20">24:20</span> Yakhawuleza, yawugalela umphanda wayo
emkhombeni wokuseza, yagidima yaya kukha futhi equleni, yazikhelela
zonke unkamela zakhe.

<span id="an_24:21">24:21</span> Indoda leyo yee nqa yiyo, ithe cwaka,
ukuze yazi ukuba uYehova uyiphumelelisile indlela yayo,
akayiphumelelisanga, kusini na.

<span id="an_24:22">24:22</span> Kwathi, iinkamela zigqibile ukusela,
indoda leyo yathabatha ijikazi lempumlo legolide, elisisiqingatha
seshekele ubunzima balo, nezacholo zozibini zokufakwa ezandleni,
eziziishekele ezilishumi zegolide ubunzima bazo; yathi, Uyintombi kabani
na wena?

<span id="an_24:23">24:23</span> Khawundixelele; kukho ndawo na yokulala
endlwini kayihlo?

<span id="an_24:24">24:24</span> Yathi kuye, Ndiyintombi kaBhetuweli,
unyana kaMika, awamzalela uNahore.

<span id="an_24:25">24:25</span> Yathi kuye, Sinawo umququ kwaneendiza
ezaneleyo, nendawo yokulala.

<span id="an_24:26">24:26</span> Yathoba indoda leyo, yaqubuda kuYehova.

<span id="an_24:27">24:27</span> Yathi, Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo
wenkosi yam uAbraham, ongayiyekelelanga inceba yakhe nenyaniso yakhe,
imke enkosini yam: uthe ndisendleleni, uYehova wandikhokelela endlwini
yabazalwana benkosi yam.

<span id="an_24:28">24:28</span> Yakhawuleza intombi leyo, yaxelela
indlu kanina ngokwala mazwi.

<span id="an_24:29">24:29</span> URebheka waye enomnakwabo, ogama
linguLabhan waya endodeni leyo ngaphandle emthonjeni.

<span id="an_24:30">24:30</span> Ke kwathi, akulibona ijikazi lempumlo,
nezacholo ezandleni zodade wabo, wathi, akuweva amazwi kaRebheka udade
wabo, esithi, Yenjenje indoda le ukuthetha kum: waya kuyo indoda, nantso
imi ngasezinkameleni ngasemthonjeni.

<span id="an_24:31">24:31</span> Wathi, Yiza, wena usikelelweyo
nguYehova; umeleni na ngaphandle? Mna ndiyilungisile indlu nendawo
yeenkamela.

<span id="an_24:32">24:32</span> Yangena indoda leyo endlwini,
wazikhulula iinkamela zayo; iinkamela wazinika umququ neendiza, wayinika
amanzi okuhlamba iinyawo zayo, neenyawo zamadoda abenayo.

<span id="an_24:33">24:33</span> Kwabekwa ukudla phambi kwayo. Yathi
yona, Andiyi kudla, ndide ndilithethe ilizwi lam. Wathi, Thetha.

<span id="an_24:34">24:34</span> Yathi, Ndingumkhonzi ka-Abraham.

<span id="an_24:35">24:35</span> UYehova uyisikelele kunene inkosi yam;
wayikhulisa, wayinika imphahla emfutshane, neenkomo, nesilivere,
negolide, nabakhonzi, nabakhonzazana, neenkamela, namaesile.

<span id="an_24:36">24:36</span> Ke uSara, umfazi wankosi yam,
wayizalela inkosi yam unyana, emveni kokuba iseyaluphele. Imnike zonke
izinto enazo.

<span id="an_24:37">24:37</span> Yandifungisa ke inkosi yam, isithi,
Unyana wam uze ungamzekeli umfazi ezintombini zamaKanan, endihleli
ezweni lawo mna.

<span id="an_24:38">24:38</span> Suka uye endlwini kabawo emizalwaneni
yakowethu, umzekele unyana wam umfazi.

<span id="an_24:39">24:39</span> Ndathi enkosini yam, Hi ke
ayandilandela inkazana leyo?

<span id="an_24:40">24:40</span> Yathi kum, UYehova, endihamba phambi
kwakhe, wosithuma isithunywa sakhe siye nawe, ayenze ibe nempumelelo
indlela yakho, umzekele unyana wam umfazi emizalwaneni yakowethu,
nasendlwini kabawo;

<span id="an_24:41">24:41</span> wandule ukuba msulwa esifungweni sam xa
ufikileyo emizalwaneni yakowethu; ukuba abathanga bakunike, woba msulwa
esifungweni sam.

<span id="an_24:42">24:42</span> Ndifikile ke namhlanje emthonjeni,
ndathi, Yehova, Thixo wenkosi yam uAbraham, ukuba kaloku uyenze
yanempumelelo indlela yam endihamba ngayo,

<span id="an_24:43">24:43</span> yabona, ndimi ngasemthonjeni wamanzi;
ke intombi ephuma isiza kukha, ndithi kuyo, Khawundiphe ndisele intwana
yamanzi emphandeni wakho;

<span id="an_24:44">24:44</span> ithi kum, Sela wena, neenkamela zakho
ndozikhelela nazo: mayibe yiyo engumfazi uYehova ammiseleyo unyana
wenkosi yam.

<span id="an_24:45">24:45</span> Ndingekagqibi mna ukuthetha
entliziyweni yam, gqi uRebheka, esiza enomphanda egxalabeni lakhe, wehla
waya emthonjeni, wakha; ndathi kuye, Khawundiphe ndisele.

<span id="an_24:46">24:46</span> Wakhawuleza, wawuhlisa umphanda wakhe
kuye, wathi, Sela, neenkamela zakho ndoziseza. Ndasela ke, waziseza
neenkamela.

<span id="an_24:47">24:47</span> Ndambuza ndathi, Uyintombi kabani na?
Wathi, Ndiyintombi kaBhetuweli, unyana kaNahore, lowo wamzalelwa
nguMilka. Ndamfaka ke ijikazi lempumlo ethatheni lakhe, nezacholo
ezandleni zakhe.

<span id="an_24:48">24:48</span> Ndathoba, ndamnqula uYehova, ndambonga
uYehova, uThixo wenkosi yam uAbraham, ondikhokeleyo endleleni
eyinyaniso, ukuba ndimzekele unyana wakhe intombi yomzalwana wenkosi
yam.

<span id="an_24:49">24:49</span> Ngoku ke, ukuba niyayenzela inceba
nenyaniso inkosi yam, ndixeleleni; ukuba anenjenjalo, ndixeleleni; ukuze
ndibheke ekunene, nokuba kusekhohlo.

<span id="an_24:50">24:50</span> Waphendula uLabhan noBhetuweli, bathi,
Le nto iphuma kuYehova; asinakuthetha nto kuwe, nokuba yembi nokuba
yelungileyo.

<span id="an_24:51">24:51</span> Nanko uRebheka phambi kwakho.
Mthabathe, uhambe, abe ngumfazi wonyana wenkosi yakho, njengoko
akuthethileyo uYehova.

<span id="an_24:52">24:52</span> Kwathi, akuweva umkhonzi ka-Abraham
amazwi abo, waqubuda emhlabeni kuYehova.

<span id="an_24:53">24:53</span> Umkhonzi wavelisa impahla yesilivere,
nempahla yegolide, nezambatho, wanika uRebheka; wanika umnakwabo nonina
izinto ezinconywayo.

<span id="an_24:54">24:54</span> Badla, basela, yena namadoda abenaye,
balala, bavuka kusasa, wathi, Ndindululeni ndiye enkosini yam.

<span id="an_24:55">24:55</span> Wathi umnakwabo nonina, Makhe ihlale
intombi nathi iintsuku nokuba zilishumi, ihambe ke emveni koko.

<span id="an_24:56">24:56</span> Wathi kubo, Musani ukundibambezela;
uYehova uyenze yanempumelelo indlela yam; ndindululeni ndiye enkosini
yam.

<span id="an_24:57">24:57</span> Bathi, Masiyibize intombi, sive
ngomlomo wayo.

<span id="an_24:58">24:58</span> Bambiza uRebheka, bathi kuye, Uya
kuhamba na nale ndoda? Wathi, Ndohamba.

<span id="an_24:59">24:59</span> Bamndulula ke uRebheka udade wabo,
nomanyisikazi wakhe, nomkhonzi ka-Abraham, namadoda abenaye.

<span id="an_24:60">24:60</span> Bamsikelela uRebheka, bathi kuye,
Ungudade wethu; yiba ngamawaka-waka, imbewu yakho ilidle ilifa isango
labo bayithiyayo.

<span id="an_24:61">24:61</span> Wesuka uRebheka nomthinjana wakhe,
bakhwela ezinkameleni, balandela emva kwendoda leyo. Umkhonzi
wamthabatha ke uRebheka, wemka.

<span id="an_24:62">24:62</span> Ke kaloku uIsake weza ngendlela evela
equleni likaPhila-ebonile; kuba ebemi ezweni lasezantsi.

<span id="an_24:63">24:63</span> Waphuma uIsake, waya kucamngca
entsimini, xa kuhlwayo; wawaphakamisa amehlo akhe, wabona nanzo
iinkamela zisiza.

<span id="an_24:64">24:64</span> URebheka wawaphakamisa amehlo akhe,
wambona uIsake, waziphosa phantsi, wehla enkameleni.

<span id="an_24:65">24:65</span> Wathi kumkhonzi, Ngubani na laa mfo
uhambayo entsimini, esiza kusikhawulela? Wathi umkhonzi, Yinkosi yam.
Wathabatha ke isigqubuthelo, wazigqubuthela.

<span id="an_24:66">24:66</span> Umkhonzi wamxelela uIsake izinto zonke
abezenzile.

<span id="an_24:67">24:67</span> UIsake wamsa ententeni kaSara unina,
wamzeka uRebheka, waba ngumkakhe; wamthanda. UIsake wathuthuzeleka ke
ngenxa yonina.

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> Wabuya uAbraham wazeka umfazi; igama
lakhe lalinguKetura.

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> Wamzalela uZimran, noYokeshan, noMedan,
noMidiyan, noIshibhaki, noShuwa.

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> UYokeshan wazala uShebha noDedan; oonyana
bakaDedan bebengama-Asiriya, namaLetushi, namaLehum.

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> Oonyana bakaMidiyan nguEfa, noEfere,
noEnoki, noAbhida, noElidaha. Bonke abo ngoonyana bakaKetura.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> UAbraham wazinika uIsake zonke izinto
abenazo.

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> Ke oonyana bamashweshwe, abenawo
uAbraham, wabanika izipho uAbraham; wabandulula, bemka kuIsake unyana
wakhe, esekho, basinga empumalanga, ezweni lasempumalanga.

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> Yiyo le imihla yeminyaka yokudla ubomi
kuka-Abraham awayidlayo; yiminyaka elikhulu elinamanci asixhenxe
aneminyaka emihlanu.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> UAbraham waphuma umphefumlo, wafa,
eyingwevu enkulu, aluphele, ephele ebudaleni; wahlanganiselwa
kwabakowabo.

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> OoIsake noIshmayeli, oonyana bakhe,
bamngcwaba emqolombeni waseMakapela, entsimini kaEfron unyana kaTsohare,
umHeti, phambi kowakwaMamre,

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> entsimini leyo wayithengayo uAbraham
kooyana bakaHeti. Ungcwatyelwe khona uAbraham, noSara umkakhe.

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> Kwathi, emveni kokufa kuka-Abraham,
uThixo wamsikelela uIsake unyana wakhe; uIsake wahlala ngasequleni
likaPhila-ebonile.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaIshmayeli, unyana
ka-Abraham, awathi uHagare umYiputazana, umkhonzazana kaSara, wamzalela
uAbraham.

<span id="an_25:13">25:13</span> Ngawo la amagama oonyana bakaIshmayeli,
ngamagama abo ngokwenzala yabo: owamazibulo kaIshmayeli nguNebhayoti,
noKedare, noAdebhele, noMibhesam,

<span id="an_25:14">25:14</span> noMishma, noDuma, noMasa;

<span id="an_25:15">25:15</span> uHadade, noTema, noYeture, noNafishi,
noKedema.

<span id="an_25:16">25:16</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaIshmayeli, ngawo
lawo amagama abo ngemizi yabo, nangeengqili zabo, izikulu ezilishumi
elinazibini ngokwezizwe zazo.

<span id="an_25:17">25:17</span> Yiyo le iminyaka yokudla ubomi
kukaIshmayeli: iminyaka elikhulu elinamanci mathathu, aneminyaka
esixhenxe. Waphuma umphefumlo, wafa, wahlanganiselwa kwabakowabo.

<span id="an_25:18">25:18</span> Bema bethabathela eHavila besa eShure,
phambi kweYiputa, ukusinga kwelakwa-Asiriya. Wazihlalisa ebusweni babo
bonke abazalwana bakhe.

<span id="an_25:19">25:19</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaIsake, unyana
ka-Abraham. UAbraham wazala uIsake.

<span id="an_25:20">25:20</span> UIsake waye eminyaka ingamashumi omane
ezelwe, ukuzeka kwakhe uRebheka, intombi kaBhetuweli, umAram
wasePadan-aram, udade boLabhan umAram, ukuba abe ngumkakhe.

<span id="an_25:21">25:21</span> Wathandaza uIsake kuYehova mayela
nomkakhe, ngokuba ebengazali. Wathandazeka uYehova, wamitha uRebheka
umkakhe.

<span id="an_25:22">25:22</span> Batyahalana abantwana embilini wakhe,
wathi, Ukuba unjalo, yini na ukuba ndibe nje? Waya kubuza kuYehova.

<span id="an_25:23">25:23</span> Wathi uYehova kuye, Zimbini iintlanga
esizalweni sakho; Kuya kwahluka zizwe zibini esiswini sakho, Esinye
somelele ngaphezu kwesinye; Omkhulu uya kukhonza omnci.

<span id="an_25:24">25:24</span> Yazaliseka ke imihla yakhe yokuzala,
nanko, ingamawele esizalweni sakhe.

<span id="an_25:25">25:25</span> Laphuma elokuqala lingqombela, lonke
liphela njengengubo exhonti; balithiya igama elinguEsawu.

<span id="an_25:26">25:26</span> Emveni koko kwaphuma umninawa walo,
isandla sakhe sibambe isithende sikaEsawu, wamthiya igama elinguYakobi.
UIsake wayeminyaka imashumi mathandathu ezelwe, ukuzalwa kwabo.

<span id="an_25:27">25:27</span> Akhula ke amakhwenkwe; uEsawu waba
lizingela, indoda yasendle; uYakobi waba yindoda egqibeleleyo, ihleli
ezintenteni.

<span id="an_25:28">25:28</span> UIsake wathanda uEsawu, ngokuba
inyamakazi ibimnandi emlonyeni wakhe; ke yena uRebheka wathanda uYakobi.

<span id="an_25:29">25:29</span> UYakobi wayepheke ukudla; wafika uEsawu
evela ezindle, etyhafile.

<span id="an_25:30">25:30</span> Wathi uEsawu kuYakobi, Khawundiphe
ndiginye kwinto engqombela, loo nto ingqombela, kuba ndityhafile; ngenxa
yoko kwathiwa igama lakhe nguEdom.

<span id="an_25:31">25:31</span> Wathi uYakobi, Thengisa namhlanje
ngobuzibulo bakho kum.

<span id="an_25:32">25:32</span> Wathi uEsawu, Yabona, ndiza kufa;
buyintoni na kum ubuzibulo?

<span id="an_25:33">25:33</span> Wathi uYakobi, Ndifungele namhlanje.
Wamfungela; wathengisa ke ngobuzibulo bakhe kuYakobi.

<span id="an_25:34">25:34</span> UYakobi wamnika uEsawu isonka
neentlumayo eziphekiweyo; wadla, wasela, wesuka wemka; wabudela ke
uEsawu ubuzibulo bakhe.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> Kwabakho indlala ezweni, ngaphandle
kweyokuqala indlala, eyayikho ngemihla ka-Abraham; waya uIsake
kuAbhimeleki, ukumkani wamaFilisti, eGerare.

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> UYehova wabonakala kuye, wathi, Musa
ukuhla uye eYiputa; ima ezweni endiya kukuxelela lona.

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> Phambukela kweli zwe. Ndoba nawe,
ndikusikelele; kuba ndiya kuwanika wena nembewu yakho onke la mazwe,
ndisimise isifungo endasifungayo kuAbraham uyihlo;

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> ndiyandise imbewu yakho njengeenkwenkwezi
zezulu, ndiyinike imbewu yakho onke la mazwe, zisikelelwe ngembewu yakho
zonke iintlanga zehlabathi;

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> ngenxa enokuba uAbraham waliphulaphulayo
izwi lam, wasigcina isigxina sam, nemithetho yam, nemimiselo yam,
nemiyalelo yam.

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> Wahlala uIsake eGerare.

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> Abuza amadoda aloo ndawo ngomkakhe.
Wathi, Ngudade wethu; kuba ebesoyika ukuthi, Ngumkam; hleze ambulale
amadoda ale ndawo ngenxa kaRebheka, ngokuba ebemhle imbonakalo.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> Kwathi, akubon’ ukuba ulibele umzuzu
khona, wondela uAbhimeleki, ukumkani wamaFilisti, ngefestile;
wakhangela, nanko, uIsake edlala noRebheka umkakhe.

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> UAbhimeleki wambiza uIsake, wathi,
Yabona, inene ngumkakho lo; ungathini na ukuthi, Ngudade wethu? Wathi
uIsake kuye, Bendisithi, hleze ndife ngenxa yakhe.

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki, Yini na ukuba wenze
le nto kuthi? Othile ebantwini ebengathi alale nomkakho, ube usizisele
ityala.

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> UAbhimeleki wawisela bonke abantu
umthetho wokuthi, Lowo uyichukumisayo le ndoda nomkayo wobulawa afe.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> UIsake wahlwayela kwelo zwe, wazuza
ngaloo mnyaka imilinganiso elikhulu; uYehova wamsikelela.

<span id="an_26:13">26:13</span> Yaba nkulu indoda leyo, yaya ikhula
ngokukhula, yada yaba nkulu kunene.

<span id="an_26:14">26:14</span> Yaba nemfuyo yempahla emfutshane,
nemfuyo yeenkomo, nabakhonzi abaninzi; ayimonela amaFilisti.

<span id="an_26:15">26:15</span> Onke amaqula, ababewambile abakhonzi
bakayise ngemihla ka-Abraham uyise, awavingca amaFilisti, awadibelela
ngomhlaba.

<span id="an_26:16">26:16</span> Wathi uAbhimeleki kuIsake, Mka kuthi,
ngokuba usuke waba namandla amakhulu kunathi.

<span id="an_26:17">26:17</span> UIsake wemka ke apho, wamisa iintente
esihlanjeni saseGerare, wahlala khona.

<span id="an_26:18">26:18</span> Wabuya uIsake wawamba amaqula amanzi,
ababewambile ngemihla ka-Abraham uyise, abevingciwe ngamaFilisti emveni
kokufa kuka-Abraham; wawabiza ngamagama abewabize ngawo uyise.

<span id="an_26:19">26:19</span> Bemba abakhonzi bakaIsake esihlanjeni
eso, bafumana khona iqula lamanzi aphilileyo.

<span id="an_26:20">26:20</span> Abalusi baseGerare babambana nabalusi
bakaIsake, besithi, Ngawethu la manzi; wathi igama lequla elo yiEseke,
kuba babezamana naye.

<span id="an_26:21">26:21</span> Bemba elinye iqula, babambana nangalo,
wathi igama lalo yiSitena.

<span id="an_26:22">26:22</span> Wesuka khona wemba elinye iqula;
ababambananga ngalo, wathi igama lalo yiRehobhoti. Wathi, Inene, ngoku
uYehova usenzele indawo ebanzi, ukuze siqhame ezweni apha.

<span id="an_26:23">26:23</span> Wenyuka wemka khona, waya eBher-shebha.

<span id="an_26:24">26:24</span> UYehova wabonakala kuye ngobo busuku,
wathi, NdinguThixo ka-Abraham uyihlo. Musa ukoyika, kuba ndinawe; ndiya
kukusikelela, ndiyandise imbewu yakho, ngenxa ka-Abraham, umkhonzi wam.

<span id="an_26:25">26:25</span> Wakha khona isibingelelo, wanqula igama
likaYehova, wayimisa khona intente yakhe; abakhonzi bakaIsake bemba
khona iqula.

<span id="an_26:26">26:26</span> Ke kaloku uAbhimeleki weza kuye ephuma
eGerare, noAhuzati, isihlobo sakhe, noFikolo, umthetheli womkhosi wakhe.

<span id="an_26:27">26:27</span> Wathi uIsake kubo, Nizeleni na kum,
nandithiyayo nje, nandindulula kuni?

<span id="an_26:28">26:28</span> Bathi, Sibone kakuhle ukuba uYehova
unawe; sathi, makubekho isifungo phakathi kwethu nawe, senze umnqophiso
nawe,

<span id="an_26:29">26:29</span> wokuba ungasenzeli bubi, njengokuba
singakusunduzanga, njengokuba sikwenzele okulungileyo kodwa, sakundulula
unoxolo; ngoku usikelelwe nguYehova.

<span id="an_26:30">26:30</span> Wabenzela isidlo, badla, basela. Bavuka
kusasa, bafungelana;

<span id="an_26:31">26:31</span> uIsake wabandulula, bemka kuye
benoxolo.

<span id="an_26:32">26:32</span> Kwathi ngaloo mini, bafika abakhonzi
bakaIsake, bamxelela indawo yequla ababelimbile, bathi kuye, Siwafumene
amanzi.

<span id="an_26:33">26:33</span> Wathi liyiShibha; ngenxa yoko igama
laloo mzi liyiBher-shebha unanamhla.

<span id="an_26:34">26:34</span> Ke kaloku uEsawu, akuba minyaka
imashumi mane ezelwe, wazeka umfazi, uYuditi intombi kaBheri, umHeti,
noBhasemati intombi kaElon, umHeti;

<span id="an_26:35">26:35</span> babacaphukisa ooIsake noRebheka.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> Kwathi, akwaluphala uIsake, amehlo akhe
enorhatyazo ukuba angaboni, wambiza uEsawu, unyana wakhe omkhulu, wathi
kuye, Nyana wam. Wathi yena kuye, Ndilapha.

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> Wathi, Khawubone, ndaluphele, andiyazi
imini yokufa kwam.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Khawuthabathe ngoku iintonga zakho,
umphongolo wakho, nesaphetha sakho, uye ezindle, undizingelele
inyamakazi;

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> undenzele ukudla okunencasa, njengoko
ndikuthandayo, ukuzise kum, ndidle; ukuze umphefumlo wam ukusikelele
ndingekafi.

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Ke kaloku uRebheka wayesiva ukuba uIsake
uthetha kuEsawu unyana wakhe. UEsawu waya kuzingela inyamakazi ezindle,
ukuba ayizise.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> URebheka wathetha kuYakobi, unyana wakhe,
wathi, Yabona, ndive uyihlo ethetha kuEsawu umkhuluwa wakho, esithi,

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> Ndizisele inyamakazi, undenzele ukudla
okunencasa, ndidle, ndikusikelele phambi koYehova ndingekafi.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> Ngoko ke, nyana wam, liphulaphule izwi
lam ngento endikuwisela umthetho ngayo.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Khawuhambe uye emhlambini, undithabathele
khona amatakane amabini ebhokhwe alungileyo, ndenzele uyihlo ukudla
okunencasa, njengoko akuthandayo;

<span id="an_27:10">27:10</span> ukuse kuyihlo, adle, ukuze akusikelele
engekafi.

<span id="an_27:11">27:11</span> Wathi uYakobi kuRebheka unina, Yabona,
uEsawu umkhuluwa wam yindoda exhonti, mna ndiyindoda egudileyo.

<span id="an_27:12">27:12</span> Mhlawumbi ubawo wondiva, ndibe
njengomgculeli emehlweni akhe, ndizizisele intshwabulelo, ndingaziziseli
intsikelelo.

<span id="an_27:13">27:13</span> Wathi unina kuye, Makube phezu kwam
ukushwatyulelwa kwakho, nyana wam; phulaphula izwi lam wena, uye
undithabathele.

<span id="an_27:14">27:14</span> Waya wawathabatha, wawazisa kunina;
unina wenza ukudla okunencasa, njengoko akuthandayo uyise.

<span id="an_27:15">27:15</span> URebheka wathabatha iingubo zikaEsawu,
unyana wakhe omkhulu, ezinqwenelekayo ezibe zikuye endlwini,
wamambathisa uYakobi unyana wakhe omnci.

<span id="an_27:16">27:16</span> Izintsu zamatakane lawo ebhokhwe
wambathisa ngazo izandla zakhe, nendawo egudileyo yentamo yakhe;

<span id="an_27:17">27:17</span> wabeka esandleni sikaYakobi unyana
wakhe ukudla okunencasa, nesonka abesenzile.

<span id="an_27:18">27:18</span> Weza kuyise, wathi, Bawo! Wathi yena,
Ndilapha. Ungubani na, nyana wam?

<span id="an_27:19">27:19</span> Wathi uYakobi kuyise, NdinguEsawu,
amazibulo akho; ndenze njengoko wathetha ngako kum; khawuvuke ke,
uhlale, udle inyamakazi yam, ukuze umphefumlo wakho undisikelele.

<span id="an_27:20">27:20</span> Wathi uIsake kunyana wakhe, Kutheni na
le nto ukhawulezileyo ukuyifumana nyana wam? Wathi yena, uYehova uThixo
wakho undithamsanqelisile.

<span id="an_27:21">27:21</span> Wathi uIsake kuYakobi, Khawusondele,
ndikuve, nyana wam, ukuba unguye na kanye unyana wam uEsawu, akunguye,
kusini na?

<span id="an_27:22">27:22</span> Wasondela uYakobi kuIsake uyise, wamva,
wathi, Ilizwi lona lilizwi likaYakobi, kodwa izandla zizandla zikaEsawu.

<span id="an_27:23">27:23</span> Akamnakana ke, kuba izandla zakhe zaba
noboya, njengezandla zikaEsawu umkhuluwa wakhe; wamsikelela ke.

<span id="an_27:24">27:24</span> Wathi, Wena lo ungunyana wam uEsawu na?
Wathi yena, Ndinguye.

<span id="an_27:25">27:25</span> Wathi, Sondeza kum ndidle inyamakazi
yonyana wam, ukuze umphefumlo wam ukusikelele. Wayisondeza kuye, wadla,
wamzisela newayini, wasela.

<span id="an_27:26">27:26</span> Wathi uyise uIsake kuye, Khawusondele
undange, nyana wam.

<span id="an_27:27">27:27</span> Wasondela, wamanga; waliva ivumba
leengubo zakhe, wamsikelela wathi, Yabona, ivumba lonyana wam
linjengevumba lelizwe elisikelelwe nguYehova.

<span id="an_27:28">27:28</span> Ngamana uThixo wakunika kuwo umbethe
wezulu, Nakuko ukuchuma komhlaba, Nentabalala yengqolowa, newayini
entsha;

<span id="an_27:29">27:29</span> Izizwe mazikukhonze, Izizwe ziqubude
kuwe. Yiba yinkosi kubazalwana bakho, Baqubude kuwe oonyana bakanyoko;
Uqalekisiwe okuqalekisayo, Usikelelwe okusikelelayo.

<span id="an_27:30">27:30</span> Kwathi, akubon’ ukuba ugqibile uIsake
ukumsikelela uYakobi ebusweni bukaIsake uyise, wangena uEsawu, umkhuluwa
wakhe, evela ekuzingeleni kwakhe.

<span id="an_27:31">27:31</span> Naye wenza ukudla okunencasa, wazisa
kuyise, wathi kuyise, Makavuke ubawo adle inyamakazi yonyana wakhe,
ukuze umphefumlo wakho undisikelele.

<span id="an_27:32">27:32</span> Wathi uIsake uyise kuye, Ungubani na?
Wathi, Ndingunyana wakho uEsawu, amazibulo akho.

<span id="an_27:33">27:33</span> UIsake wagubha ngokugubha okukhulu
kunene, wathi, Ngubani na lo phofu uzingele inyamakazi, wayizisa kum,
ndadla entweni yonke, ungekafiki wena, ndamsikelela? Wosikeleleka ke.

<span id="an_27:34">27:34</span> Akuweva uEsawu amazwi kayise, wakhala
ngesikhalo esikhulu, esikrakra kunene, wathi kuyise, Ndisikelele nam,
bawo.

<span id="an_27:35">27:35</span> Wathi yena, Kufike umninawa wakho
ngenkohliso, wayithabatha intsikelelo yakho.

<span id="an_27:36">27:36</span> Wathi, Kungokuba igama lakhe kusithiwa
nguYakobi na, le nto andigweqe ezi zihlandlo zozibini? Wathabatha
ubuzibulo bam; nanku ngoku, ethabathe nentsikelelo yam. Wathi,
Akundibekelanga ntsikelelo yam. Wathi, Akundibekelanga ntsikelelo na
mna?

<span id="an_27:37">27:37</span> Waphendula uIsake, wathi kuEsawu,
Yabona, ndimmisile waba yinkosi yakho, nabo bonke abazalwana bakhe
ndibanike yena, baba ngabakhonzi; ndamxhasa ngengqolowa nangewayini
entsha. Yintoni na kaloku endingakwenzela yona, nyana wam?

<span id="an_27:38">27:38</span> Wathi uEsawu kuyise, Inye na le
ntsikelelo unayo, bawo? Ndisikelele nam, bawo. Waliphakamisa uEsawu izwi
lakhe, walila.

<span id="an_27:39">27:39</span> Waphendula uIsake uyise, wathi kuye,
Yabona, ikhaya lakho liya kuba lee nokuchuma komhlaba, Lee nombethe
wezulu ovela phezulu.

<span id="an_27:40">27:40</span> Uya kuphila ngekrele lakho, umkhonze
umninawa wakho; Kuthi wakudlokova, Uyaphule idyokhwe yakhe, isuke
entanyeni yakho.

<span id="an_27:41">27:41</span> UEsawu wamzonda uYakobi ngenxa
yentsikelelo awamsikelela ngayo uyise; uEsawu wathi entliziyweni yakhe,
Iya kusondela imihla yesijwili sikabawo, ndimbulale ke uYakobi umninawa
wam.

<span id="an_27:42">27:42</span> Wawaxelelwa uRebheka amazwi kaEsawu,
unyana wakhe omkhulu, wathumela, wambiza uYakobi, unyana wakhe omnci,
wathi kuye, Yabona, uEsawu, umkhuluwa wakho, uzithuthuzela ngawe
ngokukubulala.

<span id="an_27:43">27:43</span> Ngoko ke, nyana wam, phulaphula izwi
lam, usuke ubalekele kuLabhan, umnakwethu, kwaHaran;

<span id="an_27:44">27:44</span> uhlale naye iintsuku ezithile, bude
bubuye ubushushu bomkhuluwa wakho,

<span id="an_27:45">27:45</span> ude umsindo womkhuluwa wakho ubuye
kuwe, ayilibale into oyenzileyo kuye; ndithumele ke, ndikuphuthume
khona. Yini na ukuba ndihluthwe nina nobabini ngamini-nye?

<span id="an_27:46">27:46</span> Ke kaloku uRebheka wathi kuIsake,
Ndikruqukile bubomi bam ngenxa yeentombi zakwaHeti. Ukuba uYakobi uthe
wazeka umfazi ezintombini zakwaHeti, ezinjengezi ntombi zeli lizwe, boba
yintoni na kum obu bomi?

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> UIsake wambiza uYakobi, wamsikelela,
wamwisela umthetho, wathi kuye, Uze ungazeki mfazi ezintombini
zakwaKanan.

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Suka uye ePadan-aram, endlwini
kaBhetuweli unyokokhulu, uzeke khona umfazi ezintombini zikaLabhan,
unyokolume.

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> Ngamana uThixo uSomandla wakusikelela,
wakuqhamisa, wakwandisa, ukuze ube sisikhungu sezizwe;

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> akunike intsikelelo ka-Abraham, wena
nembewu yakho ndawonye nawe, ukuze ulidle ilifa ilizwe lokuphambukela
kwakho, elo uThixo walinika uAbraham.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> UIsake wamndulula ke uYakobi; waya
ePadan-aram, kuLabhan unyana kaBhetuweli umAram, umnakwabo boRebheka,
unina booYakobi noEsawu.

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> UEsawu wabona ukuba uIsake umsikelele
uYakobi, wamndulula ukuba aye ePadan-aram, azeke khona umfazi;
ekumsikeleleni kwakhe wamwisela umthetho wokuthi, Uze ungazeki mfazi
ezintombini zakwaKanan;

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> noYakobi umphulaphule uyise nonina, waya
ePadan-aram.

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> Wabona uEsawu ukuba iintombi zakwaKanan
azifunwa nguIsake uyise;

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> wasuka waya uEsawu kuIshmayeli, wazeka
uMahalati, intombi kaIshmayeli, unyana ka-Abraham, udade boNebhayoti,
phezu kwabafazi bakhe, wangumkakhe.

<span id="an_28:10">28:10</span> Waphuma ke uYakobi eBher-shebha, waya
kwaHaran.

<span id="an_28:11">28:11</span> Wathi qatha ndaweni ithile, walala
khona, kuba belithshonile ilanga. Wathabatha kumatye aloo ndawo, wabeka
phantsi kwentloko yakhe, walala kuloo ndawo.

<span id="an_28:12">28:12</span> Waphupha ebona ileli imisiwe emhlabeni,
intloko yayo iye yafika emazulwini; nanzo izithunywa zikaThixo zinyuka,
zisihla ngayo;

<span id="an_28:13">28:13</span> nanko uYehova emi phezu kwayo, wathi,
NdinguYehova, uThixo ka-Abraham uyihlo, uThixo kaIsake. Ilizwe elo ulele
kulo, ndiya kulinika wena, nembewu yakho;

<span id="an_28:14">28:14</span> imbewu yakho ibe njengothuli lomhlaba,
uphangalale, usinge entshonalanga, nasempumalanga, nasentla, nasezantsi,
zisikelelwe ngawe nangembewu yakho zonke izizwe zehlabathi.

<span id="an_28:15">28:15</span> Yabona, ndinawe; ndiya kukugcina naphi
apho uya khona, ndikubuyisele kulo mhlaba; ngokuba andiyi kukushiya,
nidide ndikwenze oko ndikuthethileyo kuwe.

<span id="an_28:16">28:16</span> Wavuka uYakobi ebuthongweni bakhe,
wathi, Kunjenje ke, uYehova ukho kule ndawo, kanti mna bendingazi.

<span id="an_28:17">28:17</span> Woyika, wathi, Asikuko nokuba iyoyikeka
le ndawo; yindlu kaThixo le, ayinto yimbi; lisango lamazulu eli.

<span id="an_28:18">28:18</span> Wavuka uYakobi kwakusasa, walithabatha
ilitye abelibeke phantsi kwentloko yakhe, walimisa lasisimiso, wathulula
ioli phezu kwalo.

<span id="an_28:19">28:19</span> Wathi igama laloo ndawo yiBheteli,
nangona beliyiLuzi, igama laloo mzi ekuqaleni.

<span id="an_28:20">28:20</span> Wabhambathisa ngesibhambathiso uYakobi,
esithi, Ukuba uThixo uthe waba nam, wandigcina kuyo le ndlela
ndiyihambayo, wandinika isonka ndadla, neengubo ndambatha,

<span id="an_28:21">28:21</span> ndabuyela endlwini kabawo ndinoxolo:
uYehova woba nguThixo wam,

<span id="an_28:22">28:22</span> neli litye ndilimisileyo lasisimiso
loba yindlu kaThixo; neento zonke othe wandinika, ndokunika isishumi
sazo.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> Wesuka uYakobi, waya ezweni
labasempumalanga.

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> Wakhangela, wabona iqula ezweni, nantso
ikhona imihlambi emithathu yempahla emfutshane, ibuthile ngakulo; kuba
imihlambi yayisezwa kwelo qula. Kukho ilitye elikhulu emlonyeni wequla.

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> Yabe ihlanganiselwa khona yonke
imihlambi, baliqengqe ilitye, balisuse emlonyeni wequla, bayiseze
impahla emfutshane, balibuyisele ilitye elo emlonyeni wequla endaweni
yalo.

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> UYakobi wathi kubo, Bazalwana bam, nivela
phi na? Bathi bona, Sivela kwaHaran.

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Wathi kubo, Niyamazi na uLabhan, unyana
kaNahore? Bathi, Siyamazi.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> Wathi kubo, Usaphilile na? Bathi,
Usaphilile; nanku noRakeli, intombi yakhe, esiza nempahla emfutshane.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> Wathi, Yabonani, kusesemini enkulu,
asilixa lakuhlanganisa impahla; yisezeni impahla emfutshane, niye
kwalusa.

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> Bathi, Asinako, ide ihlanganiswe yonke
imihlambi, liqengqwe ilitye, lisuke emlonyeni wequla, siyiseze ke
impahla emfutshane.

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> Ke kaloku esathetha nabo, wafika uRakeli
nempahla emfutshane kayise; kuba ubeyalusa.

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> Kwathi, uYakobi akumbona uRakeli
intombi kaLabhan, uninalume, nempahla emfutshane kaLabhan uninalume,
wasondela uYakobi, waliqengqa ilitye lesuka emlonyeni wequla, wayiseza
impahla emfutshane kaLabhan uninalume.

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> UYakobi wamanga uRakeli, waliphakamisa
izwi lakhe, wasitsho isililo.

<span id="an_29:12">29:12</span> UYakobi wamxelela uRakeli ukuba
ungumzalwana kayise, nokuba ungunyana kaRebheka. Wagidima yena waxelela
uyise.

<span id="an_29:13">29:13</span> Kwathi, uLabhan akuluva udaba
lukaYakobi, unyana wodade wabo, wagidima waya kumkhawulela, wamwola,
wamanga, wamngenisa endlwini yakhe. Yena wambalisela uLabhan ngezo ndawo
zonke.

<span id="an_29:14">29:14</span> Wathi uLabhan kuye, Okunene ulithambo
lam, uyinyama yam. Wahlala naye inyanga iphela.

<span id="an_29:15">29:15</span> Wathi uLabhan kuYakobi, Kungokuba
ungumzalwana wam na, le nto undikhonza negelize? Ndixelele umvuzo wakho.

<span id="an_29:16">29:16</span> Ke kaloku uLabhan waye eneentombi
ezimbini; igama lenkulu lalinguLeya, igama lenci lalinguRakeli.

<span id="an_29:17">29:17</span> Ke uLeya wayenechaphothi; uRakeli
wayemhle isiqu, emhle imbonakalo.

<span id="an_29:18">29:18</span> UYakobi ubemthanda uRakeli, wathi,
Ndokukhonza iminyaka esixhenxe egenxa kaRakeli, intombi yakho enci.

<span id="an_29:19">29:19</span> Wathi uLabhan Kulungile ukuba ndimnike
wena, kunokuba ndimnike enye indoda; hlala nam ke.

<span id="an_29:20">29:20</span> UYakobi wakhonza ke iminyaka esixhenxe
ngenxa kaRakeli; yanga yimihla embalwa emehlweni akhe, ngenxa
yokumthanda kwakhe.

<span id="an_29:21">29:21</span> Wathi uYakobi kuLabhan, Ndinike umkam,
kuba izalisekile imihla yam, ukuba ndimngene.

<span id="an_29:22">29:22</span> Wawahlanganisa uLabhan onke amadoda
aloo ndawo, wenza umsitho.

<span id="an_29:23">29:23</span> Kwathi ngokuhlwa, wathabatha uLeya
intombi yakhe, wamngenisa kuye; wamngena ke yena.

<span id="an_29:24">29:24</span> Intombi yakhe uLeya, uLabhan wayinika
uZilipa, umkhonzazana wakhe, ukuba abe ngumkhonzazana wayo.

<span id="an_29:25">29:25</span> Kwathi kusasa, kwabonakala inguLeya.
Wathi kuLabhan, Yintoni na le nto uyenzileyo kum? Andikukhonze ngenxa
undikhohlise?

<span id="an_29:26">29:26</span> Wathi uLabhan, Akwenjiwa njalo kowethu,
ukuthi kwendiswe enci phambi kweyamazibulo.

<span id="an_29:27">29:27</span> Zalisa iveki yale, waleke eminye
iminyaka esixhenxe; sokunika naleyo ngenkonzo oya kundikhonza ngayo.

<span id="an_29:28">29:28</span> Wenjenjalo uYakobi, wayizalisa iveki
yale. Wamnika ke uRakeli intombi yakhe, yangumkakhe.

<span id="an_29:29">29:29</span> Intombi yakhe uRakeli, uLabhan wayinika
uBhiliha, umkhonzazana wakhe, ukuba abe ngumkhonzazana wayo.

<span id="an_29:30">29:30</span> Wamngena uRakeli, wamthanda uRakeli
phezu koLeya. Wakhonza ke, waleka eminye iminyaka esixhenxe.

<span id="an_29:31">29:31</span> UYehova wabona ukuba uLeya uthiyiwe,
wasivula isizalo sakhe; ke uRakeli ebengazali.

<span id="an_29:32">29:32</span> Wamitha ke uLeya wazala unyana,
wamthiya igama elinguRubhen, ngokuba ebesithi, UYehova uzibonile
iintsizi zam; inene, iya kundithanda ngoku indoda yam.

<span id="an_29:33">29:33</span> Wabuya wamitha, wazala unyana; wathi,
UYehova uvile ukuba ndithiyiwe, wandinika nalo; wamthiya igama
elinguSimon.

<span id="an_29:34">29:34</span> Wabuya wamitha, wazala unyana; wathi,
Khona ngoku, iya kunamathela kum indoda yam, kuba ndiyizalele oonyana
abathathu; ngenxa yoko wamthiya igama elinguLevi.

<span id="an_29:35">29:35</span> Wabuya wamitha, wazala unyana; wathi,
Okwesi sihlandlo ndiya kumdumisa uYehova; ngenxa yonke wamthiya igama
elinguYuda. Wanqamka ukuzala.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> Ke kaloku akubona uRakeli ukuba
akamzaleli mntwana uYakobi, uRakeli wammonela udade wabo, wathi
kuYakobi, Ndinike abantwana; ukuba akundiniki, ndofa.

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> Wavutha umsindo kaYakobi ngakuRakeli,
wathi, Ndisesikhundleni sikaThixo na, okuvimbileyo isiqhamo sesizalo?

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> Wathi yena, Nantso impelesi yam uBhiliha;
yingene, izalele emadolweni am, ndakheke nam ngayo.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> Wamnika ke uBhiliha, umkhonzazana wakhe,
ukuba abe ngumfazi; uYakobi wamngena.

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> Wamitha uBhiliha, wamzalela uYakobi
unyana.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> Wathi uRhakeli, UThixo undigwebele,
kananjalo uliphulaphule izwi lam, wandinika unyana; ngenxa yoko wamthiya
igama elinguDan.

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> Wabuya wamitha uBhiliha, umkhonzazana
kaRakeli, wamzalela uYakobi unyana wesibini.

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> Wathi uRakeli, Ndizamene nodade wethu
imizamo kaThixo, kananjalo ndeyisa; wamthiya igama elinguNafetali.

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> Ke kaloku wabona uLeya ukuba unqamkile
ukuzala, wathabatha uZilipa, umkhonzazana wakhe, wamnika uYakobi ukuba
abe ngumfazi.

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> UZilipa, umkhonzazana kaLeya, wamzalela
uYakobi unyana.

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> Wathi uLeya, Lithamsanqa! Wamthiya
igama elinguGadi.

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> UZilipa, umkhonzazana kaLeya, wamzalela
uYakobi unyana wesibini.

<span id="an_30:13">30:13</span> Wathi uLeya, Ndiva uyolo, ngokuba
iintombi ziya kuthi ndinoyolo. Wamthiya igama elinguAshere.

<span id="an_30:14">30:14</span> Waya uRubhen ngemihla yovuno
lwengqolowa, wafumana amathuma endle, wawazisa kuLeya unina. Wathi
uRakeli kuLeya, Khawundiphe emathumeni onyana wakho lawo.

<span id="an_30:15">30:15</span> Wathi kuye, Yinto encinane na
ukuyithabatha indoda yam, ubuye uthabathe namathuma onyana wam? Wathi
uRakeli, Ngako oko mayilale nawe ngobu busuku, ngenxa yamathuma onyana
wakho lawo.

<span id="an_30:16">30:16</span> Wafika uYakobi evela ezindle ngokuhlwa,
waphuma uLeya esiya kumkhawulela, wathi, Uze undingene, kuba
ndikuqeshile ngamathuma onyana wam. Walala ke naye ngobo busuku.

<span id="an_30:17">30:17</span> UThixo wamphulaphula uLeya; wamitha,
wamzalela uYakobi unyana wesihlanu.

<span id="an_30:18">30:18</span> Wathi uLeya, UThixo undinikile umvuzo
wam, ngenxa yokuba indoda yam ndiyinike umkhonzazana wam.

<span id="an_30:19">30:19</span> Wamthiya igama elinguIsakare. Wabuya
wamitha uLeya, wamzalela uYakobi unyana wesithandathu.

<span id="an_30:20">30:20</span> Wathi uLeya, UThixo undiphe isipho
esilungileyo; okwesi sihlandlo indoda yam iya kuhlala nam, kuba
ndiyizalele oonyana abathandathu. Wamthiya igama elinguZebhulon.

<span id="an_30:21">30:21</span> Emveni koko wazala intombi, wayithiya
igama elinguDina.

<span id="an_30:22">30:22</span> Ke kaloku uThixo wamkhumbula uRakeli
uThixo wamphulaphula, wasivula isizalo sakhe.

<span id="an_30:23">30:23</span> Wamitha, wazala unyana, wathi, UThixo
ukususile ukungcikivwa kwam.

<span id="an_30:24">30:24</span> Wamthiya igama elinguYosefu, wathi,
UYehova makongezelele omnye unyana.

<span id="an_30:25">30:25</span> Kwathi, xa uRakeli ebemzele uYosefu,
wathi uYakobi kuLabhan, Ndindulule ndiye endaweni yakowethu, ezweni
lakowethu.

<span id="an_30:26">30:26</span> Ndinike abafazi bam nabantwana bam,
endikukhonze ngenxa yabo, ndihambe; kuba wena uyayazi inkonzo yam
endikukhonze ngayo.

<span id="an_30:27">30:27</span> Wathi uLabhan kuye, Ukuba kaloku
ndibabalwe nguwe, hlala; ndihlabe ukuthi uYehova undisikelele ngenxa
yakho.

<span id="an_30:28">30:28</span> Wathi, Ndimisele kakuhle umvuzo wakho
ondifaneleyo, ndikunike.

<span id="an_30:29">30:29</span> Wathi kuye, Uyalwazi nawe uhlobo
lokukukhonza kwam, nohlobo lokuhlala kwempahla yakho nam.

<span id="an_30:30">30:30</span> Kuba obunayo ndingekafiki yabe imbalwa,
ngoku izazekile yaninzi; uYehova ukusikelele apho unyawo lwam luthe
lwanyathela; kaloku ndiya kuyisebenzela nini na mna eyam indlu?

<span id="an_30:31">30:31</span> Wathi, Ndikunike ntoni na? Wathi
uYakobi, Akuyi kundinika nento le; ukuba uthe wandenzela le ndawo,
ndobuya ndiyaluse impahla yakho emfutshane, ndiyigcine.

<span id="an_30:32">30:32</span> Ndiya kucanda phakathi kwayo yonke
impahla yakho emfutshane namhlanje, ndihambe ndikhetha kuyo zonke
iingusha ezinala, nezirhwexu, neegusha zonke ezimnyama phakathi
kwamatakane, nazo zonke ezirhwexu nezinala phakathi kweebhokhwe, zibe
ngumvuzo wam;

<span id="an_30:33">30:33</span> bundingqinele ke ubulungisa bam
ngexesha elizayo, xa uthe weza kumvuzo wam ophambi kwakho: zonke
ezingenala, nezingerhwexu phakathi kweebhokhwe, nezingemnyama phakathi
kweegusha, zoba zezibiweyo ezo, xa zithe zakum.

<span id="an_30:34">30:34</span> Wathi uLabhan, Yabona, makube
ngokwelizwi lakho elo.

<span id="an_30:35">30:35</span> Wazikhetha ngaloo mhla iinkunzi
zeebhokhwe ezinemizila, nezirhwexu, nazo zonke iimazi zeebhokwe
ezinakazi, nezirhwexukazi, zonke ezinobumhlophe, nazo zonke ezimnyama
phakathi kwamatakane, wazinikela esandleni soonyana bakhe.

<span id="an_30:36">30:36</span> Wamisa uhambo lweemini ezintathu
phakathi kwabo noYakobi; uYakobi walusa eseleyo ke impahla emfutshane
kaLabhan.

<span id="an_30:37">30:37</span> Ke kaloku uYakobi wathabatha iintonga
zompopulari omhlophe ezimanzi, nezom-amangile, nezompleyini, wachuba
iindawo ezimhlophe kuzo, exwebula buvele ubumhlophe obusezintongeni ezo.

<span id="an_30:38">30:38</span> Wazimisa iintonga abezichubile
emijelweni, emikhumbini yamanzi, apho impahla emfutshane ibiza kusela
khona, phambi kwempahla emfutshane, ukuba iphathane xa iza kusela.

<span id="an_30:39">30:39</span> Yaphathana ke impahla emfutshane phambi
kweentonga ezo, yazala impahla emfutshane enemizila, nerhwexu, nenala.

<span id="an_30:40">30:40</span> Wawahlula uYakobi amatakane lawo,
wabukhangelisa ubuso bempahla emfutshane malunga nenemizila, nemnyama,
yonke empahleni emfutshane kaLabhan; wayibeka yodwa eyakhe imihlambi,
akayibeka empahleni emfutshane kaLabhan.

<span id="an_30:41">30:41</span> Kwathi, xa iphathanayo eyomeleleyo
empahleni emfutshane, uYakobi wazibeka iintonga phambi kwempahla
emfutshane emijelweni, ukuze iphathane phakathi kweentonga.

<span id="an_30:42">30:42</span> Xa ityhafileyo impahla emfutshane,
akazibekanga; yathi ke etyhafileyo yaba yekaLabhan, eyomeleleyo yaba
yekaYakobi.

<span id="an_30:43">30:43</span> Yanda indoda leyo kakhulu kunene, Yanda
indoda leyo kakhulu kunene, yaba nempahla emfutshane enizi,
nabakhonzazana, nabakhonzi, neenkamela, namaesile.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> Ke kaloku waweva amazwi oonyana
bakaLabhan, besithi, UYakobi uzithabathile zonke izinto abenazo ubawo;
ubenze ngezinto zikabawo obu butyebi bakhe bonke.

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Wabubona uYakobi ubuso bukaLabhan, nabo
bungenjengezolo nezolo elinye kuye.

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> UYehova wathi kuYakobi, Buyela ezweni
likayihlo, kwelokuzalwa kwakho; ndoba nawe.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> UYakobi wathumela, wabiza uRakeli noLeya,
ukuba beze endle empahleni yakhe emfutshane.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> Wathi kubo, Ndiyabubona ubuso bukayihlo,
ukuba abunjengezolo nezolo elinye kum; ke uThixo kabawo ubenam.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> Niyazi nina, ukuba uyihlo ndimkhonze
ngamandla am onke;

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> ke uyihlo undidephisele, wawuguqula
umvuzo wam kalishumi; kodwa uThixo akamvumelanga ukuba andenze into
embi.

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> Xa athe, Enala yoba ngumvuzo wakho isuke
yonke impahla emfutshane yazala enala; xa athe, Enemizila yoba ngumvuzo
wakho, isuke yonke impahla emfutshane yazala enemizila.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> Wayihlutha uThixo imfuyo kayihlo,
wandinika.

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Kwathi, ngexesha lokuphathana kwempahla
emfutshane, ndawaphakamisa amehlo am, ndabona ephupheni, nanzo iinkunzi
ezikhwelayo empahleni emfutshane zinemizila, zinala, zinomchokose.

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> Sathi isithunywa sikaThixo kum
ephupheni, Yakobi; ndathi, Ndilapha.

<span id="an_31:12">31:12</span> Sathi, Khawuphakamise amehlo akho,
ubone; zonke iinkunzi ezikhwelayo empahleni emfutshane zinemizila,
zinala, zinomchokose; kuba ndizibonile zonke izinto azenzayo uLabhan
kuwe.

<span id="an_31:13">31:13</span> NdinguThixo waseBheteli, apho
wasithambisa khona isimiso, apho wabhambathisa ngesibhambathiso kum.
Suka ngoko, uphume kweli lizwe, ubuyele ezweni lokuzalwa kwakho.

<span id="an_31:14">31:14</span> Baphendula uRakeli noLeya, bathi kuye,
Sisenasabelo nalifa lini na endlwini kabawo?

<span id="an_31:15">31:15</span> Akuthiwa singabasemzini kuye yini na?
Kuba uthengise ngathi, wamana eyidla nemali yethu.

<span id="an_31:16">31:16</span> Ngoko kuze bonke ubutyebi abuhluthileyo
uThixo kubawo, bube bobethu, noboonyana bethu, kaloku ke konke
akuthethileyo uThixo kuwe kwenze.

<span id="an_31:17">31:17</span> Wesuka uYakobi wabakhwelisa oonyana
bakhe, nabafazi bakhe, ezinkameleni.

<span id="an_31:18">31:18</span> Waqhuba yonke impahla yakhe, nayo yonke
ingqwebo yakhe abeyiqwebile, impahla abeyifuyile, abeyiqwebile
ePadan-aram, ukuze aye kuIsake uyise ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_31:19">31:19</span> ULabhan ubeye kucheba impahla yakhe
emfutshane; uRakeli wayiba imilonde-khaya ebiyekayise.

<span id="an_31:20">31:20</span> UYakobi wamlalanisa uLabhan umAram,
ekubeni engamxelelanga ukuba uyabaleka.

<span id="an_31:21">31:21</span> Wabaleke ke, yena nako konke abenako;
wesuka, wawuwela uMlambo, wabubhekisa ubuso bakhe entabeni yaseGiliyadi.

<span id="an_31:22">31:22</span> Waxelelwa uLabhan ngomhla wesithathu
ukuba uYakobi ubalekile.

<span id="an_31:23">31:23</span> Wathabatha abazalwana bakhe,
wamphuthuma uhambo lwemihla esixhenxe; bafumanana entabeni yaseGiliyadi.

<span id="an_31:24">31:24</span> Weza uThixo kuLabhan umAram ephupheni
ebusuku, wathi kuye, Zilumkele, ungathethi nto kuYakobi, nokuba
yelungileyo nokuba yembi.

<span id="an_31:25">31:25</span> ULabhan wafika kuYakobi. Ke kaloku
uYakobi ubeyigxumekile intente yakhe entabeni; uLabhan nabazalwana bakhe
bagxumeka entabeni yaseGiliyadi.

<span id="an_31:26">31:26</span> Wathi uLabhan kuYakobi, Wenza ntoni na
ukundilalanisa, uziqhube iintombi zam njengabathinjwe ngekrele?

<span id="an_31:27">31:27</span> Yini na ukuba uzimele, ubaleke,
undilalanise, ungandixeleli? Ngendiba ndokundulule ngemivuyo,
nangeengoma, nangengqongqo, nangohadi.

<span id="an_31:28">31:28</span> Yini na ukuba ungandivumeli ndibange
oonyana bam neentombi zam? Kaloku wenze ngobudenge.

<span id="an_31:29">31:29</span> Kusemandleni esandla sam ukunenza
ububi; ke uThixo kayihlo uthethe nam phezolo, esithi, Zilumkele,
ungathethi nto noYakobi, nokuba yelungileyo nokuba yembi.

<span id="an_31:30">31:30</span> Ngoku umkileyo nje, ngokuba
walangazelela kakhulu indlu kayihlo, uzibeleni na zona izithixo zam?

<span id="an_31:31">31:31</span> Waphendula uYakobi wathi kuLabhan,
Bendisoyika, kuba bendisithi, Hleze uzixhakamfule kum iintombi zakho.

<span id="an_31:32">31:32</span> Osukuba uzifumana kuye izithixo zakho,
makangadli bomi. Phambi kwabazalwana bethu fanisa into yakho enam,
uyithabathe. Wayengazi uYakobi ukuba uRakeli uzibile.

<span id="an_31:33">31:33</span> Wangena uLabhan ententeni kaYakobi,
nasententeni kaLeya, nasententeni yeempelesi zombini; akazifumana.
Waphuma ententeni kaLeya, wangena ententeni kaRakeli.

<span id="an_31:34">31:34</span> Ke kaloku uRakeli ebeyithabathile
imilonde-khaya, wayifaka phakathi kwesali yenkamela, wahlala phezu
kwayo. ULabhan wayiphuthaphutha yonke intente, akayifumana.

<span id="an_31:35">31:35</span> Wathi kuyise, Mawungabi namsindo, nkosi
yam, kuba ndingenako ukusuka phambi kwakho, ngokuba ndihleli phezu
kwengca. Wagquthagqutha, akayifumana imilonde-khaya.

<span id="an_31:36">31:36</span> Wavutha umsindo kaYakobi, wabambana
noLabhan. Waphendula uYakobi, wathi kuLabhan, Luyintoni na ukreqo lwam,
siyintoni na isono sam, ukuba undisukele ngokushushu nje?

<span id="an_31:37">31:37</span> Uziphuthaphuthile zonke iimpahla zam;
ufumene ntoni na yazo zonke iimpahla zendlu yakho? Yibeke apha phambi
kwabazalwana bam, nabazalwana bakho, bahlule phakathi kwethu sobabini.

<span id="an_31:38">31:38</span> Le minyaka imashumi mabini bendinawe;
iimazi zakho zeegusha, neemazi zebhokhwe aziphunzanga, neenkunzi
zempahla yakho emfutshane andizidlanga.

<span id="an_31:39">31:39</span> Into eqwengiweyo andiyizisanga kuwe,
ndayimisela ngokwam; wayibiza esandleni sam nokuba ibiwe emini, nokuba
ibiwe ebusuku.

<span id="an_31:40">31:40</span> Emini ndadliwa bubushushu, ebusuku
yingqele; ubuthongo bam bemka emehlweni am.

<span id="an_31:41">31:41</span> Kwaba njalo kum le minyaka imashumi
mabini endlwini yakho; ndakukhonza iminyaka elishumi elinamine ngenxa
yeentombi zakho zombini, iminyaka emithandathu ngenxa yempahla yakho
emfuthsane; uwuguqule kalishumi umvuzo wam.

<span id="an_31:42">31:42</span> Koko uThixo kabawo, uThixo ka-Abraham,
Ohlonelwa nguIsake, waba nam, inene unge undindulule ndilambatha ngoku.
UThixo uzibonile iintsizi zam nokuxelenga kwezandla zam, wakohlwaya
phezolo.

<span id="an_31:43">31:43</span> ULabhan waphendula wathi kuYakobi,
Iintombi ziintombi zam, oonyana ngoonyana bam, impahla emfutshane
yimpahla yam, neento zonke ozibonayo zezam. Ndinakwenza ntoni na namhla
ezintombini zam ezi, nakoonyana azo ezibazeleyo?

<span id="an_31:44">31:44</span> Yiza ngoku, senze umnqophiso, mna nawe,
ube lingqina phakathi kwam nawe.

<span id="an_31:45">31:45</span> UYakobi wathabatha ilitye,
waliphakamisa lasisimiso.

<span id="an_31:46">31:46</span> Wathi uYakobi kubazalwana bakhe,
Cholani amatye. Bathabatha amatye, benza imfumba, badla khona phezu
kwaloo mfumba.

<span id="an_31:47">31:47</span> Wathi ukuyibiza uLabhan
yiYegarsahaduta, uYakobi wathi ukuyibiza yiGaledi.

<span id="an_31:48">31:48</span> Wathi uLabhan, Le mfumba ilingqina
phakathi kwam nawe namhla, ngenxa yoko yathiywa igama eliyiGaledi;

<span id="an_31:49">31:49</span> neliyiMizpa, ngokuba wathi Makobonisele
uYehova phakathi kwam nawe, sakuba sisithelene;

<span id="an_31:50">31:50</span> ukuba uthe wazicinezela iintombi zam,
nokuba uthe wazeka abafazi phezu kweentombi zam, akukho bani unathi.
Khangela, uThixo ulingqina phakathi kwam nawe.

<span id="an_31:51">31:51</span> ULabhan wathi kuYakobi, Yabona le
mfumba, yabona esi simiso ndisiphakamisileyo phakathi kwam nawe;

<span id="an_31:52">31:52</span> ingqina yile mfumba, ingqina sesi
simiso, ukuba andiyi kugqitha mna kule mfumba ndiye kuwe, ukuba akuyi
kugqitha wena kule mfumba nakwesi simiso uze kum, senzane ububi.

<span id="an_31:53">31:53</span> UThixo ka-Abraham, uThixo kaNahore,
uThixo woyise wabo, makagwebe phakathi kwethu. UYakobi wafunga Ohlomelwa
nguyise uIsake.

<span id="an_31:54">31:54</span> UYakobi wabingelela umbingelelo
entabeni apho, wabiza abazalwana bakhe, ukuba badle isonka. Badla ke
isonka, balala entabeni apho.

<span id="an_31:55">31:55</span> Wavuka uLabhan kusasa, wabanga oonyana
bakhe, neentombi zakhe, wabasikelela; wemka ke uLabhan, wabuyela
ekhayeni lakhe.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> UYakobi wahamba ngendlela yakhe;
zaqubisana naye izithunywa zikaThixo.

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Wathi uYakobi akuzibona, Ngumkhosi
kaThixo lo; wathi igama laloo ndawo yiMahanayim.

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> Ke kaloku uYakobi wathuma abathunywa
phambi kwakhe, baya kuEsawu, umkhuluwa wakhe, ezweni lakwaSehire,
emhlabeni wakwaEdom.

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> Wabawisela umthetho esithi, Nothi
ukuthetha enkosini yam uEsawu, Utsho umkhonzi wakho uYakobi ukuthi,
Bendingumphambukeli kuLabhan, ndalibala khona kwada kwangoku;

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> ndineenkomo namaesile, nempahla
emfutshane, nabakhonzi, nabakhonzazana; ndithumele ukuxelela inkosi yam,
ukuze indibabale.

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> Abathunywa babuyela kuYakobi besithi,
Sifikile kumkhuluwa wakho uEsawu, naye uyeza kukukhawulela, enamadoda
angamakhulu omane.

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> Woyika kunene uYakobi, wabandezeleka,
wabahlula abantu ababenaye, nempahla emfutshane, neenkomo, neenkamela;
iimfuduka zambini.

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Wathi, Ukuba uEsawu uthe wafika kwenye
imfuduka, wayichitha, yosinda imfuduka eseleyo.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> Wathi uYakobi, Thixo kabawo uAbraham,
Thixo kabawo uIsake, Yehova, uthe kum, Buyela ezweni lakowenu,
kwelokuzalwa kwakho; ndokuphatha kakuhle.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> Andiyilingene inceba yonke, nenyaniso
yonke oyenzileyo kumkhonzi wakho; kuba ndayiwela le Yordan, ndinentonga
yam yodwa, kodwa ngoku ndimfuduka mbini.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> Khawundihlangule esandleni somkhuluwa
wam, esandleni sikaEsawu; ngokuba ndiyamoyika, hleze afike andibulale,
unina ndawonye nabantwana.

<span id="an_32:12">32:12</span> Wawuthe wena, Inene, ndiya kukuphatha
kakuhle, imbewu yakho nidyenze ibe njengentlabathi yolwandle,
engenakubalwa ngenxa yobuninzi.

<span id="an_32:13">32:13</span> Ke kaloku yena walala khona ngobo
busuku. Wathabatha entweni esifike kuyo isandla sakhe, yangumnikelo
kuEsawu, umkhuluwa wakhe;

<span id="an_32:14">32:14</span> iimazi zeebhokhwe ezimakhulu mabini,
neenkunzi zeebhokhwe ezimashumi mabini, neemazi neegusha ezimakhulu
mabini, neenkunzi zeegusha ezimashumi mabini,

<span id="an_32:15">32:15</span> neenkamela ezisengwayo ezimashumi
mathathu, ezinamathole azo, neemazi zeenkomo ezimashumi mane, neenkunzi
zeenkomo ezilishumi, neemazi zamaesile ezimashumi mabini, namaxhamxwa
alishumi.

<span id="an_32:16">32:16</span> Wazinikela esandleni sabakhonzi bakhe,
walowo umhlambi wawodwa. Wathi kubakhonzi bakhe, Welani phambi kwam,
nibeke isithuba phakathi komhlambi nomhlambi.

<span id="an_32:17">32:17</span> Owokuqala wamwisela umthetho, wathi, Xa
athe uEsawu umkhuluwa wam waqubisana nawe, wakubuza ngokuthi, Ungokabani
na? Uya phi na? Zezikabani na ezi zinto ziphambi kwakho?

<span id="an_32:18">32:18</span> wothi, Zezomkhonzi wakho uYakobi:
ngumnikelo othunyelwe inkosi yam uEsawu; nanku ke naye ngasemva kwethu.

<span id="an_32:19">32:19</span> Nowesibini, nowesithathu wamwisela
umthetho, nabo bonke ababeyilandela imihlambi, esithi, Nothetha ngolo
hlobo kuEsawu, nakufumanana naye.

<span id="an_32:20">32:20</span> Kananjalo nothi, Nanko mkhonzi wakho
uYakobi engasemva kwethu. Kuba wathi, Mandibucamagushe ubuso bakhe
ngomnikelo ohamba phambi kwam, emveni koko ndibubone ubuso bakhe;
mhlawumbi wondibuka.

<span id="an_32:21">32:21</span> Umnikelo lowo wahamba phambi kwakhe; ke
yena walala ngobo busuku emfudukeni.

<span id="an_32:22">32:22</span> Wavuka ngobo busuku, wathabatha abafazi
bakhe bobabini, nabakhonzanzana bakhe bobabini noonyana bakhe abalishumi
elinamnye, waliwela izibuko le Yabhoki.

<span id="an_32:23">32:23</span> Wabathabatha ke, wabaweza emfuleni
lowo, waziweza zonke izinto abenazo.

<span id="an_32:24">32:24</span> UYakobi wasala yedwa; kwazamana indoda
naye kwada kwathi qhiphu ukusa.

<span id="an_32:25">32:25</span> Yakubona ukuba ayimeyisi, yachukumisa
usikrobana womlenze wakhe, wancothuka usikrobana womlenze kaYakobi
ngokuzamana nayo.

<span id="an_32:26">32:26</span> Yathi, Ndindulule ndihambe, kuba
kuyasa. Wathi yena, Andiyi kukundulula umke, ukuba akuthanga
undisikelele.

<span id="an_32:27">32:27</span> Yathi kuye, Ngubani na igama lakho?
Wathi, NdinguYakobi.

<span id="an_32:28">32:28</span> Yathi, Igama lakho akusayi kuba sathiwa
nguYakobi; kuya kuthiwa unguSirayeli, ngokuba ulwe noThixo nabantu,
weyisa.

<span id="an_32:29">32:29</span> Wabuza uYakobi wathi, Ndixelele igama
lakho. Yathi, Ulibuzelani na igama lam? Yamsikelela khona.

<span id="an_32:30">32:30</span> UYakobi wayithiya loo ndawo igama
eliyiPeniyeli; kuba wathi, Ndibonene noThixo, wahlangulwa umphefumlo
wam.

<span id="an_32:31">32:31</span> Lathi chapha ilanga, akudlula
ePeniweli, ejingxela ngomlenze wakhe.

<span id="an_32:32">32:32</span> Ngenxa yoko oonyana bakaSirayeli
abawudli umsipha kasikrobana ophezu kosikrobana womlenze, nanamhla;
ngokuba yachukumisa usikrobana womlenze kaYakobi emsipheni kasikrobana.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> Wawaphakamisa uYakobi amehlo akhe,
wabona, nanko uEsawu esiza, enamadoda amakhulu mane. Abantwana
wabahlulahlula, baba kuLeya, nakuRakeli, nakubakhonzazana bobabini.

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> Wababeka abakhonzazana nabantwana babo
phambili, uLeya nabantwana bakhe emva kwabo, uRakeli noYosefu emva
kanye.

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> Ke yena wagqithela phambi kwabo, waqubuda
emhlabeni kasixhenxe, wada wasondela kumkhuluwa wakhe.

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> Wagidima uEsawu emkhawulela, wamwola,
wawa entanyeni yakhe, wamanga; basitsho isililo.

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> Wawaphakamisa amehlo akhe, wababona
abafazi nabantwana, wathi, Ngoobani na aba banawe? Wathi yena,
Ngabantwana, athe uThixo wabababala umkhonzi wakho.

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> Basondela abakhonzazana, bona nabantwana
babo, baqubuda.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> Wasondela noLeya nabantwana bakhe,
baqubuda; emveni koko wasondela uYosefu noRakeli, baqubuda.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> Wathi, Iyintoni na yonke le mfuduka yakho
endiqubisene nayo? Wathi, Yeyokuba ndibabalwe emehlweni enkosi yam.

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> Wathi uEsawu, Ndanele, mninawa; makube
kokwakho okwakho.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> Wathi uYakobi, Hayi, makungabi njalo.
Ukuba kaloku ndibabalwe emehlweni akho, thabatha umnikelo wam lo
esandleni sam; kuba ngenxa yoko ndibubonile ubuso bakho, ndanga ndibona
ubuso bukaThixo, ndalikholo kuwe.

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> Khawuyithabathe intsikelelo yam
ezisiweyo kuwe, ngokuba uThixo undibabale, kuba ndineento zonke.
Wamjoka, wayithabatha.

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> Wathi uEsawu, Masinduluke, sihambe;
ndohamba phambi kwakho.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> Wathi kuye, Inkosi yam iyazi ukuba
abantwana bathambile, nempahla emfutshane, neenkomo ezanyisayo ziphezu
kwam; yothi iqhutywe kakhulu imini enye, ife yonke impahla emfutshane.

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Inkosi yam mayikhe igqithele phambi
komkhonzi wayo ndihambise kuhle ngokuhamba kwempahla ephambi kwam,
nangokuhamba kwabantwana, ndide ndifike enkosini yam kwaSehire.

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> Wathi uEsawu, Makhe ndiyishiye kuwe
inxenye yabantu abanam. Wathi yena, Ngani na? Mandibabalwe emehlweni
enkosi yam.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> Wabuya ngaloo mhla uEsawu ngendlela
yakhe, esiya kwaSehire.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> UYakobi wanduluka, waya eSukoti,
wazakhela indlu, iinkomo zakhe wazibiyela iintlantsi; ngenxa yoko
kwathiwa igama laloo ndawo yiSukoti.

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> Wafika uYakobi enoxolo emzini kaShekem,
osezweni lakwaKanan, ekuveleni kwakhe ePadan-aram; wamisa iintente
phambi komzi.

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> Wathenga isiziba somhlaba, apho
wayitwabulula khona intente yakhe, esandleni soonyana bakaHamore
usoShekem, ngekhulu lemali.

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Wamisa khona isibingelelo, wathi
ukusithiya nguThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> Ke kaloku uDina, intombi kaLeya, leyo
wayizalela uYakobi, waphuma waya kubona iintombi zelo zwe.

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> UShekem, unyana kaHamore umHivi, isikhulu
selizwe, sambona, samthabatha, salala naye, samona.

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Umphefumlo wakhe wanamathela kuDina
intombi kaYakobi; wayithanda intombi leyo, wathetha kakuhle nentombi.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> UShekem wathetha kuHamore uyise wathi,
Ndizekele le ntombi ibe ngumfazi.

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> Weva uYakobi ukuba umenze inqambi uDina,
intombi yakhe. Ke oonyana bakhe baye besempahleni yakhe endle; wathi tu
ke uYakobi, bada bafika.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> Waphuma uHamore, uyise kaShekem, eza
kuthetha noYakobi.

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> Bafika oonyana akaYakobi evela kwalusa.
Bakuyiva le nto aba bahlungu amadoda lawo, avutha kunene ngumsindo,
ngokuba wenza ubudenge kwaSirayeli ngokulala nentombi kaYakobi, into
leyo engeyakwenziwa.

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Wathetha uHamore nabo, esithi, uShekem,
unyana wam, umphefumlo wakhe uthene nca nentombi yakowenu; khanimnike
ibe ngumkakhe;

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> nendiselane nathi, nisinike iintombi
zenu, nizeke iintombi zethu;

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> nahlale nathi, ilizwe libe phambi
kwenu; hlalani nirhwebe kulo, niqiniseke ukuma kulo.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> Wathi uShekem kuyise wayo,
nakubanakwayo, Mandibabalwe emehlweni enu, nento eniyithethayo kum
ndoninika.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> Yandisani kunene ikhazi phezu kwam,
nesipho; ndoninika njengoko nithethayo kum; ndinikeni ke intombi leyo
ibe ngumfazi.

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> Oonyana bakaYakobi babaphendla ooShekem
noHamore uyise ngenkohliso, bathetha nabo, ngokuba ebemenze inqambi
uDina, udade wabo.

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> Bathi kubo, Asinakuyenza le nto, yokuba
udade wethu simnike indoda engalukanga; kuba loo nto ibe ingaba
sisingcikivo kuthi.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> Sovumelana nani ngale ndawo yodwa,
ukuba nithe naba njengathi, ngokuthi yaluke kuni yonke into eyindoda.

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> Soninika ke iintombi zethu, sizeke
iintombi zenu, sihlale nani, sibe bantu banye.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> Ukuba nithe anasiphulaphula ngokuthi
naluke, soyithabatha intombi yethu, simke.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> Alunga amazwi abo emehlweni kaHamore,
nasemehlweni kaShekem, unyana kaHamore.

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> Akalibala umfana ukuyenza loo nto, uba
ubethabathekile yintombi kaYakobi; ubezukile yena ngaphezu kwayo yonke
indlu kayise.

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> Weza uHamore noShekem, unyana wakhe,
esangweni lomzi wabo, bathetha kumadoda omzi, bathi,

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> La madoda ayavana nathi; makahlale
ezweni apha, arhwebe kulo; ilizwe eli, yabonani, libanzi ngeenxa zombini
phambi kwawo; sozizeka iintombi zawo zibe ngabafazi, siwanike iintombi
zethu.

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> Ke ovumelana nathi ngale ndawo yodwa
amadoda lawo, ukuhlala nathi, sibe bantu banye, yakwaluka kuthi yonke
into eyinoda, njengokuba alukile wona.

<span id="an_34:23">34:23</span> Imfuyo yawo, nengqwebo yawo, nawo onke
amaqegu awo, akasayi kuba ngawethu na? Siya kuthi kodwa sivumelane nawo,
ukuba ahlale nathi.

<span id="an_34:24">34:24</span> Bamphulaphula ke uHamore noShekem
unyana wakhe, bonke abaphuma ngesango omzi wabo. Yaluswa yonke into
eyindoda, bonke abaphuma ngesango lomzi wabo.

<span id="an_34:25">34:25</span> Kwathi ngomhla wesithathu, bakuba
buhlungu, besuka oonyana ababini bakaYakobi, uSimon noLevi, abanakwabo
boDina, bathabatha walowo ikrele lakhe, bawufikela loo mzi
ungakhumbulele nto, babulala yonke into eyindoda.

<span id="an_34:26">34:26</span> Babulala noHamore, noShekem unyana
wakhe, ngohlangothi lwekrele, bamthabatha uDina endlwini kaShekem,
baphuma.

<span id="an_34:27">34:27</span> Oonyana bakaYakobi babafikela
ababuleweyo, bawuphanga umzi, ngokuba bebemenze inqambi udade wabo.

<span id="an_34:28">34:28</span> Impahla yabo emfutshane, neenkomo zabo,
namaesile abo, neento zonke ezibe ziphakathi komzi, nezibe zisendle,
bazithabatha;

<span id="an_34:29">34:29</span> nobutyebi babo bonke, nabantwana babo
bonke, nabafazi babo, babathimba, baphanga neento zonke ebe zisendlwini.

<span id="an_34:30">34:30</span> UYakobi wathi kuSimon nakuLevi,
Nindihlisele ishwangusha, ukuze ndinuke phakathi kwabemi belizwe eli,
phakathi kwamaKanan, naphakathi kwamaPerizi; ndibantu bambalwa nje mna,
baya kundihlanganyela, bandibulale, nditshatyalaliswe mna, nendlu yam.

<span id="an_34:31">34:31</span> Bathi bona, udade wethu angaphathwa
njengehenyukazi yini na?

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> Ke kaloku wathi uThixo kuYakobi, Suka uye
eBheteli, uhlale khona, wenze khona isibingelelo kuThixo, owabonakalayo
kuwe ekubalekeni kwakho ebusweni bukaEsawu, umkhuluwa wakho.

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> Wathi ke uYakobi kwindlu yakhe, nakubo
bonke ababenaye, Susani izithixo zasemzini eziphakathi kwenu, nina
nizihlambulule, ninxibe ngubo zimbi;

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> sisuke, sinyuke siye eBheteli, senze
khona isibingelelo kuThixo, owandiphendula ngomhla wokubandezeleka kwam,
obe nam endleleni endandihamba ngayo.

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> Bazinika uYakobi zonke izithixo zasemzini
ebezisesandleni sabo, namajikazi abesezindlebeni zabo; uYakobi wazimbela
phantsi komoki obungakwaShekem.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> Banduluka; uqhiphulo-mbilini ngoThixo
lwaba phezu kwemizi ngeenxa zonke kubo, ayabasukela oonyana bakaYakobi.

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> Wafika uYakobi eLuzi, esezweni
lakwaKanan, ekwayiBheteli; yena nabo bonke abantu ababenaye.

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> Wakha khona isibingelelo, wathi loo ndawo
ukuyibiza nguThixo waseBheteli; kuba kulapho uThixo wazityhilayo kuye,
ekubalekeni kwakhe ebusweni bomkhuluwa wakhe.

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> Wafa uDebhora, umanyisikazi kaRebheka,
angcwatywa ngasezantsi kweBheteli, phantsi kom-oki; kwathiwa igama layo
nguMoki wokuLila.

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> UThixo wabuya wabonakala kuYakobi
ekuveleni kwakhe ePadan-aram, wamsikelela.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> Wathi uThixo kuye, Igama lakho
nguYakobi; akuyi kuba sathiwa igama lakho nguYakobi, kuya kuthiwa igama
lakho nguSirayeli; wamthiya ke igama elinguSirayeli.

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> Wathi uThixo kuye, NdinguThixo
uSomandla. Qhama, wande; uhlanga nesikhungu seentlanga siya kuvela kuwe,
nookumkani baphume esinqeni sakho.

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Ilizwe endalinika uAbraham noIsake
ndilinike wena; ndilinike imbewu yakho emva kwakho ilizwe elo.

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> Wenyuka uThixo, wemka kuye kuloo ndawo
abethethe naye kuyo.

<span id="an_35:14">35:14</span> UYakobi wamisa isimiso kuloo ndawo
abethethe naye kuyo, isimiso samatye; wathulula phezu kwaso umnikelo
othululwayo, wagalela neoli phezu kwaso.

<span id="an_35:15">35:15</span> UYakobi wathi igama laloo ndawo, uThixo
abethethe naye kuyo, yiBheteli.

<span id="an_35:16">35:16</span> Banduluka eBheteli. Kwathi,
kusemganyana ukuba kufikwe e-Efrata, wazala uRakeli, kwaba nzima ukuzala
kwakhe.

<span id="an_35:17">35:17</span> Kwathi, kwakuba nzima ukuzala kwakhe,
wathi umzalisikazi kuye, Musa ukoyika, kuba nalo ngunyana wakho.

<span id="an_35:18">35:18</span> Kwathi ekupumeni komphefumlo wakhe,
kuba wafayo, wathi nguBhenoni igama lakhe; ke yena uyise wathi
nguBhenjamin.

<span id="an_35:19">35:19</span> Wafa ke uRakeli, wangcwatyelwa
endleleni yase-Efrata eyiBhetelehem.

<span id="an_35:20">35:20</span> UYakobi wamisa isimiso phezu kwengcwaba
lakhe; sisimiso sengcwaba likaRakeli nanamhla.

<span id="an_35:21">35:21</span> USirayeli wayincothula intente yakhe,
waya wayitwabulula ngaphaya kweMigdoli-edere.

<span id="an_35:22">35:22</span> Kwathi, ekuhlaleni kukaSirayeli kwelo
zwe, waya uRubhen, wamlala uBhiliha, ishweshwe likayise; weva ke
uSirayeli. Oonyana bakaYakobi babelishumi elinababini.

<span id="an_35:23">35:23</span> Oonyana bakaLeya nguRubhen, owamazibulo
kuYakobi, noSimon, noLevi, noYuda, noIsakare, noZebhulon.

<span id="an_35:24">35:24</span> Oonyana bakaRakeli nguYosefu
noBhenjamin.

<span id="an_35:25">35:25</span> Oonyana bakaBhiliha, umkhonzazana
kaRakeli, nguDan noNafetali.

<span id="an_35:26">35:26</span> Oonyana bakaZilipa, umkhonzazana
kaLeya, nguGadi noAshere. Ngabo abo oonyana bakaYakobi, awabazalelwa
ePadan-aram.

<span id="an_35:27">35:27</span> UYakobi waya kuIsake uyise kwaMamre,
eKiriyati ka-Arbha, eHebron, apho babengabaphambukeli khona uAbraham
noIsake.

<span id="an_35:28">35:28</span> Imihla kaIsake yaba yiminyaka elikhulu
elinamanci asibhozo.

<span id="an_35:29">35:29</span> UIsake waphuma umphefumlo, wafa,
wahlanganiselwa kwabakowabo, aluphele, ephelele ebudaleni. Bamngcwaba
ooEsawu noYakobi, oonyana bakhe.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaEsawu, onguEdom.

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> UEsawu wabazeka abafazi bakhe ezintombini
zakwaKanan: uAda, intombi kaElon umHeti, oAholibhama, intombi ka-Ana,
intombi kaTsibheyon umHivi;

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> wazeka noBhasemati, intombi kaIshmayeli,
udade boNebhayoti.

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> UAda wamzalela uEsawu uElifazi:
uBhasemati wazala uRehuweli.

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> UAholibhama wazala uYehushe, noYalam,
noKora. Ngabo abo oonyana bakaEsawu, awabazalelwayo ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> UEsawu wabathabatha abafazi bakhe,
noonyana bakhe, neentombi zakhe, nabendlu yakhe yonke, nemfuyo yakhe,
namaqegu akhe onke, nengqwebo yakhe yonke abeyiqebile ezweni lakwaKanan,
waya kwelinye ilizwe, emka ngenxa kaYakobi umninawa wakhe.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Kuba ingqwebo yabo ibininzi, ukuze
bangabi nakuhlala ndawonye; nelizwe lokuphambukela kwabo libe
lingenakubathwala, ngenxa yemfuyo yabo.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Wahlala uEsawu entabeni yakwaSehire.
UEsawu ke lowo nguEdom.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaEsawu, uyise
wamaEdom, entabeni yakwaSehire.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> Ngawo la ke amagama oonyana bakaEsawu:
nguElifazi, unyana ka-Ada, umkaEsawu; nguRehuweli, unyana kaBhasemati,
umkaEsawu.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> Oonyana bakaElifazi nguTeman, no-Omare,
noTsefo, noGatam, noKenazi.

<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> UTimna ebelishweshwe likaElifazi,
unyana kaEsawu, wamzalela uElifazi uAmaleki;

<span id="an_36:13">36:13</span> ngabo abo oonyana baka-Ada, umkaEsawu.
Ngabo aba oonyana bakaRehuweli: uNahati, noZera, noShama, noMiza. Ngabo
abo oonyana bakaBhasemati, umkaEsawu.

<span id="an_36:14">36:14</span> Ngabo aba oonyana baka-Aholibhama,
intombi ka-Ana, intombi kaTsibheyon, umkaEsawu: wamzalela uEsawu
uYehushe, noYalam, noKora.

<span id="an_36:15">36:15</span> Zizo ezi izikhulu zoonyana bakaEsawu:
oonyana bakaElifazi, owamazibulo kuEsawu, sisikhulu esinguTeman,
isikhulu esingeOmare, isikhulu esinguTsefo, isikhulu esinguKenazi,
isikhulu esinguKora, isikhulu esinguGatam, isikhulu esinguAmaleki.

<span id="an_36:16">36:16</span> Zizo ezo izikhulu zakwaElifazi ezweni
lakwaEdom; ngabo abo oonyana baka-Ada.

<span id="an_36:17">36:17</span> Ngabo aba oonyana bakaRehuweli, unyana
kaEsawu: sisikhulu esinguNahati, isikhulu esinguZera, isikhulu
esinguShama, isikhulu esinguMiza; zizo ezo izikhulu zakwaRehuweli ezweni
lakwaEdom; ngabo abo oonyana bakaBhasemati, umkaEsawu.

<span id="an_36:18">36:18</span> Ngabo aba oonyana baka-Aholibhama,
umkaEsawu: sisikhulu esinguYehushe, isikhulu esinguYalam, isikhulu
esinguKora; zizo ezo izikhulu zakwa-Aholibhama, intombi ka-Ana,
umkaEsawu.

<span id="an_36:19">36:19</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaEsawu, zizo ezo
izikhulu; nguEdom ke lowo.

<span id="an_36:20">36:20</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaSehire umHori,
ababemi kwelo zwe: uLotan, noShobhali,

<span id="an_36:21">36:21</span> noTsibheyon, oAna, noDishon noEtsere,
noDishan; zizo ezo izikhulu zamaHori, oonyana bakaSehire, ezweni
lakwaEdom.

<span id="an_36:22">36:22</span> Oonyana bakaLotan babengamaHori,
noHemam; udade boLotan nguTimna.

<span id="an_36:23">36:23</span> Ngabo aba oonyana bakaShobhali:
nguAlevan, noManahati, noEbhali, noShefo, no-Onam.

<span id="an_36:24">36:24</span> Ngabo aba oonyana bakaTsibheyon: nguAya
noAna. Ngulo Ana wayifumanayo imithombo eshushu entlango, esalusa
amaesile kaTsibheyon uyise.

<span id="an_36:25">36:25</span> Ngabo aba oonyana baka-Ana: NguDishon;
uAholibhama wayeyintombi ka-Ana: nguDishon; uAholibhama wayeyintombi
ka-Ana.

<span id="an_36:26">36:26</span> Ngabo aba oonyana bakaDishon:
nguHemdan, noEshbhan, noItran, noKeran.

<span id="an_36:27">36:27</span> Ngabo aba oonyana bakaEtsere:

<span id="an_36:28">36:28</span> nguBhilehan, noZavan, noAkan. Ngabo aba
oonyana bakaDishan: ngu-Utse noAran.

<span id="an_36:29">36:29</span> Zizo ezi izikhulu zamaHori: isikhulu
esinguLotan, isikhulu esinguShobhali, isikhulu esinguTsibheyon, isikhulu
esinguAna, isikhulu esinguDishon,

<span id="an_36:30">36:30</span> isikhulu esinguEtsere, isikhulu
esinguDishan; zizo ezo izikhulu zamaHori, ngokwezikhulu zabo ezweni
lakwaSehire.

<span id="an_36:31">36:31</span> Ngabo aba ookumkani ababelawula ezweni
lakwaEdom, kungekabikho kumkani unobukumkani kubo oonyana bakaSirayeli:

<span id="an_36:32">36:32</span> uBhela, unyana kaBhehore, walawula
kwaEdom; igama lomzi wakhe yiDinabha.

<span id="an_36:33">36:33</span> Wafa uBhela, wathi uYobhabhi, unyana
kaZera waseBhotsera, walawula esikhundleni sakhe.

<span id="an_36:34">36:34</span> Wafa uYobhabhi, wathi uHusham,
wasezweni lamaTeman, walawula esikhundleni sakhe.

<span id="an_36:35">36:35</span> Wafa uHusham, wathi uHadadi, unyana
kaBhedadi, owawatshabalalisayo amaMidiyan emhlabeni wamaMowabhi,
walawula esikhundleni sakhe; igama lomzi wakhe yiAviti.

<span id="an_36:36">36:36</span> Wafa uHadadi, wathi uSamla waseMasereka
walawula esikhundleni sakhe.

<span id="an_36:37">36:37</span> Wafa uSamla, wathi uSawule,
waseRehobhoti yoMlambo, walawula esikhundleni sakhe.

<span id="an_36:38">36:38</span> Wafa uSawule, wathi uBhahali-hanan,
unyana ka-Akebhore, walawula esikhundleni sakhe.

<span id="an_36:39">36:39</span> Wafa uBhahali-hanan, unyana
ka-Akebhore, wathi uHadare walawula esikhundleni sakhe; igama lomzi
wakhe yiPawu; igama lomkakhe nguMehetabheli, intombi kaMatrede, intombi
kaMezahabhi.

<span id="an_36:40">36:40</span> Ngawo la amagama ezikhulu zakwaEsawu
ngokwezizwe zazo, ngokweendawo zazo, ngamagama azo: isikhulu
esinguTimna, isikhulu esinguAleva, isikhulu esinguYetete,

<span id="an_36:41">36:41</span> isikhulu esinguAholibhama, isikhulu
esinguEla, isikhulu esinguPinon,

<span id="an_36:42">36:42</span> isikhulu esinguKenazi, isikhulu
esinguTeman, isikhulu esinguMibhetsare,

<span id="an_36:43">36:43</span> isikhulu esinguMagediyeli, isikhulu
esinguIram. Zizo ezo izikhulu zakwaEdom, ngokwamakhaya azo, ezweni
lokuma kwazo. NguEsawu ke lowo uyise wamaEdom.
