<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> Ke kaloku uYakobi wahlala ezweni
lokuphambukela kukayise, ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> Yiyo le ke inzala kaYakobi. UYosefu,
engominyaka ilishumi linesixhenxe ezelwe, wayesalusa impahla emfutshane
ndawonye nabakhuluwa bakhe; yena ke, engumfana, wayenoonyana
bakaBhiliha, noonyana bakaZilipa, abafazi bakayise. UYosefu wazisa udaba
lwabo olubi kuyise.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> USirayeli wayemthanda uYosefu ngaphezu
kwabo bonke oonyana bakhe, ngokuba ebengunyana wokwaluphala kwakhe; yena
wamenzela ke ingubo ende enemikhono.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> Abakhuluwa bakhe babona ukuba uyise
umthanda ngaphezu kwabo bonke, bamthiya, ababa nakuthetha naye bexolile.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> UYosefu waphupha iphupha, wabaxelela
abakhuluwa bakhe; kwaba kukhona bamthiyayo.

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> Wathi kubo, Khanilive eli phupha
ndiliphuphileyo.

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> Yabonani, besibopha izithungu entsimini
phakathi; saza isithungu sam sesuka sema; zaza izithungu zenu
zasingqonga, zaqubuda kwisithungu sam.

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> Abakhuluwa bakhe bathi kuye, Yinene na
ukuba uya kuba ngukumkani phezu kwethu? Yinene na ukuba uya kusilawula?
Kwaba kukhona bamtiyayo ngenxa yamaphupha akhe, nangenxa yamazwi akhe.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> Wabuya waphupha elinye iphupha, walixela
kubakhuluwa bakhe, wathi, Yabonani, ndibuye ndaphupha iphupha; ndiphuphe
ilanga nenyanga neenkwenkwezi ezilushumi elinanye ziqubuda kum.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Wakuxela kuyise, nakubakhuluwa bakhe.
Uyise wamkhalimela, wathi kuye, Liphupha lini na eli uliphuphileyo? Mna,
nonyoko, nabakhuluwa bakho, soza size kuqubuda kuwe na emhlabeni?

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> Abakhuluwa bakhe bammonela, ke yena
uyise waligcina eli lizwi.

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> Ke kaloku abakhuluwa bakhe baya kwalusa
impahla emfutshane kayise kwaShekem.

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> USirayeli wathi kuYosefu, Abakhuluwa
bakho abalusi eShekem na? Yiza, ndikuthume kubo.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> Wathi yena kuye, Ndilapha. Wathi kuye,
Khawuye kukhangela ukuphila kwabakhuluwa bakho, nokuphila kwempahla
emfutshane; ubuye uze kundixelela. Wamthuma ke, emsusa entilini
yaseHebron, waya eShekem.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> Wafunyanwa ngumfo, ebhadula endle; umfo
lowo wambuza wathi, Ufuna ntoni na?

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> Wathi, Ndifuna abakhuluwa bam;
khawundixelele apho balusa khona.

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> Wathi umfo, Bandulukile apha, kuba
khendeva besithi, Masiye eDotan. UYosefu wabalandela abakhuluwa bakhe,
wabafumana eDotan.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> Bambona ke esekude, engekasondeli kubo,
benza iyelenqe lokumbulala.

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> Bathetha omnye komnye besithi, Nanko lo
mphuphi esiza.

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> Yizani ke ngoko, simbulale, simphose
komnye wemihadi, sithi, Udliwe lirhamncwa, size sibone ukuba amaphupha
akhe oba yintoni na.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> Weva uRubhen, wamhlangula esandleni
sabo; wathi, Masingambulali afe.

<span id="an_37:22">37:22</span> Wathi uRhubhen kubo, Musani ukuphalaza
gazi; mphoseni kulo mhadi usentlango; musani ukumsa sandla. Watsho,
ukuze amhlangule esandleni sabo, ambuyisele kuyise.

<span id="an_37:23">37:23</span> Kwathi akufika uYosefu kubakhuluwa
bakhe, bamhluba uYosefu ingubo yakhe, ingubo ende enemikhono abenayo;

<span id="an_37:24">37:24</span> bamthabatha, bamphosa emhadini; umhadi
lowo ube uze, kungekho manzi kuwo.

<span id="an_37:25">37:25</span> Bahlala phantsi, badla isonka;
baphakamisa amehlo abo, bakhangela, nango umkhoko wamaIshmayeli uvela
eGiliyadi, uneenkamela zithwele intlaka emhlophe, namafutha aqholiweyo,
nentlaka emnandi, besihla nazo besiya eYiputa.

<span id="an_37:26">37:26</span> UYuda wathi kubazalwana bakhe,
Yinzuzoni na ukuthi simbulale umninawa wethu, sifihle igazi lakhe?

<span id="an_37:27">37:27</span> Yizani sithengise ngaye kumaIshmayeli;
isandla sethu masingabi phezu kwakhe, ngokuba ngumzalwana wethu, yinyama
yethu. Bamphulaphula abazalwana bakhe.

<span id="an_37:28">37:28</span> Adlula amaMidiyan lawo angabarhwebi;
bamrhola, bamkhupha uYosefu emhadini, bathengisa ngoYosefu kumaIshmayeli
ngeesilivere ezimashumi mabini; amsa uYosefu eYiputa.

<span id="an_37:29">37:29</span> Wabuyela uRubhen emhadini. Yini?
UYosefu akakho emhadini; wazidrazula iingubo zakhe.

<span id="an_37:30">37:30</span> Wabuyela kubaninawa bakhe, wathi,
Umfana akakho; mna ke ndosuka ndiye ngaphi na?

<span id="an_37:31">37:31</span> Bayithabatha ingubo kaYosefu, baxhela
inkunzi yebhokhwe exhonti, bayithi nkxu ingubo egazini.

<span id="an_37:32">37:32</span> Bayithumela ingubo ende enemikhono
ekhaya, bayisa kuyise, bathi, Siyichole; khawufanise, ukuba yingubo
yonyana wakho, asiyiyo, sini na?

<span id="an_37:33">37:33</span> Wayifanisa, wathi, Yingubo yonyana wam;
udliwe lirhamncwa; inene, uqwengiwe uYosefu.

<span id="an_37:34">37:34</span> UYakobi wazikrazula iingubo zakhe,
wabeka ezirhwexayo esinqeni sakhe, wamenzela isijwili unyana wakhe
imihla emininzi.

<span id="an_37:35">37:35</span> Besuka bonke oonyana bakhe nazo zonke
iintombi zakhe, beza kumthuthuzela; akavuma kuthuthuzelwa, wathi, Ndiya
kuhla ndiye kunyana wam kwelabafileyo, ndisenza isijwili. Uyise
wamlilela ke.

<span id="an_37:36">37:36</span> AmaMidiyan aya athengisa ngaya eYiputa
kuPotifare, umbusi wakwaFaro, umthetheli wabasiki.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> Kwathi ngelo xesha, wehla uYuda, esuka
kubazalwana bakhe, waya wayimisa intente yakhe ngakwindoda yaseAdulam,
egama linguHira.

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> UYuda wabona khona intombi yendoda
engumKanan, egama linguShuwa; wayizeka, wayingena.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> Yamitha, yazala unyana; wathi igama lakhe
nguEre.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> Yabuya yamitha, yazala unyana; yathi
igama lakhe nguOnan.

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> Yabuya yaphinda yamitha, yazala unyana;
yathi igama lakhe nguShela; wayeseKezibhi ukumzala kwakhe.

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> UYuda wamzekela uEre, amazibulo akhe,
umfazi ogama linguTamare.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Ke uEre, amazibulo kaYuda, ubeneentlondi
ezimbi emehlweni kaYehova; waza uYehova wambulala.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> UYuda wathi kuOnan, Yiya kumfazi
womkhuluwa wakho, umngene, umvelisele imbewu umkhuluwa wakho.

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> Wayesazi uOnan ukuba imbewu ayiyi kuba
yeyakhe; wathi, xa sukuba esiya kumfazi womkhuluwa wakhe, wayiphalazela
emhlabeni ukuze angamniki mbewu umkhuluwa wakhe.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> Kwaba kubi emehlweni kaYehova oko
wakwenzayo; ngoko wambulala naye.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> Wathi uYuda kuTamare, umolokazana
wakhe, Hlala ungumhlolokazi endlwini kayihlo, ade akhule uShela, unyana
wam; kuba wathi, Hleze afe naye, njengabakhuluwa bakhe. Wemka uTamare,
waya kuhlala endlwini kayise.

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> Zakuba ninzi iintsuku, yafa intombi
kaShuwa, umkaYuda Akuthuthuzeleka uYuda, wenyuka waya kubachebi bempahla
yakhe emfutshane, yena noHira, isihlobo sakhe saseAdulam, kwaTimna.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> Waxelelwa uTamare kwathiwa, Nanko
uyihlozala, enyuka esiya kucheba impahla yakhe emfutshane kwaTimna.

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> Wazisusa iingubo zobuhlolokazi bakhe,
wazigqubuthela ngesigqubuthelo, wazithi wambu, wahlala phantsi esangweni
le-Enayim, engasendleleni eya kwaTimna; kuba ubebona ukuba ukhulile
uShela, akasiwa noko kuye ukuba abe ngumkakhe.

<span id="an_38:15">38:15</span> UYuda wambona, waba ulihenyukazi, kuba
ebegqubuthele ubuso.

<span id="an_38:16">38:16</span> Wathi gu bucala, waya kuye endleleni
wathi, Khawuze, ndikungene; kuba ubengazi ukuba ngumolokazana wakhe.
Wathi, Wondinika ntoni na, ukuze ndikuvumele ukuba undingene?

<span id="an_38:17">38:17</span> Wathi, Mna ndothumela ndithabathe
itakane lebhokwe elisempahleni emfutshane. Wathi, Ewe, ukuba uthe
wandinika isibambiso, ude ulithumele kum.

<span id="an_38:18">38:18</span> Wathi, Ndikunike sibambiso sini na?
Wathi yena, Umsesane wakho, nesidanga sakho, nomsimelelo wakho
osesandleni sakho. Wamnika ke, wamngena, wamitha yena ngaye.

<span id="an_38:19">38:19</span> Wesuka wemka, wasisusa isigqubuthelo
sakhe, wambatha iingubo zobuhlolokazi bakhe.

<span id="an_38:20">38:20</span> UYuda walithumela itakane lebhokhwe
ngesandla sesihlobo sakhe saseAdulam, ukuze samkele isibambiso esandleni
senkazana leyo; asiyifumananga ke.

<span id="an_38:21">38:21</span> Sabuza kubantu baloo ndawo, sathi,
Liphi na ing’awukazi ebe lise-Enayim ngasendleleni? Bathi, Akubangakho
ng’awukazi apha.

<span id="an_38:22">38:22</span> Sabuyela kuYuda sathi, Andilifumananga;
nabo abantu baloo ndawo bathe, Akubangakho ng’awukazi apha.

<span id="an_38:23">38:23</span> Wathi uYuda, Malizithabathe, hleze
sidelwe. Yabona, ndithumele eli takane, ke wena akulifumananga.

<span id="an_38:24">38:24</span> Kwathi, emva kweenyanga ezintathu,
waxelelwa uYuda kwathiwa, UTamare, umolokazana wakho, uhenyuzile;
kananjalo, yabona, umithi ngokuhenyuza oko. UYuda wathi, Mkhupheni
atshiswe.

<span id="an_38:25">38:25</span> Akukhutshwa, wathumela yena kuyisezala,
wathi, Ndimithiswe yindoda ezizezayo ezi zinto; wathi, Khawufanise ukuba
ngokabani na lo msesane, nesi sidanga, nalo msimelelo.

<span id="an_38:26">38:26</span> Wazifanisa uYuda, wathi, Ulilungisa
kunam; wenze kuba ndingamnikanga uShela, unyana wam. Akabanga sabuya
amazi.

<span id="an_38:27">38:27</span> Kwathi, ngexesha lokuzala kwakhe, nanku
ingamawele esizalweni sakhe.

<span id="an_38:28">38:28</span> Kwathi, ekuzaleni kwakhe, kwavela
isandla; wathabatha umzalisikazi, wabopha esandleni salo usinga
olubomvu, esithi, Eli laphuma kuqala.

<span id="an_38:29">38:29</span> Kuthe ke, lakusibuyisa isandla salo,
nanko kuphuma umzalwana walo. Wathi, Yini na ukuba uzityhobozele?
Wathiywa ke igama lokuba nguPeretse.

<span id="an_38:30">38:30</span> Kwathi emva koko, kwaphuma umzalwana
walo, obenosinga olubomvu esandleni sakhe; wathiywa igama lokuba
nguZera.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> Ke kaloku uYosefu wahliswa wasiwa
eYiputa. UPotifare, umbusi wakwaFaro, umthetheli wabasiki, umYiputa,
wamthenga kumaIshmayeli, abemhlisele khona.

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> UYehova waba naye uYosefu, waba yindoda
enempumelelo; waba sendlwini yenkosi yakhe, umYiputa lowo.

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> Yabona inkosi yakhe ukuba uYehova unaye,
ukuba zonke izinto abezenza, uYehova ubezenza zibe nempumelelo esandleni
sakhe.

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> UYosefu wababalwa emehlweni ayo,
wayilungiselela; yamenza umveleli wendlu yayo, neento zonke ebinazo
yazinikela esandleni sakhe.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Kwathi, ukususela ekubeni yamenza
umveleli wendlu yayo neento zonke ebinazo, wayisikelela uYehova indlu
yomYiputa lowo ngenxa kaYosefu. Yabakho intsikelelo kaYehova ezintweni
zonke ebinazo, endlwini nasezindle.

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> Zonke izinto ebinazo yaziyekela esandleni
sikaYosefu, ayakhathalela nanye into ebikuye, ingesiso isonka esidlayo.
Ke uYosefu ebemhle isiqu, emhle imbonakalo.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> Kwathi emveni kwezi zinto, umfazi wenkosi
yakhe waphosa amehlo akhe kuYosefu, wathi, Ndilale.

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> Wamangala, wathi kumka-nkosi yakhe,
Yabona, inkosi yam ayikhathalele nto ikum isendlwini, nezinto zonke
enazo izinikele esandleni sam.

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> Akukho bani mkhulu kum kule ndlu;
ayinqabisanga nento le kum, nguwe wedwa, ngokokuba ungumkayo;
ndingathini na ke ukwenza obu bubi bukhulu kangaka, ndone kuThixo?

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> Kwathi, nakuba ebethetha kuYosefu
imihla ngemihla, akamphulaphula yena ukuba alale ecaleni lakhe, nokuthi
abe naye.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> Kwathi kuloo mihla, wangena endlwini
eya kusebenza umsebenzi wakhe; kwaye kungekho nanye yakumadoda endlu
endlwini apho.

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Wambamba ngengubo wathi, Ndilale.
Wayishiya ingubo yakhe esandleni sakhe, wabaleka, waphumela phandle.

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> Kwathi, akubona ukuba uyishiyile ingubo
yakhe esandleni sakhe, ubalekele phandle,

<span id="an_39:14">39:14</span> wabiza amadoda endlu yakhe, wathetha
kuwo, esithi, Khangelani, usizisele indoda engumHebhere, ukuba idlale
ngathi; izile kum, isiza kundilala, ndakhala ngezwi elikhulu;

<span id="an_39:15">39:15</span> yathi, yakuva ndiphakamisa izwi,
ndikhala, yayishiya ingubo yayo ecaleni lam, yabaleka, yaphumela
phandle.

<span id="an_39:16">39:16</span> Wayibeka phantsi ingubo yayo ecaleni
lakhe, yada yafika inkosi yakhe endlwini yayo.

<span id="an_39:17">39:17</span> Wathetha kuyo ngokwaloo mazwi esithi,
Size kum isicaka esingumHebhere, esi usizisele sona, ukuba sidlale ngam;

<span id="an_39:18">39:18</span> kuthe, ndakuliphakamisa izwi lam,
ndikhala, sayishiya ingubo yaso ecaleni lam, sabalekela phandle.

<span id="an_39:19">39:19</span> Ithe, yakuweva inkosi yakhe amazwi
omkayo awawathethayo kuyo, esithi, Senjenje isicaka sakho kum, wavutha
umsindo wayo.

<span id="an_39:20">39:20</span> Inkosi kaYosefu yamthabatha, yamfaka
entolongweni, kuloo ndawo apho amakhonkxwa okumkani abekhonkxwa khona,
waba sentolongweni apho ke.

<span id="an_39:21">39:21</span> UYehova ubenoYosefu, wamthobela inceba,
wenza ukuba athandwe ngumphathi wentolongo.

<span id="an_39:22">39:22</span> Umphathi wentolongo wawanikela kuYosefu
onke amakhonkxwa asentolongweni, ukuze zonke izinto ezisukuba zisenziwa
khona, abe nguye ozenzayo.

<span id="an_39:23">39:23</span> Umphathi wentolongo akakhathalelanga
nto isesandleni sakhe, ngenxa yokuba uYehova ubenaye; zonke izinto
ebesakuzenza, uYehova ubeziphumelelisa.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> Kwathi emveni kwezi zinto, umngcamli
wokumkani waseYiputa, nomoji wezonka zakhe, bayona inkosi yabo, ukumkani
waseYiputa.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> UFaro waba noburhalarhume kubo ababusi
bakhe bobabini, umphathi wabangcamli nomphathi waboji bezonka.

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> Wabanikela elugcinweni, endlwini
yomthetheli wabasiki entolongweni, endaweni abekhonkxelwe kuyo uYosefu.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> Umthetheli wabasiki wamenza uYosefu
umveleli wabo, wabalungiselela; baba nomzuzu beselugcinweni.

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> Baphupha iphupha bobabini; elowo waphupha
iphupha lakhe ngabusuku bunye, elowo ngokokutyhilwa kwephupha lakhe,
umngcamli nomoji wezonka bokumkani waseYiputa, ababekhonkxiwe
entolongweni.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> UYosefu wangena kubo kwakusa,
wabakhangela, wafika bematshekile.

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> Wababuza ababusi bakwaFaro, ababenaye
elugcinweni endlwini yenkosi yakhe, esithi, Kutheni na ukuba ubuso benu
bube bubi namhlanje?

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> Bathi kuye, Siphuphe iphupha; akukho
ulityhilayo. UYosefu wathi kubo, Izityhilo asizezikaThixo na?
Khanindixelele iphupha elo.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> Umphathi wabangcamli wamxelela uYosefu
iphupha lakhe, wathi kuye, Ephupheni lam ndibone umdiliya uphambi kwam;

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> emdiliyeni apho amasebe emathathu,
wangathi wona uphuma amathupha, wadubula iintyantyambo zawo, izihloko
zawo zavuthwa zaziidiliya;

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> indebe kaFaro isesandleni sam;
ndizithabathe iidiliya, ndizifaxange endebeni kaFaro, ndiyinikele indebe
esandleni sikaFaro.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> UYosefu wathi kuye, Siso esi isityhilo
salo: amasebe amathathu lawo yimihla emithathu;

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> kusele imihla emithathu, aze uFaro
ayiphakamise intloko yakho, akubuyisele endaweni yakho, uyinikele indebe
kaFaro esandleni sakhe ngokwesiko langaphambili, oko ubungumngcamli
wakhe.

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Uze undikhumbule ke, wakulungelwa,
undenzele inceba, undikhankanye kuFaro, undikhuphe kule ndlu;

<span id="an_40:15">40:15</span> ngokuba inene ndabiwa ezweni
lamaHebhere, nalapha andenzanga nto, ukuba bandifake emhadini lo.

<span id="an_40:16">40:16</span> Umphathi waboji-zonka wabona ukuba
isityhilo eso silungile, wathi kuYosefu, Nam ndiphuphile; ndibone
iingobozi ezintathu zezonka ezimhlophe ezisentlokweni yam;

<span id="an_40:17">40:17</span> engobozini ephezulu kukho izidlo
ngezidlo zonke zikaFaro ezingumsebenzi womoji-zonka, iintaka zisidla
kweyona ngobozi iphezulu entlokweni yam.

<span id="an_40:18">40:18</span> Waphendula uYosefu wathi, Siso esi
isityhilo salo: iingobozi ezintathu ezo yimihla emithathu;

<span id="an_40:19">40:19</span> kusele imihla emithathu, aze uFaro
ayiphakamise intloko yakho, isuke kuwe, akuxhome emthini, ziyidle
iintaka inyama yakho iphele.

<span id="an_40:20">40:20</span> Kwathi ngomhla wasithathu, umhla
wokuzalwa kukaFaro, wabenzela isidlo bonke abakhonzi bakhe,
wayiphakamisa intloko yomphathi wabangcamli, nentloko yomphathi waboji
bezonka phakathi kwabakhonzi bakhe.

<span id="an_40:21">40:21</span> Wambuyisela umphathi wabangcamli
kubungcamli bakhe; wayinikela indebe esandleni sikaFaro.

<span id="an_40:22">40:22</span> Ke yena umphathi waboji bezonka
wamxhoma, njengoko uYosefu wabatyhilelayo.

<span id="an_40:23">40:23</span> Umphathi wabangcamli akamkhumbulanga
uYosefu, wamlibala.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> Kwathi, ekupheleni kweminyaka emibini
ezeleyo, uFaro waphupha emi phezu komlambo;

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> nanko kunyuka, kuphuma emlanjeni,
amathokazi asixhenxe amahle, etyebile, esidla engcotyeni;

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> nanko kunyuka, kuphuma emlanjeni, amanye
amathokazi asixhenxe emva kwawo, emabi, enqinile; ema ecaleni lamanye
amathokazi lawo elunxwemeni lomlambo;

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> asuka amathokazi amabi, anqinileyo,
awadla amathokazi asixhenxe amahle, atyebileyo. Waphaphama uFaro.

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> Walala waphupha okwesibini. Wabona
izikhwebu ezisixhenxe ziphuma mcingeni mnye, zityebile, zilungile.

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> Nanzo izikhwebu ezisixhenxe
ezingcakacileyo, ezitshileyo lulophu lwasempumalanga, ziphuma emva
kwazo;

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> zesuka izikhwebu ezingcakacileyo
zaziginya izikhwebu zosixhenxe ezityebileyo, ezichumileyo. Wavuka uFaro,
O, liphupha!

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> Kwathi kusasa, umoya wakhe wangqunga;
wathumela, wazibiza zonke izazi zaseYiputa, izilumko zonke zakhona.
UFaro wazixelela iphupha lakhe; akwabakho bani kuzo unokuwatyhila
kuFaro.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> Wathetha umphathi wabangcamli kuFaro,
esithi, Ndiyasikhumbula namhlanje isono sam.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> UFaro wayenoburhalarhume kubakhonzi
bakhe, wandinikela elugcinweni endlwini yomthetheli wabasiki, mna lo,
nomphathi waboji bezonka.

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Saphupha iphupha ngabusuku bunye, mna
naye; walowo waphupha ngokutyhilwa kwephupha lakhe.

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> Kwakukho kuthi umfana ongumHebhere
isicaka somthetheli wabasiki, sasixelela, sasityhilela amaphupha ethu,
samtyhilela elowo ngokwephupha lakhe.

<span id="an_41:13">41:13</span> Kwathi, ngokoko sisityhileleyo, kwaba
njalo; mna wandibuyisela endaweni yam, omnye lowo wamxhoma.

<span id="an_41:14">41:14</span> UFaro wathumela, wambiza uYosefu.
Bamgidimisa ukumkhupha emhadini; wazicheba, wanxiba ngubo zimbi, weza
kuFaro.

<span id="an_41:15">41:15</span> Wathi uFaro kuYosefu, Ndiphuphe
iphupha, akukho bani unokulityhila; mna ndive kusithiwa ngawe, uyaliva
iphupha ulityhile.

<span id="an_41:16">41:16</span> UYosefu wamphendula uFaro, esithi,
Akunam; uThixo uya kuphendula into yokumsindisa uFaro.

<span id="an_41:17">41:17</span> UFaro wathetha kuYosefu, wathi,
Ephupheni lam, yabona, bendimi elunxwemeni lomlambo;

<span id="an_41:18">41:18</span> nanko kunyuka, kuphuma emlanjeni,
amathokazi asixhenxe etyebile, emahle, esidla engcotyeni;

<span id="an_41:19">41:19</span> nanko, kunyuka kuphuma amanye
amathokazi asixhenxe emva kwawo, ebhityile, emabi kakhulu,
engamarhoqorhoqo, endingazanga ndibone anjalo kulo lonke ilizwe
laseYiputa, ukuba mabi kwawo;

<span id="an_41:20">41:20</span> amathokazi angamarhoqorhoqo, amabi,
awadla awokuqala amathokazi asixhenxe atyebileyo;

<span id="an_41:21">41:21</span> angena embilinini wawo akwazeka ukuba
angenile embilinini wawo; imbonakalo yawo yambi, njengasekuqaleni.
Ndaphaphama.

<span id="an_41:22">41:22</span> Ndabona ephupheni lam, izikhwebu
ezisixhenxe ziphuma micingeni mnye, zichumile, zilungile;

<span id="an_41:23">41:23</span> nanzo, izikhwebu ezisixhenxe
zishwabene, zingcakacile, zitshile lulophu lwasempumalanga, zihluma emva
kwazo.

<span id="an_41:24">41:24</span> Zesuka izikhwebu ezingcakacileyo,
zaziginya izikhwebu ezisixhenxe ezilungileyo. Ndathetha nezazi; akukho
bani kuzo undixelelayo.

<span id="an_41:25">41:25</span> UYosefu wathi uFaro, Iphupha likaFaro
linye; uThixo umxelele uFaro oko aya kukwenza.

<span id="an_41:26">41:26</span> Amathokazi asixhenxe alungileyo
yiminyaka esixhenxe; izikhwebu ezisixhenxe ezilungileyo yiminyaka
esixhenxe; iphupha eli linye.

<span id="an_41:27">41:27</span> Amathokazi asixhenxe angamarhoqorhoqo,
amabi, anyukileyo aphuma emva kwalawo, yiminyaka esixhenxe; nezikhwebu
ezisixhenxe ezinqinileyo, ezitshileyo lulophu lwasempumalanga, ziya kuba
yiminyaka esixhenxe yendlala.

<span id="an_41:28">41:28</span> Lelo lizwi ndilithethileyo kuFaro
lokuthi: oko aya kukwenza uThixo ukubonisile kuFaro.

<span id="an_41:29">41:29</span> Yabona, kuza iminyaka esixhenxe
yendyebo enkulu ezweni lonke laseYiputa;

<span id="an_41:30">41:30</span> ze kuvele iminyaka esixhenxe yendlala
emva kwaleyo, ilityalwe yonke indyebo ezweni laseYiputa, indlala
iligqibe ilizwe;

<span id="an_41:31">41:31</span> ingaziwa indyebo elizweni, ngenxa yaloo
iya kubakho emva kwayo, kuba iya kuba nzima kunene.

<span id="an_41:32">41:32</span> Ukuphindwa kabini kwephupha elo kuFaro
kukuqiniswa kwayo le ndawo nguThixo; uya kukhawuleza uThixo ukuyenza.

<span id="an_41:33">41:33</span> Ngoko uFaro makakhangele indoda
eyingqondi, esisilumko, ayimise phezu kwelizwe laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:34">41:34</span> Makenze le nto uFaro, alimisele
abaveleli ilizwe, athabathe isihlanu selizwe laseYiputa ngeminyaka
yosixhenxe yendyebo.

<span id="an_41:35">41:35</span> Mababuthe konke ukudla kwaloo minyaka
ilungileyo izayo, bafumbe ingqolowa phantsi kwesandla sikaFaro, ibe
kukudla emizini, bayigcine;

<span id="an_41:36">41:36</span> oko kudla kube yinto ebekelwe ilizwe
iminyaka yosixhenxe yendlala, eya kubakho ezweni laseYiputa,
lingatshabalali ilizwe yindlala.

<span id="an_41:37">41:37</span> Lalunga elo zwi emehlweni kaFaro
nasemehlweni abo bonke abakhonzi bakhe.

<span id="an_41:38">41:38</span> UFaro wathi kubakhonzi bakhe,
Sinokumfumana na umntu onje, onoMoya kaThixo?

<span id="an_41:39">41:39</span> UFaro wathi kuYosefu, Ekubeni uThixo
ekwazisile konke oku, akukho bani uyingqondi, usisilumko, njengawe.

<span id="an_41:40">41:40</span> Uya kuba phezu kwendlu yam wena,
bawuthobele umlomo wakho bonke abantu bam; kusetroneni yodwa endiya kuba
mkhulu kuwe.

<span id="an_41:41">41:41</span> UFaro wathi kuYosefu, Khangela,
ndikumise phezu kwalo lonke ilizwe laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:42">41:42</span> Wawukhulula uFaro umsesane wakhe
esandleni sakhe, wawufaka esandleni sikaYosefu, wamambathisa iingubo
zelinen ecikizekileyo, wanxiba umxokelelwane wegolide entanyeni yakhe.

<span id="an_41:43">41:43</span> Wamkhwelisa enqwelweni yesibini
abenayo, kwamenyezwa phambi kwakhe, kwathiwa, Guqani! Wammisa phezu
kwalo lonke ilizwe laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:44">41:44</span> Wathi uFaro kuYosefu, NdinguFaro;
ngaphandle kwakho, akukho bani uya kuphakamisa sandla sakhe, nalunyawo
lwakhe, ezweni lonke laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:45">41:45</span> UFaro wamthiya uYosefu igama lokuba
nguTsafenati-paneha, wamnika uAzenati, intombi kaPotifera, umbingeleli
waseOn, ukuba abe ngumkakhe. Waphuma uYosefu, walihamba ilizwe
laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:46">41:46</span> UYosefu wayeminyaka imashumi mathathu
ezelwe, ukuma kwakhe phambi koFaro, ukumkani waseYiputa; waphuma uYosefu
ebusweni bukaFaro, walicanda lonke ilizwe laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:47">41:47</span> Umhlaba wavelisa ngendiphane ngeminyaka
esixhenxe yendyebo.

<span id="an_41:48">41:48</span> Wakubutha konke ukudla kweminyaka
esixhenxe ebikho ezweni laseYiputa, wakubeka ukudla kuyo imizi; ukudla
kwamasimi abewungqongile umzi, wakubeka phakathi kwawo.

<span id="an_41:49">41:49</span> UYosefu wayifumba ingqolowa
yanjengentlabathi yolwandle, yaninzi kunene, wada wayeka ukubala, kuba
ibingenakubalwa.

<span id="an_41:50">41:50</span> UYosefu wazala oonyana bababini,
wabazalelwa nguAzenati, intombi kaPotifera, umbingeleli waseOn,
ingekafiki iminyaka yendlala.

<span id="an_41:51">41:51</span> UYosefu wamthiya owamazibulo igama
elinguManase; ngokuba wathi, UThixo undenze ndakulibala konke ukwaphuka
kwam, nayo yonke indlu kabawo.

<span id="an_41:52">41:52</span> Owesibini wamthiya igama elinguEfrayim;
ngokuba wathi, UThixo undiqhamisile ezweni leentsizi zam.

<span id="an_41:53">41:53</span> Yaphela ke iminyaka yosixhenxe yendyebo
ebisezweni laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:54">41:54</span> Yaqala ukufika iminyaka yosixhenxe
yendlala, njengoko wayekuthethile uYosefu. Yabakho indlala kumazwe onke;
ke ezweni lonke laseYiputa kwakukho isonka.

<span id="an_41:55">41:55</span> Lonke ilizwe laseYiputa laba nendlala;
abantu bakhalela isonka kuFaro; wathi uFaro kuwo onke amaYiputa, Yiyani
kuYosefu; athe wakuthetha kuni nize nikwenze.

<span id="an_41:56">41:56</span> Indlala yaba sezweni lonke; uYosefu
wazivula zonke izindlu ezinokudla, wathengisa ngengqolowa kumaYiputa;
kuba indlala yaba namandla ezweni laseYiputa.

<span id="an_41:57">41:57</span> Lesuka ilizwe liphela, leza kuthenga
ingqolowa kuYosefu eYiputa, kuba indlala ibinamandla kulo lonke.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> Wabona uYakobi ukuba kukho ingqolowa
eYiputa, wathi uYakobi koonyana bakhe, Yini na ukuba nikhangelane?

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> Wathi, Yabonani, ndivile ukuba kukho
ingqolowa eYiputa; yihlani niye khona, nisithengele ingqolowa, siphile,
singafi.

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> Behla abakhuluwa bakaYosefu abalishumi,
beya kuthenga ingqolowa eYiputa.

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> Kodwa uBhenjamin, umninawa kaYosefu,
uYakobi akamthumanga nabakhuluwa bakhe; kuba wathi, hleze ahlelwe
yingozi.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> Oonyana bakaSirayeli beza kuthenga
ingqolowa phakathi kwabo bezayo; kuba indlala ibikho ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> UYosefu wayengumlawuli welizwe elo; yena
wayethengisa ngengqolowa kubo bonke abantu belizwe elo; bafika ke
abakhuluwa bakaYosefu, baqubuda kuye ngobuso emhlabeni.

<span id="an_42:7">42:7</span> UYosefu wababona abakhuluwa bakhe,
wabazi, wazenza ongabaziyo, wathetha nabo kalukhuni, wathi kubo, Nivela
phi na? Bathi, Sivela ezweni lakwaKanan, size kuthenga ukudla.

<span id="an_42:8">42:8</span> UYosefu wabazi abakhuluwa bakhe; ke bona
abamnakananga.

<span id="an_42:9">42:9</span> Wawakhumbula uYosefu amaphupha
abewaphuphile ngabo, wathi kubo, Niziintlola nina; nize kubona ubuze
belizwe eli.

<span id="an_42:10">42:10</span> Bathi kuye, Hayi, nkosi; abakhonzi
bakho baze kuthenga ukudla.

<span id="an_42:11">42:11</span> Sonke siphela singoonyana bamfo mnye;
siyalungisa, abakhonzi bakho abazizo iintlola.

<span id="an_42:12">42:12</span> Wathi kubo, Hayi, nize kubona ubuze
belizwe eli.

<span id="an_42:13">42:13</span> Bathi, Abakhonzi bakho balishumi
elinababini; siyazalana, singoonyana bamfo mnye ezweni lakwaKanan.
UYabona, omncinane ukubawo namhla, omnye akakho.

<span id="an_42:14">42:14</span> Wathi uYosefu kubo, Yile nto
bendiyithetha kuni, ndisithi, Niziintlola.

<span id="an_42:15">42:15</span> Niya kucikidwa ngale ndawo: ehleli nje
uFaro, anisayi kuphuma apha, ukuba akathanga eze apha umninawa wenu
omncinane.

<span id="an_42:16">42:16</span> Thumani omnye kuni apha, aphuthume
umninawa wenu, nikhonkxwe nina; acikidwe amazwi enu ukuba ninenyaniso
na; ukuba akubanga njalo, ehleli nje uFaro, inene noba niziintlola.

<span id="an_42:17">42:17</span> Wabanikela bonke elugcinweni imihla
yamithathu.

<span id="an_42:18">42:18</span> UYosefu wathi kubo ngomhla wesithathu,
Yenzani oku, niphile; kuba ndiyamoyika uThixo.

<span id="an_42:19">42:19</span> Ukuba ninyanisile, omnye umzalwana kuni
apha makakhonkxwe endlwini yokugcinwa kwenu, nihambe nina, niyise
ingqolowa ngenxa yendlala yezindlu zenu.

<span id="an_42:20">42:20</span> Umninawa wenu omncinane nimzise kum;
okholeka ke amazwi enu, ningafi.

<span id="an_42:21">42:21</span> Benjenjalo ke. Bathetha omnye komnye
besithi, Inyaniso, sinetyala ngenxa yomninawa wethu, sabe sikubona nje
ukubandezeleka komphefumlo wakhe, oko abetarhuzisa kuthi,
asamphulaphula; kungenxa yoko le nto kusifikeleyo oku kubandezeleka.

<span id="an_42:22">42:22</span> Wabaphendulu uRubhen esithi, Ndabe
ndingatsho na kuni ukuthi, Musani ukumona umfana? Anaphulaphula;
yabonani ke, igazi lakhe liyabizwa.

<span id="an_42:23">42:23</span> Babengazi bona ukuba uYosefu uyeva,
kuba kwakumi umkhumshi phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_42:24">42:24</span> Wathi guququ, walila; wabuya weza kubo,
wathetha nabo, wamthabatha uSimon kubo, wamkhonkxa bekhangele.

<span id="an_42:25">42:25</span> Wawisa umthetho uYosefu wokuba
zizaliswe iingxowa zabo ngengqolowa, imali yabo ibuyiselwe kulowo nalowo
engxoweni yakhe, banikwe nomphako wendlela; kwenjiwa njalo ke kubo.

<span id="an_42:26">42:26</span> Bawabopha ingqolowa amaesile abo, bemka
ke apho.

<span id="an_42:27">42:27</span> Uthe ke omnye akuyivula ingxowa yakhe,
ukuba aphe iesile lakhe iindiza apho balalisa khona, wayibona imali
yakhe, esemlonyeni wengxowa yakhe.

<span id="an_42:28">42:28</span> Wathi kubazalwana bakhe, Ibuyisiwe
imali yam; nantsi ikho nokubakho engxoweni yam. Baphela amandla,
bakhangelana begubha, bathi, Yintoni na le ayenzileyo uThixo kuthi?

<span id="an_42:29">42:29</span> Bafika kuYakobi uyise ezweni
lakwaKanan, bamxelela yonke into ebahleleyo, besithi,

<span id="an_42:30">42:30</span> Indoda, inkosi yelo zwe, yathetha nathi
kalukhuni, yathi siziintlola zelo zwe.

<span id="an_42:31">42:31</span> Sathi kuyo, Sinyanisile;

<span id="an_42:32">42:32</span> asizizo iintlola, singabazalwana
abalishumi elinababini, oonyana bakabawo; omnye akakho, omncinane
ukubawo namhla, ezweni lakwaKanan.

<span id="an_42:33">42:33</span> Indoda leyo, inkosi yelo zwe, yathi
kuthi, Ndiya kwazi ngale ndawo ukuba ninyanisile: shiyani abe mnye
umzalwana wenu kum apha, niphathele izindlu zenu ukudla ngenxa yendlala,
nihambe;

<span id="an_42:34">42:34</span> nimzise umninawa wenu omncinane kum,
ndize ndazi ukuba ninyanisile, anizizo iintlola; ndimnikele kuni
umzalwana wenu, nirhwebe ezweni apha.

<span id="an_42:35">42:35</span> Kwathi, bakukhuphela iingxowa zabo,
babona isiqhuma semali salowo nalowo engxoweni yakhe; bakuzibona
iziqhuma zabo zemali boyika, bona noyise.

<span id="an_42:36">42:36</span> Wathi kubo uYakobi uyise, Nindihluthe
abantwana; uYosefu akakho, uSimon akakho, niza kuthabatha noBhenjamin;
zikhwele kum zonke ezo zinto.

<span id="an_42:37">42:37</span> Wathi uRubhen kuyise, Babulale bobabini
oonyana bam, ukuba andithanga ndimzise kuwe; mnikele esandleni sam,
ndombuyisela kuwe mna.

<span id="an_42:38">42:38</span> Wathi yena, Unyana wam akasayi kuhla
nani; ngokuba ufile umkhuluwa wakhe, yena usele yedwa. Ukuba uthe
wahlelwa yingozi endleleni eniyihambayo, izimvi zam nozithobela
kwelabafileyo ndinesingqala.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> Indlala yayinzima kwelo zwe.

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> Kwathi, bakuba begqibile ukuyidla
ingqolowa ababeze nayo bevela eYiputa, wathi uyise kubo, Buyani niye
kusithengela intwana yokudla.

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> Wathi uYuda kuye, Indoda leyo
yaqononondisa kuthi, yathi, Aniyi kububona ubuso bam, engabangakho nani
umninawa wenu.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> Ukuba uthe wamthuma umninawa wethu nathi,
sohla siye kukuthengela ukudla.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> Ukuba akuthanga umthume, asiyi kuhla;
kuba indoda leyo yathi kuthi, Aniyi kububona ubuso bam, engabangakho
nani umninawa wenu.

<span id="an_43:6">43:6</span> USirayeli wathi, Yini na ukuba nindenzele
ububi, niyixelele indoda leyo ukuthi, nisenomninawa?

<span id="an_43:7">43:7</span> Bathi, Indoda leyo yabuza kunene ngathi
nangemizalwana yethu, isithi, Usaphilile na uyihlo? Nisenomninawa na?
Sayixelela ngokwaloo mazwi. Besisazi yini na ukuba ibiya kuthi, Yihlani
nomninawa wenu?

<span id="an_43:8">43:8</span> UYuda wathi kuSirayeli uyise, Mthume nam
umfana, sisuke sihambe, siphile, singafi thina, nawe, nabantwana bethu.

<span id="an_43:9">43:9</span> Mna ndiya kummela, wombiza esandleni sam;
ukuba andithanga ndimzise kuwe, ndimbeke phambi kwakho, mandibe netyala
kuwe yonke imihla yam.

<span id="an_43:10">43:10</span> Kuba, ukuba besingazilazilanga, inene
ngesiba ngoku sesibuye okwesibini.

<span id="an_43:11">43:11</span> USirayeli uyise wathi kubo, Ukuba
kunjalo okunene, yenzani ke oku: thabathani kwezinconywayo izinto
zelizwe eli, nizifake ezingxoweni zenu, nihle niyisele indoda leyo
umnikelo: intwana yamafutha aqholiweyo, nentwana yencindi yobusi,
nentlaka emhlophe, nentlaka emnandi, neenkozo zepistasi, neeamangile.

<span id="an_43:12">43:12</span> Phathani enye imali esandleni senu;
naloo mali yabuyiswayo emlonyeni weengxowa zenu, buyani nayo esandleni
senu; mhlawumbi sisiphosiso.

<span id="an_43:13">43:13</span> Nomninawa wenu mthabatheni, ninduluke,
nibuyele kwindoda leyo.

<span id="an_43:14">43:14</span> Ngamana uThixo uSomandla waniphatha
ngemfesane phambi kwendoda leyo, ukuba inikhululele omnye umzalwana wenu
lowo noBhenjamin. Mna, ukuba ndihluthiwe abantwana, ndihluthiwe.

<span id="an_43:15">43:15</span> Amadoda lawo awuthabatha loo mnikelo,
neemali zombini aziphatha esandleni sawo, noBhenjamin, asuka ehla aya
eYiputa, ema phambi koYosefu.

<span id="an_43:16">43:16</span> UYosefu wambona uBhenjamin enabo, wathi
kumphathi wendlu yakhe, Wangenise loo madoda endlwini, uxhele, ulungise;
kuba la madoda aya kudla nam emini enkulu.

<span id="an_43:17">43:17</span> Indoda leyo yenza njengoko watshoyo
uYosefu; indoda yawangenisa amadoda endlwini kaYosefu.

<span id="an_43:18">43:18</span> Amadoda oyika, ngokuba engeniswe
endlwini kaYosefu, athi, Kungenxa yemali eyayibuyiselwe ezingxoweni
zethu ekuqaleni, le nto singeniswe apha; ukuze agaleleke phezu kwethu,
asiwele, asithabathe sibe ngamakhoboka, kwanamaesile ethu.

<span id="an_43:19">43:19</span> Asondela kuloo ndoda iphethe indlu
kaYosefu, athetha nayo emnyango wendlu, athi, Tarhu, nkosi!

<span id="an_43:20">43:20</span> Sehla okunene ekuqaleni, sisiza
kuthenga ukudla.

<span id="an_43:21">43:21</span> Kwathi, sakufika endaweni yokulalisa,
sazivula iingxowa zethu, kwavela imali yalowo nalowo emlonyeni wengxowa
yakhe, imali yethu ngomlinganiso wayo. Sibuye nayo ke siyiphethe.

<span id="an_43:22">43:22</span> Nenye imali sihle seza nayo esandleni
sethu, ukuba sithenge ukudla; asimazi oyifakileyo imali ezingxoweni
zethu.

<span id="an_43:23">43:23</span> Yathi, Xolani, musani ukoyika; uThixo
wenu, uThixo kayihlo, uninikile ubutyebi ezingxoweni zenu; imali yenu
ndayamkela. Yabakhuphela uSimon.

<span id="an_43:24">43:24</span> Indoda leyo yawangenisa amadoda
endlwini kaYosefu, yawanika amanzi, ahlamba iinyawo zawo; yawapha
iindiza amaesile awo.

<span id="an_43:25">43:25</span> Umnikelo lowo awulungisela ukufika
kukaYosefu emini enkulu; kuba ebeve kusithiwa aya kudla isonka khona.

<span id="an_43:26">43:26</span> Wangena uYosefu endlwini; amzisela
endlwini umnikelo obusesandleni sawo, aqubuda kuye emhlabeni.

<span id="an_43:27">43:27</span> Wawabuza ukuphila kwawo, wathi, Uyihlo
usaphilile na, ixhego enanithethe ngalo? Usadla ubomi na?

<span id="an_43:28">43:28</span> Athi, Usaphilile ubawo umkhonzi wakho,
usadla ubomi. Bathoba baqubuda.

<span id="an_43:29">43:29</span> Wawaphakamisa amehlo akhe, wambona
uBhenjamin umninawa wakhe, umntwana kanina, wathi, Nguye na lo umninawa
wenu omncinane, enibe nithetha ngaye kum? Wathi, Ngamana uThixo
wakubabala, nyana wam.

<span id="an_43:30">43:30</span> Wakhawuleza uYosefu; kuba wasikwa
yimfesane ngenxa yomninawa wakhe, wafuna indawo angalilela kuyo, wangena
engontsini, walila khona.

<span id="an_43:31">43:31</span> Waza wahlamba ubuso bakhe, waphuma
ezibambile, wathi, Bekani isonka.

<span id="an_43:32">43:32</span> Bambekela yedwa, bababekela bodwa bona,
bawabekela odwa amaYiputa abesidla naye; kuba amaYiputa akanakudla sonka
namaHebhere; kuba lisikizi elo kumaYiputa.

<span id="an_43:33">43:33</span> Bhalala phantsi phambi kwakhe,
owamazibulo ngokobuzibulo bakhe, omncinane ngokobuncinane bakhe. Amadoda
akhangelana ethe manga.

<span id="an_43:34">43:34</span> Aselwa izabelo ezisuka phambi kwakhe;
ke isabelo sikaBhenjamin saba sikhulu kahlanu kwizabelo zabo bonke
bephela. Basela, baba mnandi benaye.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> Wamwisela umthetho umphathi wendlu,
esithi, Zizalise iingxowa zala madoda ngokudla, njengoko zinako
ukukhongozela, uyibeke imali yalowo nalowo emlonyeni wengxowa yakhe;

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> uyibeke indebe yam, indebe yesilivere,
emlonyeni wengxowa yomncinane, nemali yengqolowa yakhe. Wenza ke
ngokwelizwi likaYosefu abelithethile.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> Kwakuthi qhiphu ukusa, andululwa loo
madoda, wona namaesile awo.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> Akubona ukuba aphumile emzini, engekayi
kude, wathi uYosefu kumphathi wendlu yakhe, Suka, uwasukele laa madoda;
wakuwafumana uze uthi kuwo, Yini na ukuba niphindezele okulungileyo
ngokubi?

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Le nto asiyile na inkosi yam isela ngayo,
ihlabe nezihlabo ngayo? Yinto embi le nto niyenzileyo.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Wawafumana, wathetha kuwo loo mazwi.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Athi kuye, Yini na ukuba inkosi yam
ithethe ngokwaloo mazwi? Makube lee kubakhonzi bakho ukwenza ngokwelo
lizwi.

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> Uyabona, imali esayifumanayo emlonyeni
weengxowa zethu, sayibuyisela kuwe, sivela ezweni lakwaKanan. Singathini
na ke ukuba endlwini yenkosi yakho isilivere nokuba yigolide?

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> Osukuba ifunyenwe kuye phakathi
kwabakhonzi bakhe, makafe; kananjalo thina sibe ngamakhoboka enkosini
yam.

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Wathi, Makube njengokwamazwi enu; ke
ngoko osukuba ifunyenwe kuye, woba sisicaka sam, ke nina noba msulwa.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Bakhawuleza, bathula elowo ingxowa
yakhe, bayibeka emhlabeni, bavula elowo ingxowa yakhe.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> Wagquthagqutha, eqalela komkhulu,
egqibela komncinane; yafunyanwa indebe engxoweni kaBhenjamin.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> Bazikrazula iingubo zabo, babopha elowo
iesile lakhe, babuyela kuloo mzi.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> Wafika uYuda nabazalwana bakhe endlwini
kaYosefu; ubesekhona yena. Bawa phambi kwakhe emhlabeni.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> UYosefu wathi kubo, Sisenzo sini na esi
nisenzileyo? Beningazi na ukuba indoda enjengam nje ibingahlaba
izihlabo?

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> UYuda wathi, Siya kuthini na enkosini
yam? Siya kuthetha ntoni na? Siya kuzihlamba njani na? UThixo ubufumene
ubugwenxa babakhonzi bakho; yabona, singabakhonzi benkosi yam, thina
aba, nalowa indebe ifunyenwe esandleni sakhe.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Wathi, Makube lee kum ukwenza loo nto;
indoda efunyenwe esandleni sayo indebe, yiyo eya kuba sisicaka kum; ke
nina nyukani nixolile, niye kuyihlo.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> UYuda wasondela kuye, wathi, Tarhu,
nkosi yam! Makhe athethe ilizwi umkhonzi wakho ezindlebeni zinkosi yam;
mawungavuthi umsindo wakho ngakumkhonzi wakho, ngokuba ungangoFaro wena.

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> Yababuza inkosi yam abakhonzi bayo,
isithi, Ninoyihlo na? Ninomninawa na?

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Sathi thina enkosini yam, Sinobawo
ixhego, nomntwana wobuxhego bakhe omncinane; umkhuluwa wakhe wafa, yena
usele yedwa kunina, uyise uyamthanda.

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> Wathi ke wena kubakhonzi bakho, Yihlani
naye eze kum, ndiwamise amehlo am kuye.

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> Sathi thina kwinkosi yam, Umfana lowo
akanako ukumshiya uyise; emshiyile, uyise angafa.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> Wathi wena kubakhonzi bakho, Ukuba
umninawa wenu omncinane akathanga ehle nani, aniyi kubuya nibubone ubuso
bam.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> Kwathi, xenikweni senyukayo saya
kumkhonzi wakho ongubawo, samxelela amazwi enkosi yam.

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> Wathi ubawo, Buyani niye kusithengela
intwana yokudla.

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> Sathi, Asinakuhla. Ukuba umninawa wethu
omncinane unathi, sohla; kuba asinakububona ubuso bendoda leyo,
engenathi umninawa wethu omncinane.

<span id="an_44:27">44:27</span> Wathi ubawo umkhonzi wakho kuthi,
Niyazi nina, ukuba umkam wandizalela oonyana ababini.

<span id="an_44:28">44:28</span> Omnye waphuma kum, ndathi, Inene,
uqwengiwe; andimbonanga unangoku.

<span id="an_44:29">44:29</span> Nimthabatha nje nalo ebusweni bam, ethe
wahlelwa yingozi, nozihlisela izimvi zam zinobubi kwelabafileyo.

<span id="an_44:30">44:30</span> Ngoko ke, ukuba ndithe ndafike kubawo
umkhonzi wakho, engenathi umfana (umphefumlo wakhe ubotshwe nomphefumlo
wakhe nje),

<span id="an_44:31">44:31</span> kothi, akubona ukuba akakho umfana,
afe, nabakhonzi bakho bahlise izimvi zomkhonzi wakho ubawo enesingqala,
ziye kwelabafileyo.

<span id="an_44:32">44:32</span> Kuba umkhonzi wakho lo wammela umfana
lowo kubawo, ndisithi, Ukuba andithanga ndimzise kuwe, ndoba netyala
kubawo yonke imihla yam.

<span id="an_44:33">44:33</span> Ngoko makahlale umkhonzi wakho lo
esikhundleni somfana, ndibe likhoboka enkosini yam mna; umfana anyuke
nabakhuluwa bakhe.

<span id="an_44:34">44:34</span> Kuba ndingathini na ukunyuka ndiye
kubawo, engenam umfana? hleze ndibubone ububi obomfumana ubawo.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> UYosefu akabanga nakuzibamba phambi kwabo
bonke ababemi ngakuye. Wadanduluka wathi, Khuphani bonke abantu, bemke
kum. Akwabakho mntu umi ngakuye ekuzaziseni kukaYosefu kubazalwana
bakhe.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Wasibeka isililo; eva amaYiputa, yeva
nendlu kaFaro.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Wathi uYosefu kubazalwana bakhe,
NdinguYosefu; usaphilile na ubawo? Ababa nako ukumphendula abazalwana
bakhe; kuba bakhwankqiswa phambi kwakhe.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Wathi, uYosefu kubazalwana bakhe,
Khanisondele kum apha. Basondela. Wathi, NdinguYosefu, umzalwana wenu,
enathengisayo ngaye eYiputa.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> Ngoko musani ukuba buhlungu,
ningaziqumbeli, ukuba nathengisa ngam apha; kuba uThixo wandithuma
phambi kwenu ukuze ndisindise abantu.

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> Kuba ngoku iminyaka mibini indlala ikho
phakathi kwelizwe; isemihlanu iminyaka ezayo, ekungayi kubakho kulima
nakuvuna ngayo.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> UThixo undithume phambi kwenu, ukuba
ndinimisele amasalela ezweni, ukuba ndisindise ubomi benu, ibe kukusinda
okukhulu.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> Ngoko ke asinini abandithume apha,
nguThixo; wandenza uyise kuFaro, nenkosi phezu kwayo yonke indlu yakhe,
nomlawuli ezweni lonke laseYiputa.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Khawulezani, ninyuke niye kubawo, nithi
kuye, Utsho unyana wakho uYosefu ukuthi, UThixo undenze inkosi kuyo
yonke iYiputa; yihla uze kum, musa ukulibala.

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> Wohlala ezweni laseGoshen, ube kufuphi
kum, wena, noonyana bakho, noonyana boonyana bakho, nempahla yakho
emfutshane, neenkomo zakho, nezinto zonke onazo;

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> ndikondle khona, kuba isaya kuba
mihlanu iminyaka yendlala; hleze uhlwempuzeke wena, nendlu yakho, nento
yonke onayo.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> Yabonani, amehlo enu ayabona, namehlo
omninawa wam uBhenjamin, ukuba ngumlomo wam lo uthethayo kuni.

<span id="an_45:13">45:13</span> Nize nimxelele ubawo lonke uzuko lwam
eYiputa, nezinto zonke enizibonileyo, nikhawuleze nihle nobawo, eze
apha.

<span id="an_45:14">45:14</span> Wawa entanyeni kaBhenjamin, umninawa
wakhe, walila; uBhenjamin walila entanyeni yakhe.

<span id="an_45:15">45:15</span> Wabanga bonke abazalwana bakhe, walila
phezu kwabo. Emveni koko, abazalwana bakhe bathetha naye.

<span id="an_45:16">45:16</span> Lavakala izwi endlwini kaFaro, lisithi,
Bafikele abazalwana bakaYosefu. Kwalunga oko emehlweni kaFaro,
nasemehlweni abakhonzi bakhe.

<span id="an_45:17">45:17</span> Wathi uFaro kuYosefu, Yithi kubazalwana
bakho, Yenzani oku: bophani amaqegu enu, nihambe niye ezweni lakwaKanan,

<span id="an_45:18">45:18</span> nithabathe uyihlo nezindlu zenu, nise
kum apha. Ndoninika izinto ezilungileyo zelizwe laseYiputa, nidle
ukutyeba kwelizwe.

<span id="an_45:19">45:19</span> Wena ke uwiselwe umthetho, yenzani oku;
bathabatheleni abantwana benu, nabafazi benu, iinqwelo ezweni
laseYiputa, nithwale uyihlo, nize.

<span id="an_45:20">45:20</span> Iliso lenu malingabi nanceba empahleni
yenu, kuba zonke izinto ezilungileyo zelizwe lonke laseYiputa zezenu.

<span id="an_45:21">45:21</span> Benjenjalo ke oonyana bakaSirayeli.
UYosefu wabanika iinqwelo ngokomthetho kaFaro; wabanika nomphako
wendlela.

<span id="an_45:22">45:22</span> Wabanika bonke elowo iingubo
zokukhululana. Wamnika uBhenjamin iisilivere ezimakhulu mathathu,
neengubo ezintlanu zokukhululana.

<span id="an_45:23">45:23</span> Kuyise wathumela ezilolu hlobo:
amaesile alishumi, ethwele izinto ezilungileyo zaseYiputa, neemazi
zamaesile ezilishumi, zithwele ingqolowa, nesonka, nomphako kayise
wendlela.

<span id="an_45:24">45:24</span> Wabandulula ke abazalwana bakhe,
bahamba; wathi kubo, Ize ningaxabani endleleni.

<span id="an_45:25">45:25</span> Benyuka, bemke ke eYiputa, bafika
ezweni lakwaKanan kuYakobi uyise.

<span id="an_45:26">45:26</span> Bamxelela besithi, UYosefu usahleli;
ewe, ungumphathi welizwe lonke laseYiputa. Yaqoba intliziyo yakhe, kuba
ebengakholwa ngabo.

<span id="an_45:27">45:27</span> Bawathetha kuye onke amazwi kaYosefu,
abewathethile kubo. Wazibona iinqwelo abezithumele uYosefu, ukuba
zimthwale; waza waphila umoya kaYakobi uyise.

<span id="an_45:28">45:28</span> Wathi uSirayeli, Kwanele. UYosefu
unyana wam usahleli. Ndiya kuya ndimbone, ndingekafi.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> Wanduluka ke uSirayeli neento zonke
abenazo, wafika eBher-shebha, wabingelela imibingelelo kuThixo kayise
uIsake.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> Wathetha uThixo kuSirayeli emibonweni
yobusuku, wathi, Yakobi, Yakobi! Wathi yena, Ndilapha.

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Wathi, NdinguThixo, uThixo wooyihlo, musa
ukoyika ukuhla uye eYiputa; kuba ndiya kukwenza uhlanga olukhulu khona.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> Mna ndiya kuhla ndiye nawe eYiputa,
ndinyuke nokunyuka nawe; uYosefu asibeke isandla sakhe phezu kwamehlo
akho.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> Wesuka uYakobi eBher-shebha; oonyana
bakaSirayeli bamthwala uYakobi uyise, nabantwana babo, nabafazi babo,
ngeenqwelo ebezithunyelwe nguFaro ukuba zimthwale.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> Bayithabatha imfuyo yabo, nengqwebo yabo
ababeyiqwebile ezweni lakwaKanan, bafika eYiputa uYakobi nembewu yakhe
yonke, ndawonye naye;

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> oonyana bakhe, noonyana boonyana bakhe
ndawonye naye, iintombi zakhe, neentombi zoonyana bakhe, nembewu yakhe
yonke, weza nayo eYiputa.

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> Ngawo la amagama oonyana bakaSirayeli
abafikayo eYiputa, uYakobi noonyana bakhe: amazibulo kaYakobi nguRubhen.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> Oonyana bakaRubhen nguHanoki, noFalu,
noHetseron, noKarmi.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> Oonyana bakaSimon, nguYemuweli,
noYamin, no-Ohadi, noYakin, noTsohare, noSawule, unyana womKananekazi.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> Oonyana bakaLevi nguGershon, noKehati,
noMerari.

<span id="an_46:12">46:12</span> Oonyana bakaYuda nguEre, no-Onan,
noShela, noPeretse, noZera; ke ooEre no-Onan bafela ezweni lakwaKanan.
Oonyana bakaPeretse nguHetseron noHamuli.

<span id="an_46:13">46:13</span> Oonyana bakaIsakare nguTola, noPuwa,
noYobhi, noShimron.

<span id="an_46:14">46:14</span> Oonyana bakaZebhulon nguZerede,
noEloni, noYaleli.

<span id="an_46:15">46:15</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaLeya, awabazalela
uYakobi ePadan-aram, noDina intombi yakhe; yonke imiphefumlo yoonyana
bakhe neyeentombi zakhe ingamashumi omathathu anamithathu.

<span id="an_46:16">46:16</span> Oonyana bakaGadi nguTsifiyon, noHagi,
noShuni, noEtsebhon, noEri, noArodi, noAreli.

<span id="an_46:17">46:17</span> Oonyana baka-Ashere nguImna, noIshwa,
noIshvi, noBheriya, noSera udade wabo; oonyana bakaBheriya nguEbhere
noMalekiyeli.

<span id="an_46:18">46:18</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaZilipa, awathi
uLabhan wamnika uLeya intombi yakhe; abo wabazalela uYakobi, imiphefumlo
elishumi elinamithandathu.

<span id="an_46:19">46:19</span> Oonyana bakaRakeli, umkaYakobi,
nguYosefu noBhenjamin.

<span id="an_46:20">46:20</span> Wazala ke uYosefu ezweni laseYiputa,
uManase, noEfrayim, awamzalela bona uAzenati, intombi kaPotifera,
umbingeleli waseOn.

<span id="an_46:21">46:21</span> Oonyana bakaBhenjamin nguBhela,
noBhekere, noAshbhele, noGera, noNahaman, noEhi, noRoshe, noMupim,
noHupim, noArdi.

<span id="an_46:22">46:22</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaRakeli,
abazalelwa uYakobi; iyonke yimiphefumlo elishumi elinamine.

<span id="an_46:23">46:23</span> Oonyana bakaDan nguHushim.

<span id="an_46:24">46:24</span> Oonyana bakaNafetali nguYatseli,
noGuni, noYetsere, noShilem.

<span id="an_46:25">46:25</span> Ngabo abo oonyana bakaBhiliha, awathi
uLabhan wamnika uRakeli intombi yakhe; abo wabazalela uYakobi, iyonke
yimiphefumlo esixhenxe.

<span id="an_46:26">46:26</span> Iyonke imiphefumlo eyaya noYakobi
eYiputa, eyaphuma esinqeni sakhe, ngaphandle kwabafazi boonyana
bakaYakobi, iyonke yimiphefumlo emashumi mathandathu anamithandathu.

<span id="an_46:27">46:27</span> Oonyana bakaYosefu awabazalelwa eYiputa
yimiphefumlo emibini. Iyonke imiphefumlo yendlu kaYakobi eyaya eYiputa
ibimashumi asixhenxe.

<span id="an_46:28">46:28</span> Wasusa uYuda ukuba amandulele aye
kuYosefu, ambonise indlela eya eGoshen; bafika ke ezweni laseGoshen.

<span id="an_46:29">46:29</span> UYosefu wayibopha inqwelo yakhe,
wenyuka waya kumkhawulela uSirayeli uyise eGoshen. Bathe bakubonana,
wawa entanyeni yakhe, walila umzuzu omkhulu entanyeni yakhe.

<span id="an_46:30">46:30</span> Wathi uSirayeli kuYosefu, Ndibubonile
nje ubuso bakho, ukuba usahleli, mandife ngoku.

<span id="an_46:31">46:31</span> Wathi uYosefu kubazalwana bakhe
nakwindlu kayise, Ndiya kunyuka ndiye kubika kuFaro, ndithi kuye,
Abazalwana bam nendlu kabawo, ababesezweni lakwaKanan, bafikile;

<span id="an_46:32">46:32</span> kunjalo nje la madoda ngabalusi
bempahla emfutshane, kuba ngabafuyi; impahla yawo emfutshane, neenkomo
zawo, neento zonke ananzo, aze nazo.

<span id="an_46:33">46:33</span> Xa athe wanibiza uFaro, wathi, Uyintoni
na umsebenzi wenu? nothi,

<span id="an_46:34">46:34</span> Abakhonzi bakho ngabafuyi bempahla
kwasebuncinaneni bethu unangoku, thina aba noobawo bethu; ukuze nime
ezweni laseGoshen, kuba bonke abalusi bempahla emfutshane balisikizi
kumaYiputa.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> UYosefu waya kumbikela uFaro, wathi,
Ufikile ubawo nabazalwana bam, nempahla yabo emfutshane, neenkomo zabo,
neento zonke abanazo, bevela ezweni lakwaKanan; nabo besezweni
laseGoshen.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> Wakhetha kubo abazalwana bakhe amadoda
amahlanu, wawamisa phambi koFaro.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Wathi uFaro kubazalwana bakhe, Uyintoni
na umsebenzi wenu? Bathi kuFaro, Abakhonzi bakho ngabafuyi bempahla
emfutshane, thina aba kwanoobawo bethu.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> Babuya bathi kuFaro, Siphambukele kweli
lizwe, kuba akukho tyani bampahla imfutshane abanayo abakhonzi bakho,
kuba inzima indlala ezweni lakwaKanan; ngoko ke mabakhe bahlale ezweni
laseGoshen abakhonzi bakho.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> Wathetha uFaro kuYosefu, wathi, Uyihlo
nabazalwana bakho bafikile kuwe.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> Ilizwe laseYiputa liphambi kwakho: uyihlo
nabazalwana bakho bahlalise kweyona ndawo intle yelizwe; mabahlale
ezweni laseGoshen. Ukuba uyazi ukuba kukho kuwo amadoda aziinkunkqele
emsebenzini, wamise abe ngabaphathi bemfuyo endinayo.

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> UYosefu wamngenisa uYakobi uyise, wammisa
phambi koFaro. UYakobi wamsikelela uFaro.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> UFaro wathi kuYakobi, Mingaphi na
iminyaka yobudala bakho?

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> Wathi uYakobi kuFaro, Imihla yeminyaka
yokuba lundwendwe kwam emhlabeni yiminyaka elikhulu elinamanci mathathu;
imbalwa, imibi, imihla yeminyaka yobudala bam; ayifikanga emihleni
yeminyaka yobudala boobawo, emihleni yokuba lundwendwe kwabo emhlabeni.

<span id="an_47:10">47:10</span> UYakobi wamsikela ke uFaro; waphuma,
wemka ebusweni bukaFaro.

<span id="an_47:11">47:11</span> UYosefu wambeka uyise nabazalwana bakhe
ezweni laseYiputa, wabanika indawo yokuma kweyona ndawo intle yelizwe,
ezweni laseRameses, ngokomthetho kaFaro.

<span id="an_47:12">47:12</span> UYosefu wamondla uyise, nabazalwana
bakhe, nendlu yonke kayise, ngesonka, ngangokuswela kosapho lwabo.

<span id="an_47:13">47:13</span> Bekungekho kudla kulo lonke ilizwe;
kuba ibinzima kunene indlala; ilizwe laseYiputa nelizwe lakwaKanan
laphelelwa ngamandla ngenxa yendlala.

<span id="an_47:14">47:14</span> Wayihlanganisa uYosefu yonke imali
eyafunyanwayo ezweni laseYiputa nasezweni lakwaKanan, yengqolowa
ababeyithenga; wayingenisa uYosefu imali endlwini kaFaro.

<span id="an_47:15">47:15</span> Yaphela imali ezweni laseYiputa
nasezweni lakwaKanan. Onke amaYiputa eza kuYosefu, esithi, Sinike
ukudla. Yini na ukuba sife phambi kwakho, kuba imali iphelile.

<span id="an_47:16">47:16</span> Wathi uYosefu, Rholani imfuyo yenu;
ndoninika ngemfuyo yenu, ukuba imali iphelile.

<span id="an_47:17">47:17</span> Ayizisa imfuyo yawo kuYosefu; uYosefu
wawanika ukudla ngamahashe, nangemfuyo eyimpahla emfutshane, nangemfuyo
eziinkomo, nangamaesile; wawapha ukudla endaweni yayo yonke imfuyo yawo
ngaloo mnyaka.

<span id="an_47:18">47:18</span> Waphela ke loo mnyaka. Eza kuye
ngomnyaka wesibini, athi kuye, Asinakukufihla enkosini yam, ukuba imali
nemfuyo eziinkomo iphelele enkosini yam; akusalanga nto kuthi phambi
kwenkosi yam, yimizimba yethu nimihlaba yethu yodwa kuphela.

<span id="an_47:19">47:19</span> Yini na ukuba sife phambi kwakho, thina
aba nomhlaba wethu. Sithenge thina nomhlaba wethu ngokudla, ukuze thina
nomhlaba wethu sibe ngabakhonzi bakaFaro. Sinike imbewu, ukuze siphile,
singafi, kube senkangala.

<span id="an_47:20">47:20</span> UYosefu wawuthengela uFaro wonke
umhlaba waseYiputa; kuba amaYiputa athengisa elowo ngentsimi yakhe, kuba
indlala yabe inzima phezu kwawo; umhlaba ke waba ngokaFaro.

<span id="an_47:21">47:21</span> Abantu wabafudusela emizini,
kwathabathela ekupheleni komnye umda waseYiputa kwesa ekupheleni komnye.

<span id="an_47:22">47:22</span> Ngumhlaba wababingeleli wodwa
angawuthenganga; kuba ababingeleli babenesabelo abasimiselweyo esivela
kuFaro, besidla isabelo eso simiselweyo, babesinikwe nguFaro; ngenxa
yoko bona abathengisanga ngomhlaba wabo.

<span id="an_47:23">47:23</span> Wathi uYosefu ebantwini, Yabonani,
namhla nina nomhlaba wenu ndinithengele uFaro; nantsi ke imbewu yenu,
hlwayelani umhlaba.

<span id="an_47:24">47:24</span> Nothi kwinto eniyizuzileyo, nimnike
uFaro esesihlanu isahlulo, ezine izahlulo zibe zezenu, zibe yimbewu
yentsimi, nezokudliwa nini nangabasezindlwini zenu, nezokudliwa lusapho
lwenu.

<span id="an_47:25">47:25</span> Bathi, Usisindisile; mayisibabale
inkosi yam, soba ngabakhonzi kuFaro.

<span id="an_47:26">47:26</span> UYosefu wayimisa loo nto yaba
ngummiselo unanamhla phezu komhlaba waseYiputa, ukuba esesihlanu
isahlulo sibe sesikaFaro; ngumhlaba wababingeleli wodwa ongabanga
ngokaFaro.

<span id="an_47:27">47:27</span> Wahlala uSirayeli ezweni laseYiputa,
ezweni laseGoshen; baqiniseka ukuma khona, baqhama, banda kunene.

<span id="an_47:28">47:28</span> UYakobi wadla ubomi ezweni laseYiputa
iminyaka elishumi elinesixhenxe; imihla kaYakobi, iminyaka yobudala
bakhe, yaba yiminyaka elikhulu elinamanci amane, aneminyaka esixhenxe.

<span id="an_47:29">47:29</span> Yasondela imihla kaSirayeli yokuba afe;
wabiza unyana wakhe uYosefu, wathi kuye, Ukuba kaloku ndibabalwe nguwe,
khawubeke isandla sakho phantsi kwethanga lam, undenzele inceba
nenyaniso. Uze ungakhe undingcwabe eYiputa.

<span id="an_47:30">47:30</span> Ke ndiya kulala koobawo; uze undisuse
eYiputa, undingcwabe engcwabeni labo. Wathi ke yena, Ndiya kwenza
ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_47:31">47:31</span> Wathi, Funga; wafunga ke. Waqubuda
uSirayeli phezu kwentloko yesingqengqelo.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> Kwathi emveni kwezi zinto, kwathiwa
kuYosefu, Uyabona, uyihlo uyafa. Wathabatha oonyana bakhe bobabini,
uManase noEfrayim, bahamba naye.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Waxelelwa uYakobi kwathiwa, Nanku unyana
wakho uYosefu esiza kuwe. Wazomeleza uSirayeli, wavuka, wahlala
esingqengqelweni.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> UYakobi wathi uYosefu, uThixo uSomandla
wabonakala kum ndiseLuzi, ezweni lakwaKanan, wandisikelela.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> Wathi kum, Yabona, ndiya kukuqhamisa,
ndikwandise, ndikwenze isikhungu sezizwe; eli lizwe ndilinike imbewu
yakho emva kwakho, libe lelakho ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> Ngako oko oonyana bakho ababini,
owabazalelwayo ezweni laseYiputa, ndingekafiki kuwe eYiputa, ngabam;
uEfrayim noManase baya kuba ngabam; njengoRubhen noSimon.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Ke othe wabazala emva kwabo, baya kuba
ngabakho; baya kubizwa ngokwegama labazalwana babo elifeni labo.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> Ekumkeni kwam mna ePadan, ndafelwa
nguRakeli ezweni lakwaKanan endleleni, ndakubona ukuba ndimganyana ukuze
kufikwe e-Efrata; ndamngcwabela khona endleleni yase-Efrata
eyiBhetelehem.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> USirayeli wababona oonyana bakaYosefu,
wathi, Ngoobani na aba?

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> Wathi uYosefu kuyise, Ngoonyana bam
endibaphiwe nguThixo apha. Wathi yena, Khawubasondeze kum,
ndibasikelele.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> Ke amehlo kaSirayeli ayeselenorhatyazo
kukwaluphala, engasaboni. Wabasondeza ke kuye, wabanga, wabawola.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> USirayeli wathi uYosefu, Ukubona ubuso
bakho bendingasakucingi; nanku uThixo endibonise nembewu yakho.

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> UYosefu wabakhupha phakathi kwamadolo
akhe, waqubuda ngobuso bakhe emhlabeni.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> UYosefu wabathabatha bobabini, uEfrayim
ngesokunene kwesasekhohlo sikaSirayeli, noManase ngesokhohlo kwesokunene
sikaSirayeli, wabasondeza kuye.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> USirayeli wasolula esokunene sakhe,
wasibeka entloko kuEfrayim engomncinane, nesokhohlo sakhe entloko
kuManase, ezenjenjalo izandla zakhe ngengqiqo; ngokuba uManase
ebengowamazibulo.

<span id="an_48:15">48:15</span> Wamsikelela uYosefu, wathi, Ngamana
uThixo, abahamba phambi kwakhe oobawo uAbraham noIsake, owandondla
kwasekuveleni kwam kwada kwanamhla, osisithunywa esindikhululeyo ebubini
bonke,

<span id="an_48:16">48:16</span> angabasikelela abafana, lithi igama lam
negama loobawo libizwe phezu kwabo, uAbraham noIsake, bande, babe
baninzi ehlabathini.

<span id="an_48:17">48:17</span> Wabona uYosefu ukuba uyise usibeke
isandla sakhe sokunene entloko kuEfrayim, kwakubi emehlweni akhe;
wasibamba isandla sikayise wasishenxisa entlokweni kaEfrayim, esisa
entlokweni kaManase.

<span id="an_48:18">48:18</span> Wathi uYosefu kuyise, Makungabi njalo,
bawo, kuba ngulo owamazibulo; beka esokunene entlokweni yakhe.

<span id="an_48:19">48:19</span> Akavuma uyise, wathi, Ndiyazi, nyana
wam, ndiyazi; naye uya kuba sisizwe, naye uya kuba mkhulu; kodwa
umninawa wakhe uya kuba mkhulu kuye, nembewu yakhe ibe ziintlanga
ezininzi.

<span id="an_48:20">48:20</span> Wabasikelela ngaloo mini, esithi, Ngawe
uya kusikelela uSirayeli, esithi, Ngamana uThixo wakwenza njengoEfrayim
nanjengoManase. Wambeka ke uEfrayim phambi koManase.

<span id="an_48:21">48:21</span> USirayeli wathi kuYosefu, Yabona, ndiza
kufa; uThixo uya kuba nani, anibuyisele ezweni looyihlo.

<span id="an_48:22">48:22</span> Mna ndikunike isiqwenga somhlaba
ngaphezu kwabazalwana bakho, eso ndasithimbayo esandleni sama-Amori,
ngekrele lam nangesaphetha sam.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> Wababiza ke uYakobi oonyana bakhe, wathi,
Zihlanganiseni, ndinixelele okuya kunihlela ngemihla yokugqibela.

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> Qukanani, niphulaphule, nyana bakaYakobi,
Niphulaphule uSirayeli uyihlo.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> Rubhen, wena mazibulo am, mandla am,
ngqalo yokuqina kwam, Ncamisa yokuphakama, ncamisa yegunya,

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> Uxhaphazelayo njengamanzi, akusayi kuba
ncamisa kunje; Kuba wenyukayo waya esililini sikayihlo, Wangcolisa oko,
wenyuka waya emandlalweni wam.

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> USimon noLevi ngabazalwana; Ziintonga
zokugonyamela izikhali zabo.

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> Egquguleni labo uze ungangeni umphefumlo
wam, Nesikhungu sabo lungazibandakanyi uzuko lwam; Kuba ngomsindo wabo
babulala amadoda, Ngokuzithandela kwabo bazinqumla imisipha iinkomo.

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> Uqalekisiwe umsindo wabo, ngokuba
unobungcwangu: Ukuphuphuma kwabo umsindo, ngokuba unzima. Ndiya
kubachithachitha kwaYakobi, Ndibaphangalalise kwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> Yuda, abazalwana bakho baya kukudumisa,
Isandla sakho sibe sentanyeni yeentshaba zakho; Baya kuqubuda kuwe
oonyana bakayihlo.

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> Lithole lengonyama uYuda; Usuke
ekuqwengeni, nyana wam, Waguqa, wabuthuma njengengonyama,
Njengengonyamakazi; ngubani na oya kumvusa?

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> Intonga ayiyi kumka kuYuda, Intonga
yommisi-mthetho ayiyi kumka phakathi kweenyawo zakhe, Ade afike uShilo,
Zimlulamele izizwe.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> Ngukhuleka emdiliyeni imazi yakhe
ye-esile, Ukhuleka kowohlobo inkonyana yakhe ye-esile; uhlamba ngewayini
isambatho sakhe, Ngegazi lediliya ingubo yakhe;

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> Umehlo abomvu yiwayini, Umazinyo
amhlophe ngamasi.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> UZebhulon uya kuma ngasezibukweni
lolwandle,

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Ewe, ngasezibukweni leenqanawa, Icala
lakhe lisingise eTsidon. UIsakare yinyathi ye-esile, Ulala phakathi
kweentlanti.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> Wakubona ukuphumla ukuba kulungile,
Nelizwe ukuba limnandi; Igxalaba lakhe walithobela ukuthwala, waba
ngumsebenzi ofakwa uviko.

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> UDan uya kugweba phakathi kwabantu
bakowabo, Njengezinye izizwe zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> UDan makabe yinyoka ngasendleleni,
Irhamba ngasemendweni, Eliluma izithende zehashe, Awe ngomva
olikhweleyo.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> Usindiso lwakho, Yehova, ndiluthembile.

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> UGadi ungenelwa ngamatutu, Ke yena
uwangenela ezithendeni.

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> KuAshere kuphuma amafutha, isonka sakhe
eso; Yena unika izinto eziyolisa ookumkani.

<span id="an_49:21">49:21</span> UNafetali yimazi yexhama ekhululweyo,
ukhupha amazwi amahle.

<span id="an_49:22">49:22</span> NguGatya lomthi oqhamayo uYosefu,
UGatya lomthi oqhamayo ngasemthonjeni, Omasebe aqabele eludongeni.

<span id="an_49:23">49:23</span> UBamcubunga bamtola, Bamchasa abatoli;

<span id="an_49:24">49:24</span> USihlala sithe nkqi isaphetha sakhe,
UMikhono yezandla zakhe inokusityeda, Ngezandla zembalasane kaYakobi,
Khona apho akhoyo umalusi, ilitye likaSirayeli;

<span id="an_49:25">49:25</span> NgoThixo wooyihlo—akuncede,
NgoSomandla—akusikelele, Ibe ziintsikelelo zamazulu ezivela phezulu,
Iintsikelelo zamanzi enzonzobila alele ezantsi, Iintsikelelo zamabele,
nezesizalo.

<span id="an_49:26">49:26</span> Iintsikelelo zikayihlo Zizigqithile
iintsikelelo zomawokhulu, Zasa nasemdeni weentaba zanini; Mazibe
sentloko kuYosefu, Ebuchotsheni bobalulweyo kubazalwana bakhe!

<span id="an_49:27">49:27</span> UBhenjamin yingcuka eqwengayo; Kusasa
uya kudla okuphangiweyo, Ngokuhlwa uya kwaba okuthinjiweyo.

<span id="an_49:28">49:28</span> Bonke aba zizizwe zakwaSirayeli
ezilishumi elinazibini; yiyo leyo into awayithethayo kubo uyise,
wabasikelela; elowo ngokwentsikelelo yakhe wabasikelela.

<span id="an_49:29">49:29</span> Wabawisela umthetho, wathi kubo, Ndiza
kuhlanganiselwa kwabakowethu; ndingcwabeni noobawo emqolombeni
osentsimini kaEfron umHiti,

<span id="an_49:30">49:30</span> emqolombeni osentsimini yaseMakapela,
ophambi kowakwaMamre, ezweni lakwaKanan, awawuthengayo uAbraham ndawonye
nentsimi kuEfron umHiti, ukuba abe nendawo eyiyeyakhe yokungcwaba.

<span id="an_49:31">49:31</span> Bamngcwaba khona apho uAbraham noSara
umkakhe; bamngcwaba khona apho uIsake noRebheka umkakhe; ndamngcwaba
khona apho uLeya.

<span id="an_49:32">49:32</span> Yathengwa intsimi leyo nomqolomba okuyo
koonyana bakaHeti.

<span id="an_49:33">49:33</span> Wagqiba ke uYakobi ukuyolela oonyana
bakhe, wazifinyezela esingqengqelweni iinyawo zakhe, waphuma umphefumlo,
wahlanganiselwa kwabakowabo.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> Wawa uYosefu phezu kobuso bukayise,
walila phezu kwakhe, wamanga.

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> UYosefu wabawisela umthetho abakhonzi
bakhe, amagqirha, ukuba amqhole uyise; amagqirha amqhola ke uSirayeli.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> Bamzalisela imihla emashumi mane, kuba
bebesenjenjalo ukuyizalisa imihla yabaqholiweyo; amaYiputa amlilela
imihla emashumi asixhenxe.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> Yadlula ke imihla yokulilelwa kwakhe,
uYosefu wathetha kwindlu kaFaro, wathi, Ukuba kaloku niyandibabala,
khanithethe ezindlebeni zikaFaro, nithi,

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> Ubawo wandifungisa esithi, Yabona, ndiza
kufa; engcwabeni lam endizimbeleyo ezweni lakwaKanan, wondingcwabela
khona apho. Ngoko makhe ndinyuke ndiye kumngcwaba ubawo; ndobuya
ndibuye.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> Wathi uFaro, Nyuka uye kumngcwaba uyihlo
ngoko akufungise ngako.

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> Wenyuka ke uYosefu waya kumngcwaba uyise;
benyuka naye bonke abakhonzi bakaFaro, amadoda amakhulu endlu yakhe,
amadoda amakhulu onke ezwe laseYiputa;

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> nendlu kaYosefu yonke, nabazalwana bakhe,
nendlu kayise. Kwasala iintsapho zabo zodwa, nempahla yabo emfutshane,
neenkomo zabo, ezweni laseGoshen.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> Kwenyuka naye iinqwelo, nabamahashe, yaba
ngumkhosi omkhulu kunene.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> Bafika esandeni sika-Atadi esiphesheya
kweYordan, bambambazela izifuba, batsho khona ngesililo esikhulu,
esinzima kunene; bamenzela uyise isijwili imihla esixhenxe.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> Basibona abemi belo zwe, amaKanan,
isijwili esandeni sika-Atadi, bathi, Sikhulu esi sijwili kumaYiputa;
ngenxa yoko kwathiwa igama laso yiAbhele-mitserayim, ephesheya
kweYordan.

<span id="an_50:12">50:12</span> Oonyana bakhe benza ke kuye
njengokuyolela kwakhe.

<span id="an_50:13">50:13</span> Bamthwala oonyana bakhe, bamsa ezweni
lakwaKanan, bamngcwaba emqolombeni wentsimi yaseMakapela, awawuthengayo
uAbraham ndawonye nentsimi, ukuba ube yindawo eyiyeyakhe yokungcwaba,
kuEfron umHiti phambi kowakwaMamre.

<span id="an_50:14">50:14</span> UYosefu wabuyela eYiputa ke, yena
nabazalwana bakhe, nabo bonke abenyuka naye beya kumngcwaba uyise, emva
kokungcwaba kwakhe uyise.

<span id="an_50:15">50:15</span> Ke kaloku abakhuluwa bakaYosefu babona
ukuba uyise wabo ufile, bathi, Azi uYosefu uya kusitshutshisa na,
abubuyisele kanye na kuthi bonke ububi esimenzele bona?

<span id="an_50:16">50:16</span> Bathumela kuYosefu, besithi, Uyihlo
wayolela phambi kokufa kwakhe, wathi,

<span id="an_50:17">50:17</span> Notsho kuYosefu ukuthi, Khawuluxolele
ukreqo lwabakhuluwa bakho, nesono sabo sokuba bekwenze into embi; ngoko
khawuluxolele ukreqo lwabakhozi boThixo wooyihlo. Walila uYosefu
ekuthetheni kwabo kuye.

<span id="an_50:18">50:18</span> Baya nabakhuluwa bakhe, baziphosa
phantsi phambi kwakhe, bathi, Yabona, singabakhonzi bakho.

<span id="an_50:19">50:19</span> Wathi uYosefu kubo, Musani ukoyika;
ndisesikhundleni sikaThixo yini na?

<span id="an_50:20">50:20</span> Nina nacinga ububi ngam; ke yena uThixo
wacinga okulungileyo, ukuze kuthi, njengoko kwenzekileyo namhla, kusinde
abantu abaninzi.

<span id="an_50:21">50:21</span> Ngoko musani ukoyika; ndonondla nina,
nentsapho yenu. Wabathuthuzela ke, wathetha kakuhle nabo.

<span id="an_50:22">50:22</span> UYosefu wena eYiputa, yena nendlu
kayise. UYosefu wahlala iminyaka elikhulu elinashumi-nye.

<span id="an_50:23">50:23</span> UYosefu wabona oonyana besesithathu
isizukulwana sikaEfrayim, kwanoonyana bakaMakire, unyana kaManase,
ababezalelwe emadolweni kaYosefu.

<span id="an_50:24">50:24</span> Wathi uYosefu kubakhuluwa bakhe, Ndiza
kufa; uThixo okunene uya kunivelela, aninyuse, niphume kweli lizwe, niye
ezweni abelifungele uAbraham, noIsake, noYakobi.

<span id="an_50:25">50:25</span> UYosefu wabafungisa oonyana
bakaSirayeli, esithi, UThixo okunene eya kunivelela nje, nowanyusa
amathambo am, emke apha.

<span id="an_50:26">50:26</span> Wafa ke uYosefu engominyaka ilikhulu
linashumi-nye; bamqhola; wafakwa etyeyeni eYiputa.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
